# Surah 29 — Al-Ankabut

**Status:** ✅ Publishable · Fidelity 95/100 · Prose overlap (4-gram) 0.092 · Longest prose run 17 words · Em dashes 0

_Translated by claude-sonnet-5 (opus-4.8 on flagged revisions); graded by gemini-3.1-pro-preview at 2026-07-07T11:16:12.721Z. Quality metrics are surah-level. Review each translation against the Arabic below, never against any other translation._

**Overlap spans to check:** "ibn abbas said how can you ask the people of the book about anything when your book"

**Examiner verdict:** The candidate translation is generally excellent and highly accurate, but contains one major mistranslation of a conditional clause.

---

## 29:1-4 — verses 1-4 (shared commentary)

### Translation

In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful

[It is] Meccan.

As for the discussion of the disjointed letters, it has already been presented at the beginning of Surat al-Baqarah.

Concerning His saying: {Do people think that they will be left to say, "We believe," and they will not be tried?}, this is an interrogative of denial (istifham inkar), and its meaning is that Allah, glorified and exalted is He, must inevitably try His believing servants according to the measure of faith they possess, as has come in the sound hadith: "The people most severely tried are the prophets, then the righteous, then those most excellent in rank after them. A man is tried according to his religion. If there is firmness in his religion, the trial is increased for him." This verse is like His saying: {Or did you think that you would enter Paradise while Allah has not yet made evident those among you who strive and made evident the steadfast?} [Al Imran: 142], and there is a similar verse in Surat Bara'ah (al-Tawbah). And He said in al-Baqarah: {Or do you think that you will enter Paradise while such [trial] has not yet come to you as came to those who passed on before you? They were touched by poverty and hardship and were shaken until [even their] messenger and those who believed with him said, "When is the help of Allah?" Unquestionably, the help of Allah is near} [al-Baqarah: 214]. Therefore He said here: {And We had certainly tried those before them, so Allah will surely make evident those who are truthful and He will surely make evident the liars}, meaning those who are truthful in their claim to faith, as distinguished from those who are liars in their word and their claim. Allah, glorified and exalted is He, knows what has been, what will be, and what has not been, how it would be if it were. This is a matter of consensus (ijma) among the imams of the Sunnah and the Jama'ah. It is for this reason that Ibn Abbas and others, regarding a similar phrase such as {except that We may know} [al-Baqarah: 143], say: except that We may see. This is because "seeing" pertains only to what exists, while "knowledge" is more general than "seeing," for it pertains both to what does not exist and to what does exist.

And His saying: {Or do those who commit evil deeds think that they can outrun Us? Evil is what they judge}, meaning: let not those who have not entered into faith think that they will escape this trial and testing, for behind them lies a punishment and a chastisement even harsher and more overwhelming than this. It is for this reason that He said: {Or do those who commit evil deeds think that they can outrun Us}, meaning, escape Us, {evil is what they judge}, meaning, evil indeed is what they suppose.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

بسم الله الرحمن الرحيم

[وهي] مكية.

* *

أَمَّا الْكَلَامُ عَلَى الْحُرُوفِ الْمُقَطَّعَةِ فَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي أَوَّلِ سُورَةِ "الْبَقَرَةِ".

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَحَسِبَ النَّاسُ أَنْ يُتْرَكُوا أَنْ يَقُولُوا آمَنَّا وَهُمْ لَا يُفْتَنُونَ﴾ اسْتِفْهَامُ إِنْكَارٍ، وَمَعْنَاهُ: أَنَّ اللَّهَ سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى لَا بُدَّ أَنْ يَبْتَلِيَ عِبَادَهُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ بِحَسْبِ مَا عِنْدَهُمْ مِنَ الْإِيمَانِ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ الصَّحِيحِ: "أَشَدُّ النَّاسِ بَلَاءً الْأَنْبِيَاءُ ثُمَّ الصَّالِحُونَ، ثُمَّ الْأَمْثَلُ فَالْأَمْثَلُ، يُبْتَلَى الرَّجُلُ عَلَى حَسَبِ دِينِهِ، فَإِنْ كَانَ فِي دِينِهِ صَلَابَةٌ زِيدَ فِي الْبَلَاءِ" . وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿أَمْ حَسِبْتُمْ أَنْ تَدْخُلُوا الْجَنَّةَ وَلَمَّا يَعْلَمِ اللَّهُ الَّذِينَ جَاهَدُوا مِنْكُمْ وَيَعْلَمَ الصَّابِرِينَ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ: ١٤٢] ، وَمِثْلُهَا فِي سُورَةِ "بَرَاءَةٌ" وَقَالَ فِي الْبَقَرَةِ: ﴿أَمْ حَسِبْتُمْ أَنْ تَدْخُلُوا الْجَنَّةَ وَلَمَّا يَأْتِكُمْ مَثَلُ الَّذِينَ خَلَوْا مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ مَسَّتْهُمُ الْبَأْسَاءُ وَالضَّرَّاءُ وَزُلْزِلُوا حَتَّى يَقُولَ الرَّسُولُ وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مَعَهُ مَتَى نَصْرُ اللَّهِ أَلا إِنَّ نَصْرَ اللَّهِ قَرِيبٌ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢١٤] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿وَلَقَدْ فَتَنَّا الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ فَلَيَعْلَمَنَّ اللَّهُ الَّذِينَ صَدَقُوا وَلَيَعْلَمَنَّ الْكَاذِبِينَ﴾ أَيِ: الَّذِينَ صَدَقُوا فِي دَعْوَاهُمُ الْإِيمَانَ مِمَّنْ هُوَ كَاذِبٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ وَدَعْوَاهُ. وَاللَّهُ سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى يَعْلَمُ مَا كَانَ وَمَا يَكُونُ، وَمَا لَمْ يَكُنْ لَوْ كَانَ كَيْفَ يَكُونُ . وَهَذَا مُجْمَعٌ عَلَيْهِ عِنْدَ أَئِمَّةِ السُّنَّةِ وَالْجَمَاعَةِ؛ وَلِهَذَا يَقُولُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ وَغَيْرُهُ فِي مِثْلِ: ﴿إِلا لِنَعْلَمَ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ١٤٣] : إِلَّا لِنَرَى؛ وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ الرُّؤْيَةَ إِنَّمَا تَتَعَلَّقُ بِالْمَوْجُودِ، وَالْعِلْمُ أَعَمُّ مِنَ الرُّؤْيَةِ، فَإِنَّهُ [يَتَعَلَّقُ] بِالْمَعْدُومِ وَالْمَوْجُودِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَمْ حَسِبَ الَّذِينَ يَعْمَلُونَ السَّيِّئَاتِ أَنْ يَسْبِقُونَا سَاءَ مَا يَحْكُمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَحْسَبَنَّ الَّذِينَ لَمْ يَدْخُلُوا فِي الْإِيمَانِ أَنَّهُمْ يَتَخَلَّصُونَ مِنْ هَذِهِ الْفِتْنَةِ وَالِامْتِحَانِ، فَإِنَّ مِنْ وَرَائِهِمْ مِنَ الْعُقُوبَةِ والنكال ما هُوَ أَغْلَظُ مِنْ هَذَا وَأَطَمُّ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿أَمْ حَسِبَ الَّذِينَ يَعْمَلُونَ السَّيِّئَاتِ أَنْ يَسْبِقُونَا﴾ أَيْ: يَفُوتُونَا، ﴿سَاءَ مَا يَحْكُمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: بِئْسَ مَا يَظُنُّونَ.

---

## 29:5-7 — verses 5-7 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says: {Whoever hopes for the meeting with Allah}, that is, in the Hereafter, and does righteous deeds hoping for the abundant reward that is with Allah, then Allah will surely fulfill his hope for him and repay his deeds in full, complete and abundant, for that is bound to happen without fail, because He is the Hearer of supplication, the All-Seeing of all that exists. This is why He said: {Whoever hopes for the meeting with Allah, then indeed the appointed time of Allah is coming, and He is the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing}.

As for His saying: {And whoever strives, strives only for himself}, this is like His saying: {Whoever does righteousness, it is for himself} [Fussilat: 46], meaning: whoever does a righteous deed, the benefit of his deed returns only to himself, for Allah is free of need of the deeds of His servants. Even if all of them were as pious as the heart of the most God-fearing man among them, that would not add anything to His dominion. This is why He said: {And whoever strives, strives only for himself. Indeed, Allah is free of need of all the worlds}.

Al-Hasan al-Basri said: A man may strive, yet never have struck a single blow with a sword in his entire life.

Then He informs us that, despite His being free of need of all creation, out of His kindness and generosity toward them, He rewards those who believe and do righteous deeds with the best reward. This means that He erases from them the worst of what they did, and repays them for their deeds with the best of what they used to do. He accepts even a small amount of good deeds, and rewards a single good deed with ten times its like, up to seven hundredfold, while He repays an evil deed with its equivalent, or else pardons and overlooks it, as the Exalted said: {Indeed, Allah does not wrong anyone even the weight of an atom, and if there is a good deed, He multiplies it and gives from Himself a great reward} [al-Nisa: 40]. And He said here: {And those who believe and do righteous deeds, We will surely erase from them their sins and We will surely reward them with the best of what they used to do}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿مَنْ كَانَ يَرْجُو لِقَاءَ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ، وَعَمِلَ الصَّالِحَاتِ رَجَاءَ مَا عِنْدَ اللَّهِ مِنَ الثَّوَابِ الْجَزِيلِ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ سَيُحَقِّقُ لَهُ رَجَاءَهُ وَيُوَفِّيهِ عَمَلَهُ كَامِلًا مَوْفُورًا ، فَإِنَّ ذَلِكَ كَائِنٌ لَا مَحَالَةَ؛ لِأَنَّهُ سَمِيعُ الدُّعَاءِ، بَصِيرٌ بِكُلِّ الْكَائِنَاتِ ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿مَنْ كَانَ يَرْجُو لِقَاءَ اللَّهِ فَإِنَّ أَجَلَ اللَّهِ لآتٍ وَهُوَ السَّمِيعُ الْعَلِيمُ﴾ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَنْ جَاهَدَ فَإِنَّمَا يُجَاهِدُ لِنَفْسِهِ﴾ ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿مَنْ عَمِلَ صَالِحًا فَلِنَفْسِهِ﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ: ٤٦] أَيْ: مَنْ عَمِلَ صَالَحَا فَإِنَّمَا يَعُودُ نَفْعُ عَمَلِهِ عَلَى نَفْسِهِ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ غَنِيٌّ عَنْ أَفْعَالِ الْعِبَادِ، وَلَوْ كَانُوا كُلُّهُمْ عَلَى أَتْقَى قَلْبِ رَجُلٍ [وَاحِدٍ] مِنْهُمْ، مَا زَادَ ذَلِكَ فِي مُلْكِهِ شَيْئًا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَمَنْ جَاهَدَ فَإِنَّمَا يُجَاهِدُ لِنَفْسِهِ إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَغَنِيٌّ عَنِ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾ .

قَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: إِنَّ الرَّجُلَ لِيُجَاهِدُ، وَمَا ضَرَبَ يَوْمًا مِنَ الدَّهْرِ بِسَيْفٍ.

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ أَنَّهُ مَعَ غِنَاهُ عَنِ الْخَلَائِقِ جَمِيعِهِمْ مِنْ إِحْسَانِهِ وَبِرِّهِ بِهِمْ يُجَازِي الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ أَحْسَنَ الْجَزَاءِ، وَهُوَ أَنَّهُ يُكَفِّرُ عَنْهُمْ أَسْوَأَ الَّذِي عَمِلُوا، وَيَجْزِيهِمْ أَجْرَهُمْ بِأَحْسَنِ مَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ، فَيَقْبَلُ الْقَلِيلَ مِنَ الْحَسَنَاتِ، وَيُثِيبُ عَلَيْهَا الْوَاحِدَةُ بِعَشْرِ أَمْثَالِهَا إِلَى سَبْعِمِائَةِ ضِعْفٍ، وَيَجْزِي عَلَى السَّيِّئَةِ بِمِثْلِهَا أَوْ يَعْفُو وَيَصْفَحُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَظْلِمُ مِثْقَالَ ذَرَّةٍ وَإِنْ تَكُ حَسَنَةً يُضَاعِفْهَا وَيُؤْتِ مِنْ لَدُنْهُ أَجْرًا عَظِيمًا﴾ [النِّسَاءِ: ٤٠] ، وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ لَنُكَفِّرَنَّ عَنْهُمْ سَيِّئَاتِهِمْ وَلَنَجْزِيَنَّهُمْ أَحْسَنَ الَّذِي كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ﴾

---

## 29:8-9 — verses 8-9 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says, commanding His servants to show kindness to their parents after urging them to hold fast to His oneness, for parents are the cause of a person's existence, and they have upon him the utmost measure of kindness owed. The father through spending, the mother through tender compassion. For this reason the Exalted said: {And your Lord has decreed that you worship none but Him, and that you show kindness to parents. Whether one or both of them reach old age in your care, do not say to them "ugh" nor rebuke them, but speak to them a noble word. And lower to them the wing of humility out of mercy, and say: My Lord, have mercy upon them as they raised me when I was small} [al-Isra: 23, 24].

And alongside this instruction of tenderness, mercy, and kindness toward them, in return for their aforementioned kindness, He said: {But if they strive to make you associate with Me that of which you have no knowledge, do not obey them}, meaning: if they are eager for you to follow them in their religion when they are polytheists, then beware, do not obey them in that, for your return is to Me on the Day of Resurrection, and I will reward you for your kindness to them and your patience in holding to your religion, and I will gather you with the righteous, not among the ranks of your parents, even though you are the closest of people to them in this world. For a person is gathered on the Day of Resurrection with whomever he loved, meaning a religious love. For this reason He said: {And those who believed and did righteous deeds, We will surely admit them among the righteous}.

Al-Tirmidhi said, in his commentary on this verse: [chain] Muhammad ibn Bashshar and Muhammad ibn al-Muthanna told us, Muhammad ibn Ja'far told us, Shu'bah told us, from Simak ibn Harb, who said: I heard Mus'ab ibn Sa'd narrating from his father Sa'd, who said: Four verses were revealed concerning me. He then mentioned a story: Sa'd's mother said, "Has God not commanded you to show filial devotion? By God, I will not eat food nor drink drink until I die, or until you disbelieve." He said: So whenever they wanted to feed her, they would force her mouth open. Then God sent down: {And We have enjoined upon man kindness to his parents, but if they strive} the verse.

This hadith was also related by Imam Ahmad, Muslim, Abu Dawud, and al-Nasa'i. Al-Tirmidhi said: hasan sahih (a sound and authentic report).

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى آمِرًا عِبَادُهُ بِالْإِحْسَانِ إِلَى الْوَالِدَيْنِ بَعْدَ الْحَثِّ عَلَى التَّمَسُّكِ بِتَوْحِيدِهِ، فَإِنَّ الْوَالِدَيْنِ هَمَّا سَبَبُ وُجُودِ الْإِنْسَانِ، وَلَهُمَا عَلَيْهِ غَايَةُ الْإِحْسَانِ، فَالْوَالِدُ بِالْإِنْفَاقِ وَالْوَالِدَةُ بِالْإِشْفَاقِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَقَضَى رَبُّكَ أَلا تَعْبُدُوا إِلا إِيَّاهُ وَبِالْوَالِدَيْنِ إِحْسَانًا إِمَّا يَبْلُغَنَّ عِنْدَكَ الْكِبَرَ أَحَدُهُمَا أَوْ كِلاهُمَا فَلا تَقُلْ لَهُمَا أُفٍّ وَلا تَنْهَرْهُمَا وَقُلْ لَهُمَا قَوْلا كَرِيمًا، وَاخْفِضْ لَهُمَا جَنَاحَ الذُّلِّ مِنَ الرَّحْمَةِ وَقُلْ رَبِّي ارْحَمْهُمَا كَمَا رَبَّيَانِي صَغِيرًا﴾ [الإسراء: ٢٣، ٢٤] .

وَمَعَ هَذِهِ الْوَصِيَّةِ بِالرَّأْفَةِ وَالرَّحْمَةِ وَالْإِحْسَانِ إِلَيْهِمَا، فِي مُقَابَلَةِ إِحْسَانِهِمَا الْمُتَقَدِّمِ، قَالَ: ﴿وَإِنْ جَاهَدَاكَ لِتُشْرِكَ بِي مَا لَيْسَ لَكَ بِهِ عِلْمٌ فَلا تُطِعْهُمَا﴾ أَيْ: وَإِنْ حَرَصا عَلَيْكَ أَنْ تُتَابِعَهُمَا عَلَى دِينِهِمَا إِذَا كَانَا مُشْرِكَيْنِ، فَإِيَّاكَ وَإِيَّاهُمَا، لَا تُطِعْهُمَا فِي ذَلِكَ، فَإِنَّ مَرْجِعَكُمْ إِلَيَّ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَأَجْزِيكَ بِإِحْسَانِكَ إِلَيْهِمَا، وَصَبْرِكَ عَلَى دِينِكَ، وَأَحْشُرُكَ مَعَ الصَّالِحِينَ لَا فِي زُمْرَةِ وَالِدَيْكَ، وَإِنْ كُنْتَ أَقْرَبَ النَّاسِ إِلَيْهِمَا فِي الدُّنْيَا، فَإِنَّ الْمَرْءَ إِنَّمَا يُحْشَرُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ مَعَ مَنْ أَحَبَّ، أَيْ: حُبًّا دِينِيًّا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ لَنُدْخِلَنَّهُمْ فِي الصَّالِحِينَ﴾ .

وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ عِنْدَ تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بَشَّارٍ وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الْمُثَنَّى، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ سِمَاك بْنُ حَرْبٍ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ مُصعَب بْنَ سَعْدٍ يُحَدِّثُ عَنْ أَبِيهِ سَعْدٍ، قَالَ: نَزَلَتْ فيَّ أَرْبَعُ آيَاتٍ. فَذَكَرَ قِصَّةً، وَقَالَتْ أُمُّ سَعْدٍ: أَلَيْسَ قَدْ أَمَرَكَ اللَّهُ بِالْبَرِّ؟ وَاللَّهِ لَا أطعَمُ طَعَامًا وَلَا أَشْرَبُ شَرَابًا حَتَّى أَمُوتَ أَوْ تَكْفُرَ، قَالَ: فَكَانُوا إِذَا أَرَادُوا أَنْ يُطْعِمُوهَا شَجَروا فَاهَا، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ ﴿وَوَصَّيْنَا الإنْسَانَ بِوَالِدَيْهِ حُسْنًا وَإِنْ جَاهَدَاكَ﴾ الْآيَةَ.

وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، وَمُسْلِمٌ، وَأَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ أَيْضًا ، وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ.

---

## 29:10-11 — verses 10-11 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing about the characteristics of a group of the [deniers] who claim faith with their tongues while faith has not been established firmly in their hearts: that when a trial and hardship comes to them in this world, they believe that this is a punishment from Allah against them, and so they apostatize from Islam. Hence He said: {Among the people are those who say, "We believe in Allah," but when they are harmed for the sake of Allah, they treat the persecution of people as if it were the punishment of Allah}.

Ibn Abbas said: meaning, their trial is that they apostatize from their religion when they are harmed for the sake of Allah. Others among the scholars of the earlier generations said likewise. This verse is like His statement: {And among the people is he who worships Allah on the edge: if good befalls him he is content with it, but if a trial befalls him he turns his face away, losing this world and the Hereafter. That is the manifest loss} [al-Hajj: 11].

Then He said: {And if victory comes from your Lord, they will surely say, "Indeed, we were with you"}, meaning: and if a near victory comes from your Lord, O Muhammad, along with conquest and spoils, these people will say to you: "Indeed, we were with you," meaning, "we were your brothers in religion," just as the Almighty said: {Those who wait to see what happens to you: if a victory comes to you from Allah, they say, "Were we not with you?" But if the disbelievers get a share, they say, "Did we not gain the advantage over you and protect you from the believers?"} [al-Nisa: 141]. And the Almighty said: {So perhaps Allah will bring victory or a matter from Himself, and they will become, over what they concealed within themselves, regretful} [al-Ma'idah: 52].

The Almighty says here, informing about them: {And if victory comes from your Lord, they will surely say, "Indeed, we were with you"}, then He said: {Is not Allah most knowing of what is in the breasts of all creatures?} meaning: is not Allah most knowing of what is in their hearts, and what their inner selves conceal, even if they show you outward agreement?

His statement: {And Allah will surely know those who believe, and He will surely know the hypocrites} means: Allah will surely test people through hardship and ease, so that these may be distinguished from those, and whoever obeys Allah in both hardship and ease does so only for the good of his own soul, just as the Almighty said: {And We will surely test you until We know those who strive among you and those who are patient, and We will test your accounts} [Muhammad: 31]. And the Almighty said after the battle of Uhud, in which there occurred what occurred of testing and trial: {Allah would not leave the believers in the state you are in until He distinguishes the corrupt from the good}, the verse [Al Imran: 179]. And Allah knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ صِفَاتِ قَوْمٍ مِنَ [الْمُكَذِّبِينَ] الَّذِينَ يَدَّعُونَ الْإِيمَانَ بِأَلْسِنَتِهِمْ، وَلَمْ يَثْبُتِ الْإِيمَانُ فِي قُلُوبِهِمْ، بِأَنَّهُمْ إِذَا جَاءَتْهُمْ فِتْنَةٌ وَمِحْنَةٌ فِي الدُّنْيَا، اعْتَقَدُوا أَنَّ هَذَا مِنْ نِقْمَةِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى بِهِمْ، فَارْتَدُّوا عَنِ الْإِسْلَامِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَمِنَ النَّاسِ مَنْ يَقُولُ آمَنَّا بِاللَّهِ فَإِذَا أُوذِيَ فِي اللَّهِ جَعَلَ فِتْنَةَ النَّاسِ كَعَذَابِ اللَّهِ﴾ .

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: يَعْنِي فِتْنَتَهُ أَنْ يَرْتَدَّ عَنْ دِينِهِ إِذَا أُوذِيَ فِي اللَّهِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ غَيْرُهُ مِنْ عُلَمَاءِ السَّلَفِ. وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمِنَ النَّاسِ مَنْ يَعْبُدُ اللَّهَ عَلَى حَرْفٍ فَإِنْ أَصَابَهُ خَيْرٌ اطْمَأَنَّ بِهِ وَإِنْ أَصَابَتْهُ فِتْنَةٌ انْقَلَبَ عَلَى وَجْهِهِ خَسِرَ الدُّنْيَا وَالآخِرَةَ ذَلِكَ هُوَ الْخُسْرَانُ الْمُبِينُ﴾ [الْحَجِّ: ١١] .

ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿وَلَئِنْ جَاءَ نَصْرٌ مِنْ رَبِّكَ لَيَقُولُنَّ إِنَّا كُنَّا مَعَكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: وَلَئِنْ جَاءَ نَصْرٌ قَرِيبٌ مِنْ رَبِّكَ -يَا مُحَمَّدُ -وَفَتْحٌ وَمَغَانِمُ، لَيَقُولُنَّ هَؤُلَاءِ لَكُمْ: إِنَّا كُنَّا مَعَكُمْ، أَيْ [كُنَّا] إخوانكم في الدين، كما قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿الَّذِينَ يَتَرَبَّصُونَ بِكُمْ فَإِنْ كَانَ لَكُمْ فَتْحٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ قَالُوا أَلَمْ نَكُنْ مَعَكُمْ وَإِنْ كَانَ لِلْكَافِرِينَ نَصِيبٌ قَالُوا أَلَمْ نَسْتَحْوِذْ عَلَيْكُمْ وَنَمْنَعْكُمْ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ [النِّسَاءِ: ١٤١] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَعَسَى اللَّهُ أَنْ يَأْتِيَ بِالْفَتْحِ أَوْ أَمْرٍ مِنْ عِنْدِهِ فَيُصْبِحُوا عَلَى مَا أَسَرُّوا فِي أَنْفُسِهِمْ نَادِمِينَ﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ: ٥٢] .

وَقَالَ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْهُمْ هَاهُنَا: ﴿وَلَئِنْ جَاءَ نَصْرٌ مِنْ رَبِّكَ لَيَقُولُنَّ إِنَّا كُنَّا مَعَكُمْ﴾ ، ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَوَلَيْسَ اللَّهُ بِأَعْلَمَ بِمَا فِي صُدُورِ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: أَوَلَيِسَ اللَّهُ بِأَعْلَمَ بِمَا فِي قُلُوبِهِمْ، وَمَا تكنُّه ضَمَائِرُهُمْ، وَإِنْ أَظْهَرُوا لَكُمُ الْمُوَافَقَةَ؟

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَيَعْلَمَنَّ اللَّهُ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَلَيَعْلَمَنَّ الْمُنَافِقِينَ﴾ أَيْ: وليختبرَنّ اللَّهُ النَّاسَ بِالضَّرَّاءِ وَالسَّرَّاءِ، لِيَتَمَيَّزَ هَؤُلَاءِ مِنْ هَؤُلَاءِ، وَمَنْ يُطِيعُ اللَّهَ فِي الضَّرَّاءِ وَالسَّرَّاءِ، إِنَّمَا يُطِيعُهُ فِي حَظِّ نَفْسِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَنَبْلُوَنَّكُمْ حَتَّى نَعْلَمَ الْمُجَاهِدِينَ مِنْكُمْ وَالصَّابِرِينَ وَنَبْلُوَ أَخْبَارَكُمْ﴾ [مُحَمَّدٍ: ٣١] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى بَعْدَ وَقْعَةِ أُحُدٍ، الَّتِي كَانَ فِيهَا مَا كَانَ مِنَ الِاخْتِبَارِ وَالِامْتِحَانِ: ﴿مَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيَذَرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عَلَى مَا أَنْتُمْ عَلَيْهِ حَتَّى يَمِيزَ الْخَبِيثَ مِنَ الطَّيِّبِ﴾ الْآيَةَ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ: ١٧٩] ، [وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ] .

---

## 29:12-13 — verses 12-13 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, reporting about the disbelievers of Quraysh, that they said to those among them who believed and followed guidance: return from your religion to our religion, and follow our path, {and let us carry your sins}, meaning: and your burdens, if you have any burdens in that, upon us and on our necks, just as a speaker says, "Do this, and your fault is on my neck." God said, denying their claim: {But they will not carry anything of their sins. Indeed, they are liars}, meaning: in what they said, that they would carry the sins of those people, for no one carries the burden of another. {And if a heavily laden soul calls for help with its load, nothing of it will be carried, even if he be a close relative} [Fatir: 18]. And the Almighty said: {And no intimate friend will ask about an intimate friend. They will be shown to each other} [al-Ma'arij: 10, 11].

His saying: {And they will surely carry their own burdens, and other burdens along with their own burdens} is a report about those who call to disbelief and misguidance, that on the Day of Resurrection they will carry the burdens of their own selves, and other burdens because of the people they misguided, without anything being diminished from the burdens of those others, just as the Almighty said: {That they may carry their own burdens in full on the Day of Resurrection, and some of the burdens of those whom they misguide without knowledge. Unquestionably, evil is that which they bear} [al-Nahl: 25].

In the Sahih: "Whoever calls to guidance will have a reward like the rewards of those who follow him until the Day of Resurrection, without anything being diminished from their rewards, and whoever calls to misguidance will bear a sin like the sins of those who follow him until the Day of Resurrection, without anything being diminished from their sins." And in the Sahih: "No soul is killed unjustly except that a share of its blood falls upon the first son of Adam, because he was the first to establish the practice of killing."

His saying: {And they will surely be asked on the Day of Resurrection about what they used to fabricate}, meaning: what they used to lie about and invent of slander.

Ibn Abi Hatim mentioned here a hadith, saying: [chain] Abu Umamah, may God be pleased with him, said: the Messenger of God ﷺ conveyed what he had been sent with, then said: "Beware of injustice, for God will make a solemn declaration on the Day of Resurrection and say: By My might, no injustice shall pass by Me today! Then a caller will call out and say: Where is so-and-so son of so-and-so? He will come with good deeds following him like mountains, and the people will fix their gazes upon them until he stands before God, the Most Merciful, Mighty and Majestic. Then He will command the caller, who will call out: whoever has a claim, or a grievance, against so-and-so son of so-and-so, let him come forward. So they will come until they gather standing before the Most Merciful, and the Most Merciful will say: settle My servant's debt. They will say: how shall we settle it on his behalf? He will say to them: take from his good deeds for them. So they will keep taking from them until no good deed remains for him, while some of the wronged parties still remain. He will say: settle My servant's debt. They will say: no good deed remains for him. He will say: take from their evil deeds and place them upon him." Then the Prophet ﷺ drew out this noble verse: {And they will surely carry their own burdens, and other burdens along with their own burdens, and they will surely be asked on the Day of Resurrection about what they used to fabricate}.

This hadith has a corroborating witness in the Sahih from a different route.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Mu'adh ibn Jabal, may God be pleased with him, said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said to me: "O Mu'adh, indeed the believer will be asked on the Day of Resurrection about all of his efforts, even about the kohl of his eyes, and about the crumbs of clay between his two fingers, so do not let Me find you coming on the Day of Resurrection with anyone happier than you with what God has given you."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ كُفَّارِ قُرَيْشٍ: أَنَّهُمْ قَالُوا لِمَنْ آمَنَ مِنْهُمْ وَاتَّبَعَ الْهُدَى: ارْجِعُوا عَنْ دِينِكُمْ إِلَى دِينِنَا، وَاتَّبَعُوا سَبِيلَنَا، ﴿وَلْنَحْمِلْ خَطَايَاكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: وَآثَامَكُمْ -إِنْ كَانَتْ لَكُمْ آثَامٌ فِي ذَلِكَ -عَلَيْنَا وَفِي رِقَابِنَا، كَمَا يَقُولُ الْقَائِلُ: "افْعَلْ هَذَا وَخَطِيئَتُكَ فِي رَقَبَتِي". قَالَ اللَّهُ تَكْذِيبًا لَهُمْ: ﴿وَمَا هُمْ بِحَامِلِينَ مِنْ خَطَايَاهُمْ مِنْ شَيْءٍ إِنَّهُمْ لَكَاذِبُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فِيمَا قَالُوهُ: إِنَّهُمْ يَحْمِلُونَ عَنْ أُولَئِكَ خَطَايَاهُمْ، فَإِنَّهُ لَا يَحْمِلُ أَحَدٌ وِزْرَ أَحَدٍ، ﴿وَإِنْ تَدْعُ مُثْقَلَةٌ إِلَى حِمْلِهَا لَا يُحْمَلْ مِنْهُ شَيْءٌ وَلَوْ كَانَ ذَا قُرْبَى﴾ [فَاطِرَ: ١٨] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلا يَسْأَلُ حَمِيمٌ حَمِيمًا. يُبَصَّرُونَهُمْ﴾ [الْمَعَارِجِ: ١٠، ١١] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَيَحْمِلُنَّ أَثْقَالَهُمْ وَأَثْقَالا مَعَ أَثْقَالِهِمْ﴾ : إِخْبَارٌ عَنِ الدُّعَاةِ إِلَى الْكُفْرِ وَالضَّلَالَةِ، أَنَّهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ يَحْمِلُونَ أَوْزَارَ أَنْفُسِهِمْ، وَأَوْزَارًا أخَر بِسَبَبِ مَنْ أَضَلُّوا مِنَ النَّاسِ، مِنْ غَيْرِ أَنْ يُنْقَصَ مِنْ أَوْزَارِ أُولَئِكَ شَيْئًا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لِيَحْمِلُوا أَوْزَارَهُمْ كَامِلَةً يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَمِنْ أَوْزَارِ الَّذِينَ يُضِلُّونَهُمْ بِغَيْرِ عِلْمٍ أَلا سَاءَ مَا يَزِرُونَ﴾ [النَّحْلِ: ٢٥] .

وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ: "مَنْ دَعَا إِلَى هَدْيٍ كَانَ لَهُ مِنَ الْأَجْرِ مِثْلُ أُجُورِ مَنِ اتَّبَعَهُ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ، مِنْ غَيْرِ أَنْ يَنْقُصَ مِنْ أُجُورِهِمْ شَيْئًا، وَمَنْ دَعَا إِلَى ضَلَالَةٍ كَانَ عَلَيْهِ مِنَ الْإِثْمِ مِثْلُ آثَامِ مَنِ اتَّبَعَهُ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ، مِنْ غَيْرِ أَنْ يَنْقُصَ مِنْ آثَامِهِمْ شَيْئًا" وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ: "مَا قُتِلَتْ نَفْسٌ ظُلْمًا إِلَّا كَانَ عَلَى ابْنِ آدَمَ الْأَوَّلِ كِفْلٌ مِنْ دَمِهَا؛ لِأَنَّهُ أَوَّلُ مَنْ سَنّ الْقَتْلَ" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَيُسْأَلُنَّ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ عَمَّا كَانُوا يَفْتَرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يَكْذِبُونَ وَيَخْتَلِقُونَ مِنَ الْبُهْتَانِ.

وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ هَاهُنَا حَدِيثًا فَقَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا هِشَامُ بْنُ عَمَّارٍ، حَدَّثَنَا صَدَقَةُ، حَدَّثَنَا عُثْمَانُ بْنُ حَفْصِ بْنِ أَبِي الْعَالِيَةِ، حَدَّثَنِي سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ حَبِيبٍ الْمُحَارِبِيُّ عَنْ أَبِي أُمَامَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: إِنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَلَّغَ مَا أُرْسِلَ بِهِ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: "إِيَّاكُمْ وَالظُّلْمَ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يَعْزِمُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ فَيَقُولُ: وَعِزَّتِي لَا يَجُوزُنِي الْيَوْمَ ظُلْمٌ! ثُمَّ يُنَادِي مُنَادٍ فَيَقُولُ: أَيْنَ فُلَانُ ابْنُ فُلَانٍ؟ فَيَأْتِي يَتْبَعُهُ مِنَ الْحَسَنَاتِ أَمْثَالُ الْجِبَالِ، فَيُشْخِصُ النَّاسُ إِلَيْهَا أَبْصَارَهُمْ حَتَّى يَقُومَ بَيْنَ يَدَيِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَنِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ ثُمَّ يَأْمُرُ الْمُنَادِي فَيُنَادِي مَنْ كَانَتْ لَهُ تِبَاعة -أَوْ: ظُلامة -عِنْدَ فُلَانِ ابْنِ فُلَانٍ، فَهَلُمَّ. فَيُقْبِلُونَ حَتَّى يَجْتَمِعُوا قِيَامًا بَيْنَ يَدَيِ الرَّحْمَنِ، فَيَقُولُ الرَّحْمَنُ: اقْضُوا عَنْ عَبْدِي. فَيَقُولُونَ: كَيْفَ نَقْضِي عَنْهُ؟ فَيَقُولُ لَهُمْ: خُذُوا لَهُمْ مِنْ حَسَنَاتِهِ. فَلَا يَزَالُونَ يَأْخُذُونَ مِنْهَا حَتَّى لَا يَبْقَى لَهُ حَسَنَةٌ، وَقَدْ بَقِيَ مِنْ أَصْحَابِ الظُّلَامَاتِ، فَيَقُولُ: اقْضُوا عَنْ عَبْدِي. فَيَقُولُونَ: لَمْ يَبْقَ لَهُ حَسَنَةٌ. فَيَقُولُ: خُذُوا مِنْ سَيِّئَاتِهِمْ فَاحْمِلُوهَا عَلَيْهِ". ثُمَّ نَزَعَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ: ﴿وَلَيَحْمِلُنَّ أَثْقَالَهُمْ وَأَثْقَالا مَعَ أَثْقَالِهِمْ وَلَيُسْأَلُنَّ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ عَمَّا كَانُوا يَفْتَرُونَ﴾ .

وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ لَهُ شَاهِدٌ فِي الصَّحِيحِ مِنْ غَيْرِ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ أَبِي الْحِوَارِيِّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو بِشْرٍ الْحَذَّاءُ، عَنْ أَبِي حَمْزَةَ الثُّمَالِيِّ، عَنْ مُعَاذِ بْنِ جَبَلٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ لِي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "يَا مُعَاذُ، إِنَّ الْمُؤْمِنَ يُسْأَلُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ عَنْ جَمِيعِ سَعْيِهِ، حَتَّى عَنْ كُحْل عَيْنَيْهِ، وَعَنْ فُتَاتِ الطِّينَةِ بِأُصْبُعَيْهِ ، فَلَا ألْفَيَنَّكَ تَأْتِي يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَأَحَدٌ أَسْعَدُ بِمَا آتَاكَ اللَّهُ مِنْكَ" .

---

## 29:14-15 — verses 14-15 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is a consolation from Allah Most High to His servant and messenger Muhammad ﷺ, informing him about Nuh (peace be upon him): that he remained among his people for this length of time calling them to Allah by night and by day, secretly and openly, and despite this it only increased them in fleeing from the truth, turning away from it, and denying it, and none believed with him except a few. Therefore He said: {So he remained among them a thousand years less fifty years, then the flood seized them while they were wrongdoers}. That is: after this long period, the conveying of the message and the warning had no beneficial effect upon them. So you, O Muhammad, do not grieve over those of your people who disbelieved in you, and do not be sorrowful over them, for Allah guides whom He wills and leads astray whom He wills, and the matter is in His hand and to Him all matters return. {Indeed, those upon whom the word of your Lord has come into effect will not believe. Even if every sign should come to them, until they see the painful punishment} [Yunus: 96, 97]. And know that Allah will make you manifest, grant you victory, and support you, and will humiliate your enemy, cast them down, and make them the lowest of the low.

Hammad ibn Salamah said, from Ali ibn Zayd, from Yusuf ibn Mahak, from Ibn Abbas, who said: Nuh was sent as a prophet at the age of forty, and he remained among his people for a thousand years less fifty years, and he lived after the flood for sixty years, until people multiplied and spread.

Qatadah said: It is said that his entire lifespan was a thousand years less fifty years; he remained among them before calling them for three hundred years, called them for three hundred years, and remained after the flood for three hundred and fifty years.

This is a gharib (unusual) statement, and the apparent sense of the wording of the verse is that he remained among his people calling them to Allah for a thousand years less fifty years.

Awn ibn Abi Shaddad said: Allah sent Nuh to his people when he was three hundred and fifty years old, and he called them for a thousand years less fifty years, then he lived after that for three hundred and fifty years.

This too is gharib. It was narrated by Ibn Abi Hatim and Ibn Jarir. The statement of Ibn Abbas is closer to being correct, and Allah knows best.

Al-Thawri said, from Salamah ibn Kuhayl, from Mujahid, who said: Ibn Umar said to me: How long did Nuh remain among his people? I said: A thousand years less fifty years. He said: People have continued to decrease in their lifespans, their intellects, and their character up to this very day of yours.

His saying: {So We saved him and the companions of the ship}, that is, those who believed in Nuh (peace be upon him). Mention of this has already been given in detail in Surat Hud, and its exegesis has already been presented in a manner that makes repeating it unnecessary.

His saying: {And We made it a sign for the worlds}, that is: We made that ship remain, whether its very self, as Qatadah said: that it remained until the early period of Islam upon Mount al-Judi, or its kind, which He made for people as a reminder of His favors upon creation, of how He saved them from the flood, as He, Most High, said: {And a sign for them is that We carried their offspring in the laden ship. And We created for them from the like of it that which they ride. And if We willed, We could drown them, then no one would cry out for them, nor would they be saved, except by mercy from Us and as enjoyment for a time} [Ya-Sin: 41-44]. And He, Most High, said: {Indeed, when the water overflowed, We carried you in the sailing ship, that We might make it for you a reminder, and that a retaining ear might retain it} [al-Haqqah: 11, 12]. And He said here: {So We saved him and the companions of the ship and made it a sign for the worlds}. This is of the type of gradation from the particular individual to the general kind, like His saying, Most High: {And We have certainly adorned the nearest heaven with lamps and made them missiles for the devils} [al-Mulk: 5], meaning: and We made their kind so, for the ones that are thrown are not the same ones that are an adornment for the sky. And He, Most High, said: {And We did certainly create man from an extract of clay. Then We made him a sperm-drop in a firm lodging} [al-Muminun: 12, 13]. There are many similar examples to this.

Ibn Jarir said: If it were said that the pronoun in His saying {and made it} refers back to the punishment, that would be a plausible interpretation, and Allah knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذِهِ تَسْلِيَةٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى لِعَبْدِهِ وَرَسُولِهِ مُحَمَّدٍ صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، يُخْبِرُهُ عَنْ نُوحٍ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ: أَنَّهُ مَكَثَ فِي قَوْمِهِ هَذِهِ الْمُدَّةَ يَدْعُوهُمْ إِلَى اللَّهِ لَيْلًا وَنَهَارًا، وَسِرًّا، وجهارًا، وَمَعَ هَذَا مَا زَادَهُمْ ذَلِكَ إِلَّا فِرَارًا عَنِ الْحَقِّ، وَإِعْرَاضًا عَنْهُ وَتَكْذِيبًا لَهُ، وَمَا آمَنُ مَعَهُ مِنْهُمْ إِلَّا قَلِيلٌ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَلَبِثَ فِيهِمْ أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ إِلا خَمْسِينَ عَامًا فَأَخَذَهُمُ الطُّوفَانُ وَهُمْ ظَالِمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: بَعْدَ هَذِهِ الْمُدَّةِ الطَّوِيلَةِ مَا نَجَعَ فِيهِمُ الْبَلَاغُ وَالْإِنْذَارُ، فَأَنْتَ -يَا مُحَمَّدُ -لَا تَأْسَفْ عَلَى مَنْ كَفَرَ بِكَ مِنْ قَوْمِكَ، وَلَا تَحْزَنْ عَلَيْهِمْ؛ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يَهْدِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيَضِلُّ مَنْ يَشَاءُ، وَبِيَدِهِ الْأَمْرُ وَإِلَيْهِ تُرْجَعُ الْأُمُورُ، ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ حَقَّتْ عَلَيْهِمْ كَلِمَةُ رَبِّكَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ. وَلَوْ جَاءَتْهُمْ كُلُّ آيَةٍ حَتَّى يَرَوُا الْعَذَابَ الألِيمَ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ٩٦،٩٧] ، وَاعْلَمْ أَنَّ اللَّهَ سَيُظْهِرُكَ وَيَنْصُرُكَ وَيُؤَيِّدُكَ، وَيُذِلُّ عَدُوَّكَ، وَيَكْبِتُهُمْ وَيَجْعَلُهُمْ أَسْفَلَ السَّافِلِينَ.

قَالَ حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ زَيْدٍ، عَنْ يُوسُفَ بْنِ ماهَك ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: بُعِثَ نُوحٌ وَهُوَ لِأَرْبَعِينَ سَنَةٍ، وَلَبِثَ فِي قَوْمِهِ أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ إِلَّا خَمْسِينَ عَامًا، وَعَاشَ بَعْدَ الطُّوفَانِ سِتِّينَ عَامًا، حَتَّى كَثُرَ النَّاسُ وَفَشَوْا.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: يُقَالُ إِنَّ عُمُرَهُ كُلَّهُ [كَانَ] أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ إِلَّا خَمْسِينَ عَامًا، لَبِثَ فِيهِمْ قَبْلَ أَنْ يَدْعُوَهُمْ ثَلَثَمِائَةِ سَنَةٍ، وَدَعَاهُمْ ثَلَثَمِائَةٍ وَلَبِثَ بَعْدَ الطُّوفَانِ ثَلَثَمِائَةٍ وَخَمْسِينَ سَنَةً.

وَهَذَا قَوْلٌ غَرِيبٌ، وَظَاهِرُ السِّيَاقِ مِنَ الْآيَةِ أَنَّهُ مَكَثَ فِي قَوْمِهِ يَدْعُوهُمْ إِلَى اللَّهِ أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ إِلَّا خَمْسِينَ عَامًا.

وَقَالَ عَوْنُ بْنُ أَبِي شَدَّادٍ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ أَرْسَلَ نُوحًا إِلَى قَوْمِهِ وَهُوَ ابْنُ خَمْسِينَ وَثَلَثَمِائَةِ سَنَةٍ، فَدَعَاهُمْ أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ إِلَّا خَمْسِينَ عَامًا، ثُمَّ عَاشَ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ ثَلَثَمِائَةٍ وَخَمْسِينَ سَنَةً.

وَهَذَا أَيْضًا غَرِيبٌ، رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَقَوْلُ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَقْرَبُ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ سَلَمَةَ بْنِ كُهَيْل، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ قَالَ: قَالَ لِيَ ابْنُ عُمَرَ: كَمْ لَبِثَ نُوحٌ فِي قَوْمِهِ؟ قَالَ: قُلْتُ أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ إِلَّا خَمْسِينَ عَامًا. قَالَ: فَإِنَّ النَّاسَ لَمْ يَزَالُوا فِي نُقْصَانٍ مِنْ أَعْمَارِهِمْ وَأَحْلَامِهِمْ وَأَخْلَاقِهِمْ إِلَى يَوْمِكَ هَذَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَأَنْجَيْنَاهُ وَأَصْحَابَ السَّفِينَةِ﴾ أَيِ: الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا بِنُوحٍ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ. وَقَدْ تقدَّم ذِكْرُ ذَلِكَ مُفَصَّلًا فِي سُورَةِ "هُودٍ"، وتقدَّم تَفْسِيرُهُ بِمَا أَغْنَى عَنْ إِعَادَتِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَجَعَلْنَاهَا آيَةً لِلْعَالَمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: وَجَعَلْنَا تِلْكَ السَّفِينَةَ بَاقِيَةً، إِمَّا عَيْنُهَا كَمَا قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: إِنَّهَا بَقِيَتْ إِلَى أَوَّلِ الْإِسْلَامِ عَلَى جَبَلِ الْجُودِيِّ، أَوْ نَوْعُهَا جَعَلَهُ لِلنَّاسِ تَذْكِرَةً لِنِعَمِهِ عَلَى الْخَلْقِ، كَيْفَ نَجَّاهُمْ مِنَ الطُّوفَانِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَآيَةٌ لَهُمْ أَنَّا حَمَلْنَا ذُرِّيَّتَهُمْ فِي الْفُلْكِ الْمَشْحُونِ. وَخَلَقْنَا لَهُمْ مِنْ مِثْلِهِ مَا يَرْكَبُونَ. وَإِنْ نَشَأْ نُغْرِقْهُمْ فَلا صَرِيخَ لَهُمْ وَلا هُمْ يُنْقَذُونَ. إِلا رَحْمَةً مِنَّا وَمَتَاعًا إِلَى حِينٍ﴾ [يس: ٤١-٤٤] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّا لَمَّا طَغَى الْمَاءُ حَمَلْنَاكُمْ فِي الْجَارِيَةِ. لِنَجْعَلَهَا لَكُمْ تَذْكِرَةً وَتَعِيَهَا أُذُنٌ وَاعِيَةٌ﴾ [الْحَاقَّةِ: ١١، ١٢] ، وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿فَأَنْجَيْنَاهُ وَأَصْحَابَ السَّفِينَةِ وَجَعَلْنَاهَا آيَةً لِلْعَالَمِينَ﴾ ، وَهَذَا مِنْ بَابِ التَّدْرِيجِ مِنَ الشَّخْصِ إِلَى الْجِنْسِ، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ زَيَّنَّا السَّمَاءَ الدُّنْيَا بِمَصَابِيحَ وَجَعَلْنَاهَا رُجُومًا لِلشَّيَاطِينِ﴾ [الْمُلْكِ: ٥] أَيْ: وَجَعَلَنَا نَوْعَهَا، فَإِنَّ الَّتِي يُرْمَى بِهَا لَيْسَتْ هِيَ الَّتِي زِينَةٌ لِلسَّمَاءِ . وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ خَلَقْنَا الإنْسَانَ مِنْ سُلالَةٍ مِنْ طِينٍ. ثُمَّ جَعَلْنَاهُ نُطْفَةً فِي قَرَارٍ مَكِينٍ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ: ١٢، ١٣] ، وَلِهَذَا نَظَائِرُ كَثِيرَةٌ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: لَوْ قِيلَ: إِنَّ الضَّمِيرَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَجَعَلْنَاهَا﴾ ، عَائِدٌ إِلَى الْعُقُوبَةِ، لَكَانَ وَجْهًا، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

---

## 29:16-18 — verses 16-18 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs us about His servant, messenger, and intimate friend Ibrahim, the leader of the huneafa (upright monotheists), that he called his people to the worship of God alone, without partner, to sincerity toward Him in piety, to seeking provision from Him alone without partner, and to affirming His oneness in gratitude, for He is the One who is thanked for blessings, and there is no bestower of them other than Him. He said to his people: {Worship God and fear Him}, meaning: make your worship and fear sincerely His alone. {That is better for you, if you but knew}, meaning: if you do that, good will be secured for you in this world and the hereafter, and evil will be repelled from you in this world and the hereafter.

Then he informed them that the idols and images which they worship neither harm nor benefit, and that they themselves had merely invented names for them, calling them gods, when in fact they are created things like yourselves. This is how al-Awfi related it from Ibn Abbas, and Mujahid and al-Suddi said likewise.

Al-Walibi related from Ibn Abbas concerning {and you fabricate a falsehood}: meaning, you carve them into idols. Mujahid said the same in one report, as did Ikrimah, al-Hasan, Qatadah, and others, and Ibn Jarir, may God have mercy on him, chose this view.

They possess no power to provide for you any provision, so {seek provision from God}. This is a more emphatic expression of exclusivity, like His saying: {You alone we worship, and You alone we ask for help} [al-Fatihah: 5], and {My Lord, build for me a house near You in Paradise} [al-Tahrim: 11]. Hence He said: {fabtaghu} (so seek) {from God provision}, meaning: not from anyone else, for no one besides Him possesses anything. {And worship Him and be grateful to Him}, meaning: eat from His provision, worship Him alone, and be grateful to Him for what He has bestowed upon you as blessing. {To Him you will be returned}, meaning: on the Day of Resurrection, when He will requite every doer according to his deed.

Concerning His saying: {And if you deny, then nations before you have already denied}, meaning: so there has reached you news of what befell them of punishment and retribution for opposing the messengers. {And the messenger is responsible only for clear conveyance}, meaning: the messenger's duty is only to convey to you what God, exalted is He, commanded him regarding the message. God leads astray whom He wills and guides whom He wills, so strive earnestly for yourselves to be among the fortunate.

Qatadah said concerning His words: {And if you deny, then nations before you have already denied}: this is to console His Prophet ﷺ. This statement of Qatadah implies that the preceding discourse had ended, and that this is inserted as a parenthetical remark up to His saying: {But what was the answer of his people}. Ibn Jarir likewise stated this explicitly.

But what is apparent from the context is that all of this is the speech of Ibrahim the Intimate Friend, peace be upon him, addressed to his people, arguing with them to establish the reality of the resurrection, given His saying after all of this: {But what was the answer of his people}. And God knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ عَبْدِهِ وَرَسُولِهِ وَخَلِيلِهِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ إِمَامِ الْحُنَفَاءِ: أَنَّهُ دَعَا قَوْمَهُ إِلَى عِبَادَةِ اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، وَالْإِخْلَاصِ لَهُ فِي التَّقْوَى، وَطَلَبِ الرِّزْقِ مِنْهُ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، وَتَوْحِيدِهِ فِي الشكر ، فإنه المشكور على النعم، لا مُسْدٍ لَهَا غَيْرُهُ، فَقَالَ لِقَوْمِهِ: ﴿اعْبُدُوا اللَّهَ وَاتَّقُوهُ﴾ أَيْ: أَخْلِصُوا لَهُ الْعِبَادَةَ وَالْخَوْفَ، ﴿ذَلِكُمْ خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ تَعْلَمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: إِذَا فَعَلْتُمْ ذَلِكَ حَصَلَ لَكُمُ الْخَيْرُ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، وَانْدَفَعَ عَنْكُمُ الشَّرُّ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ.

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَهُمْ أَنَّ الْأَصْنَامَ الَّتِي يَعْبُدُونَهَا وَالْأَوْثَانَ، لَا تَضُرُّ وَلَا تَنْفَعُ، وَإِنَّمَا اخْتَلَقْتُمْ أَنْتُمْ لَهَا أَسْمَاءً، سَمَّيْتُمُوهَا آلِهَةً، وَإِنَّمَا هِيَ مَخْلُوقَةٌ مِثْلُكُمْ. هَكَذَا رَوَى الْعَوْفِيُّ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ. وَبِهِ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ.

وَرَوَى الْوَالِبِيُّ ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: وَتَصْنَعُونَ إِفْكًا، أَيْ: تَنْحِتُونَهَا أَصْنَامًا. وَبِهِ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ -فِي رِوَايَةٍ -وَعِكْرِمَةُ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وقَتَادَةُ وَغَيْرُهُمْ، وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ.

وَهِيَ لَا تَمْلِكُ لَكُمْ رِزْقًا، ﴿فَابْتَغُوا عِنْدَ اللَّهِ الرِّزْقَ﴾ وَهَذَا أَبْلَغُ فِي الْحَصْرِ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِيَّاكَ نَعْبُدُ وَإِيَّاكَ نَسْتَعِينُ﴾ [الْفَاتِحَةِ: ٥] ، ﴿رَبِّ ابْنِ لِي عِنْدَكَ بَيْتًا فِي الْجَنَّةِ﴾ [التَّحْرِيمِ: ١١] ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَابْتَغُوا﴾ أَيْ: فَاطْلُبُوا ﴿عِنْدَ اللَّهِ الرِّزْقَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا عِنْدَ غَيْرِهِ، فَإِنَّ غَيْرَهُ لَا يَمْلِكُ شَيْئًا، ﴿وَاعْبُدُوهُ وَاشْكُرُوا لَهُ﴾ أَيْ: كُلُوا مِنْ رِزْقِهِ وَاعْبُدُوهُ وَحْدَهُ ، وَاشْكُرُوا لَهُ عَلَى مَا أَنْعَمَ بِهِ عَلَيْكُمْ، ﴿إِلَيْهِ تُرْجَعُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَيُجَازِي كُلَّ عَامِلٍ بِعَمَلِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنْ تُكَذِّبُوا فَقَدْ كَذَّبَ أُمَمٌ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: فَبَلَّغَكُمْ مَا حَلَّ بِهِمْ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ وَالنَّكَالِ فِي مُخَالَفَةِ الرُّسُلِ، ﴿وَمَا عَلَى الرَّسُولِ إِلا الْبَلاغُ الْمُبِينُ﴾ يَعْنِي: إِنَّمَا عَلَى الرَّسُولِ أَنْ يبلغكم ما أمره الله تعالى بِهِ مِنَ الرِّسَالَةِ، وَاللَّهُ يُضِلُّ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيَهْدِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ، فَاحْرِصُوا لِأَنْفُسِكُمْ أَنْ تَكُونُوا مِنَ السُّعَدَاءِ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَإِنْ تُكَذِّبُوا فَقَدْ كَذَّبَ أُمَمٌ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ﴾ قَالَ: يُعزي نَبِيَّهُ ﷺ. وَهَذَا مِنْ قَتَادَةَ يَقْتَضِي أَنَّهُ قَدِ انْقَطَعَ الْكَلَامُ الْأَوَّلُ، وَاعْتَرَضَ بِهَذَا إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَمَا كَانَ جَوَابَ قَوْمِهِ﴾ . وَهَكَذَا نَصَّ عَلَى ذَلِكَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَيْضًا .

وَالظَّاهِرُ مِنَ السِّيَاقِ أَنَّ كُلَّ هَذَا مِنْ كَلَامِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ الْخَلِيلِ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ [لِقَوْمِهِ] يَحْتَجُّ عَلَيْهِمْ لِإِثْبَاتِ الْمَعَادِ، لِقَوْلِهِ بَعْدَ هَذَا كُلِّهِ: ﴿فَمَا كَانَ جَوَابَ قَوْمِهِ﴾ ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

---

## 29:19-23 — verses 19-23 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Most High says, informing about al-Khalil (the Intimate Friend, i.e., Ibrahim), peace be upon him, that he guided them to affirming the resurrection which they denied, by means of what they witness in themselves: that God created them after they had been nothing mentioned, then they came into existence and became people who hear and see. So the One who originated this is able to bring it back again, for that is easy for Him, simple in His sight.

Then he guided them to reflecting upon the signs witnessed in the horizons, from among the things God created: the heavens and what is in them of luminous stars, both fixed and moving, and the earths and what is in them of level plains and mountains, valleys and open lands and barren wastes, trees and rivers, fruits and seas. All of that points to their being originated in themselves, and to the existence of their Maker, the Doer, the Chooser, who says to a thing "Be," and it is. For this reason He said: {Have they not seen how God originates creation, then repeats it? Indeed that is easy for God}, just as He said: {And He is the One who originates creation, then repeats it, and that is easier for Him} [al-Rum: 27].

Then the Most High said: {Say: Travel through the earth and observe how He originated creation, then God will bring about the final creation}, meaning the Day of Resurrection, {Indeed God has power over all things}. This passage is similar to His saying: {We will show them Our signs in the horizons and in themselves until it becomes clear to them that it is the truth} [Fussilat: 53], and to His saying: {Or were they created from nothing, or are they the creators? Or did they create the heavens and the earth? Rather, they are not certain} [al-Tur: 35-36].

His saying: {He punishes whom He wills and shows mercy to whom He wills} means: He is the Judge, the Disposer, who does what He wills and decrees what He intends. There is no one to overturn His judgment, and He is not asked about what He does, while they are asked. To Him belong creation and command. Whatever He does is just, for He is the Owner who does not wrong so much as the weight of an atom, as has come in the hadith reported by the compilers of the Sunan: "Indeed if God were to punish the people of His heavens and the people of His earth, He would punish them while not being unjust to them." For this reason the Most High said: {He punishes whom He wills and shows mercy to whom He wills, and to Him you will be turned back}, meaning: you will return on the Day of Resurrection.

His saying: {And you cannot escape Him in the earth or in the heaven} means: none among the people of His heavens and His earth can escape Him. Rather He is the Subjugator above His servants, and everything fears Him and is in need of Him, while He is Self-Sufficient, needing nothing beyond Himself.

{And you have no protector or helper besides God. And those who disbelieve in the signs of God and in meeting Him}, meaning: they denied them and disbelieved in the resurrection, {those have despaired of My mercy}, meaning: they have no share in it, {and for them is a painful punishment}, meaning: a painful punishment in this world and the next.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنِ الْخَلِيلِ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، أَنَّهُ أَرْشَدَهُمْ إِلَى إِثْبَاتِ الْمَعَادِ الَّذِي يُنْكِرُونَهُ، بِمَا يُشَاهِدُونَهُ فِي أَنْفُسِهِمْ مِنْ خَلْقِ اللَّهِ إِيَّاهُمْ، بَعْدَ أَنْ لَمْ يَكُونُوا شَيْئًا مَذْكُورًا، ثُمَّ وُجِدُوا وَصَارُوا أُنَاسًا سَامِعِينَ مُبْصِرِينَ، فَالَّذِي بَدَأَ هَذَا قَادِرٌ عَلَى إِعَادَتِهِ؛ فَإِنَّهُ سَهْلٌ عَلَيْهِ يَسِيرٌ لَدَيْهِ.

ثُمَّ أَرْشَدَهُمْ إِلَى الِاعْتِبَارِ بِمَا فِي الْآفَاقِ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ الْمُشَاهَدَةِ مِنْ خَلْقِ اللَّهِ الْأَشْيَاءَ: السَّمَوَاتِ وَمَا فِيهَا مِنَ الْكَوَاكِبِ النَّيِّرَةِ: الثَّوَابِتِ، وَالسَّيَّارَاتِ، وَالْأَرَضِينَ وَمَا فِيهَا مِنْ مِهَادٍ وَجِبَالٍ، وَأَوْدِيَةٍ وبرارٍ وَقِفَارٍ، وَأَشْجَارٍ وَأَنْهَارٍ، وَثِمَارٍ وَبِحَارٍ، كُلُّ ذَلِكَ دَالٌّ عَلَى حُدُوثِهَا فِي أَنْفُسِهَا، وَعَلَى وُجُودِ صَانِعِهَا الْفَاعِلِ الْمُخْتَارِ، الَّذِي يَقُولُ لِلشَّيْءِ: كُنْ، فَيَكُونُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَرَوْا كَيْفَ يُبْدِئُ اللَّهُ الْخَلْقَ ثُمَّ يُعِيدُهُ إِنَّ ذَلِكَ عَلَى اللَّهِ يَسِيرٌ﴾ ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَهُوَ الَّذِي يَبْدَأُ الْخَلْقَ ثُمَّ يُعِيدُهُ وَهُوَ أَهْوَنُ عَلَيْهِ﴾ [الرُّومِ: ٢٧] .

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلْ سِيرُوا فِي الأرْضِ فَانْظُرُوا كَيْفَ بَدَأَ الْخَلْقَ ثُمَّ اللَّهُ يُنْشِئُ النَّشْأَةَ الآخِرَةَ﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ﴾ . وَهَذَا الْمَقَامُ شَبِيهٌ بِقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿سَنُرِيهِمْ آيَاتِنَا فِي الآفَاقِ وَفِي أَنْفُسِهِمْ حَتَّى يَتَبَيَّنَ لَهُمْ أَنَّهُ الْحَقُّ﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ: ٥٣] ، وَكَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَمْ خُلِقُوا مِنْ غَيْرِ شَيْءٍ أَمْ هُمُ الْخَالِقُونَ * أَمْ خَلَقُوا السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضَ بَل لَا يُوقِنُونَ﴾ [الطُّورِ: ٣٥، ٣٦] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يُعَذِّبُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيَرْحَمُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ الْحَاكِمُ الْمُتَصَرِّفُ، الَّذِي يَفْعَلُ مَا يَشَاءُ، وَيَحْكُمُ مَا يُرِيدُ، لَا مُعَقِّبَ لِحُكْمِهِ، وَلَا يُسأل عَمَّا يَفْعَلُ وَهُمْ يُسْأَلُونَ، فَلَهُ الْخَلْقُ وَالْأَمْرُ، مَهْمَا فَعَلَ فَعَدْلٌ؛ لأنه الْمَالِكُ الَّذِي لَا يَظْلِمُ مِثْقَالَ ذَرَّةٍ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ أَهْلُ السُّنَنِ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَوْ عَذَّبَ أَهْلَ سَمَاوَاتِهِ وَأَهْلَ أَرْضِهِ، لَعَذَّبَهُمْ وَهُوَ غَيْرُ ظَالِمٍ لَهُمْ" . وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يُعَذِّبُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيَرْحَمُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَإِلَيْهِ تُقْلَبُونَ﴾ أَيْ: تَرْجِعُونَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا أَنْتُمْ بِمُعْجِزِينَ فِي الأرْضِ وَلا فِي السَّمَاءِ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يُعْجِزُهُ أَحَدٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ سَمَاوَاتِهِ وَأَرْضِهِ، بَلْ هُوَ الْقَاهِرُ فَوْقَ عِبَادِهِ، وَكُلُّ شَيْءٍ خَائِفٌ مِنْهُ، فَقِيرٌ إِلَيْهِ، وَهُوَ الْغَنِيُّ عَمَّا سِوَاهُ.

﴿وَمَا لَكُمْ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ مِنْ وَلِيٍّ وَلا نَصِيرٍ. وَالَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ وَلِقَائِهِ﴾ أَيْ: جَحَدُوهَا وَكَفَرُوا بِالْمَعَادِ، ﴿أُولَئِكَ يَئِسُوا مِنْ رَحْمَتِي﴾ أَيْ: لَا نَصِيبَ لَهُمْ فِيهَا، ﴿وَأُولَئِكَ لَهُمْ عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ﴾ أي: موجع في الدنيا والآخرة.

---

## 29:24-25 — verses 24-25 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty is informing us about the people of Abraham (peace be upon him), regarding their disbelief, their obstinacy, their arrogant persistence, and their pushing away the truth with falsehood. They had no answer after this statement of Abraham, which contained guidance and clear proof, {except that they said, "Kill him or burn him"}, and that was because the proof had been established against them and the argument had been directed at them, so they resorted to using their standing and the strength of their kingdom. {They said, "Build for him a structure and throw him into the blazing fire." So they intended a plot against him, but We made them the lowest ones} [al-Saffat: 97, 98]. That was because they gathered great quantities of firewood over a long period, surrounded it, then kindled the fire in it, and its flame rose up to the horizon of the sky. No fire greater than it had ever been kindled. Then they went to Abraham, bound him, placed him in the sling of a catapult, and hurled him into it. But Allah made it cool and safe for him, and he emerged from it unharmed after having remained in it for some days. For this and things like it, Allah made him a leader (imam) for mankind. For he offered himself to the Most Merciful, his body to the fires, gave up his son willingly as a sacrifice, and devoted his wealth to guests. For this reason, the love of him has united the followers of all religions.

His saying, {So Allah saved him from the fire}, means: Allah delivered him from it by making it cool and safe for him. {Indeed, in that are signs for a people who believe. And he said, "You have only taken idols besides Allah out of mutual love among yourselves in the worldly life"}. He is saying to his people, rebuking and reproaching them for their evil conduct in worshipping idols: you have only taken these so that you might unite in worshipping them in this world, out of friendship and affection between one another in the worldly life. This is according to the reading that renders "mawaddata baynakum" (mutual love among yourselves) in the accusative, making it an object of purpose. But according to the reading with the nominative case, its meaning is: your taking of these only secures for you mutual affection in this world alone. {Then on the Day of Resurrection} this condition will be reversed, and this friendship and affection will turn into hatred and enmity, so {you will disbelieve in one another}, meaning you will deny what was between you, {and curse one another}, meaning the followers will curse those they followed, and those who were followed will curse their followers, {every time a nation enters, it will curse its sister nation} [al-A'raf: 38]. The Almighty also said, {Close friends, that Day, will be enemies to one another, except the righteous} [al-Zukhruf: 67]. And here He said, {Then on the Day of Resurrection you will disbelieve in one another and curse one another, and your refuge will be the Fire, and you will have no helpers}, meaning: your destination and your return, after the terrors of the standing of Resurrection, will be to the Fire, and you will have no helper to help you and no rescuer to save you from the punishment of Allah. This is the condition of the disbelievers, but the believers are otherwise.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from Umm Hani, sister of Ali ibn Abi Talib, who said: The Prophet ﷺ said to me, "Shall I tell you that Allah, Exalted is He, will gather the first and the last on the Day of Resurrection on one level ground, so who knows where the two ends are?" She said: Allah and His Messenger know best. "Then a caller will call out from beneath the Throne: O people of monotheism (tawhid)!" and they will raise their heads eagerly, Abu Asim said: meaning they will lift up their heads, "then he will call again: O people of monotheism! Then he will call a third time: O people of monotheism! Indeed Allah has pardoned you." He said: "Then people, who had clung to one another over worldly grievances, meaning wrongs done to one another, will say... then he will call out: O people of monotheism, let each of you forgive the other, and the reward is upon Allah."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ قَوْمِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ فِي كُفْرِهِمْ وَعِنَادِهِمْ وَمُكَابَرَتِهِمْ، وَدَفْعِهِمُ الْحَقَّ بِالْبَاطِلِ: إِنَّهُ مَا كَانَ لَهُمْ جَوَابٌ بَعْدَ مَقَالَةِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ هَذِهِ الْمُشْتَمِلَةِ عَلَى الْهُدَى وَالْبَيَانِ، ﴿إِلا أَنْ قَالُوا اقْتُلُوهُ أَوْ حَرِّقُوهُ﴾ ، وَذَلِكَ لِأَنَّهُمْ قَامَ عَلَيْهِمُ الْبُرْهَانُ، وَتَوَجَّهَتْ عَلَيْهِمُ الْحُجَّةُ، فَعَدَلُوا إِلَى اسْتِعْمَالِ جَاهِهِمْ وَقُوَّةِ مُلْكِهِمْ، ﴿قَالُوا ابْنُوا لَهُ بُنْيَانًا فَأَلْقُوهُ فِي الْجَحِيمِ. فَأَرَادُوا بِهِ كَيْدًا فَجَعَلْنَاهُمُ الأسْفَلِينَ﴾ [الصَّافَّاتِ: ٩٧، ٩٨] ، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّهُمْ حَشَدوا فِي جَمْعِ أَحِطَابٍ عَظِيمَةٍ مُدَّةً طَوِيلَةً، وحَوّطوا حَوْلَهَا، ثُمَّ أَضْرَمُوا فِيهَا النَّارَ، فَارْتَفَعَ لَهَا لَهَبٌ إِلَى عَنَان السَّمَاءِ: وَلَمْ تُوقَدْ نَارٌ قَطُّ أَعْظَمُ مِنْهَا، ثُمَّ عَمَدُوا إِلَى إِبْرَاهِيمَ فَكَتَّفُوهُ وَأَلْقَوْهُ فِي كفَّة الْمَنْجَنِيقِ، ثُمَّ قَذَفُوا بِهِ فِيهَا، فَجَعَلَهَا اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ بَرْدًا وَسَلَامًا، وَخَرَجَ مِنْهَا سَالِمًا بَعْدَ مَا مَكَثَ فِيهَا أَيَّامًا. وَلِهَذَا وَأَمْثَالِهِ جَعَلَهُ اللَّهُ لِلنَّاسِ إِمَامًا. فَإِنَّهُ بَذَلَ نَفْسَهُ لِلرَّحْمَنِ، وَجَسَدَهُ لِلنِّيرَانِ، وَسَخَا بِوَلَدِهِ لِلْقُرْبَانِ، وَجَعَلَ مَالَهُ لَلضِّيفَانِ، وَلِهَذَا اجْتَمَعَ عَلَى مَحَبَّتِهِ جَمِيعُ أَهْلِ الْأَدْيَانِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَأَنْجَاهُ اللَّهُ مِنَ النَّارِ﴾ أَيْ: سَلَّمه [اللَّهُ] مِنْهَا، بِأَنْ جَعَلَهَا عَلَيْهِ بَرْدًا وَسَلَامًا، ﴿إِنَّ فِي ذَلِكَ لآيَاتٍ لِقَوْمٍ يُؤْمِنُونَ. وَقَالَ إِنَّمَا اتَّخَذْتُمْ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ أَوْثَانًا مَوَدَّةَ بَيْنِكُمْ فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا﴾ يَقُولُ لِقَوْمِهِ مقرِّعا لَهُمْ وَمُوَبَّخًا عَلَى سُوءِ صَنِيعِهِمْ، فِي عِبَادَتِهِمُ الْأَوْثَانَ: إِنَّمَا اتَّخَذْتُمْ هَذِهِ لِتَجْتَمِعُوا عَلَى عِبَادَتِهَا فِي الدُّنْيَا، صَدَاقَةً وَأُلْفَةً مِنْكُمْ، بَعْضُكُمْ لِبَعْضٍ فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا. وَهَذَا عَلَى قِرَاءَةِ مَنْ نَصَبَ ﴿مَوَدَّةَ بَيْنِكُمْ﴾ ، عَلَى أَنَّهُ مَفْعُولٌ لَهُ، وَأَمَّا عَلَى قِرَاءَةِ الرَّفْعِ فَمَعْنَاهُ: إِنَّمَا اتِّخَاذُكُمْ هَذَا يُحَصّل لَكُمُ الْمَوَدَّةَ فِي الدُّنْيَا فَقَطْ ﴿ثُمَّ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ﴾ يَنْعَكِسُ هَذَا الْحَالُ، فَتَبْقَى هَذِهِ الصَّدَاقَةُ وَالْمَوَدَّةُ بَغْضَة وَشَنَآنًا، فَـ ﴿يَكْفُرُ بَعْضُكُمْ بِبَعْضٍ﴾ أَيْ: تَتَجَاحَدُونَ مَا كَانَ بَيْنَكُمْ، ﴿وَيَلْعَنُ بَعْضُكُمْ بَعْضًا﴾ أَيْ: يَلْعَنُ الْأَتْبَاعُ الْمَتْبُوعِينَ، وَالْمَتْبُوعُونَ الْأَتْبَاعَ، ﴿كُلَّمَا دَخَلَتْ أُمَّةٌ لَعَنَتْ أُخْتَهَا﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٣٨] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿الأخِلاءُ يَوْمَئِذٍ بَعْضُهُمْ لِبَعْضٍ عَدُوٌّ إِلا الْمُتَّقِينَ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ: ٦٧] ، وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا ﴿ثُمَّ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ يَكْفُرُ بَعْضُكُمْ بِبَعْضٍ وَيَلْعَنُ بَعْضُكُمْ بَعْضًا وَمَأْوَاكُمُ النَّارُ وَمَا لَكُمْ مِنْ نَاصِرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: وَمَصِيرُكُمْ وَمَرْجِعُكُمْ بَعْدَ عَرَصَاتِ الْقِيَامَةِ إِلَى النَّارِ، وَمَا لَكَمَ مِنْ نَاصِرٍ يَنْصُرُكُمْ، وَلَا مُنْقِذٍ يُنْقِذُكُمْ مِنْ عَذَابِ اللَّهِ. وَهَذَا حَالُ الْكَافِرِينَ، فَأَمَّا الْمُؤْمِنُونَ فَبِخِلَافِ ذَلِكَ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ الأحْمَسي حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَاصِمٍ الثَّقَفِيُّ [حَدَّثَنَا] الرَّبِيعُ بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جَعْدَةَ بْنِ هُبَيْرة الْمَخْزُومِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ جَدِّهِ عَنْ أُمِّ هَانِئٍ -أُخْتِ عَلِيِّ بْنِ أَبِي طَالِبٍ -قَالَتْ: قَالَ لِيَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "أخبرِك أَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى يَجْمَعُ الْأَوَّلِينَ وَالْآخَرِينَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ فِي صَعِيدٍ وَاحِدٍ، فَمَنْ يَدْرِي أَيْنَ الطَّرَفَانِ " ، فَقَالَتِ اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَعْلَمُ. "ثُمَّ يُنَادِي مُنَادٍ مِنْ تَحْتِ الْعَرْشِ: يَا أَهْلَ التَّوْحِيدِ، فَيَشْرَئِبُّونَ" قال أبو عاصم: يرفعون رؤوسهم. "ثُمَّ يُنَادِي: يَا أَهْلَ التَّوْحِيدِ، ثُمَّ يُنَادِي الثَّالِثَةَ: يَا أَهْلَ التَّوْحِيدِ، إِنَّ اللَّهَ قَدْ عَفَا عَنْكُمْ" قَالَ: "فَيَقُولُ النَّاسُ قَدْ تَعَلَّقَ بَعْضُهُمْ بِبَعْضٍ فِي ظُلامات الدُّنْيَا -يَعْنِي: الْمَظَالِمَ -ثُمَّ يُنَادِي: يَا أَهْلَ التَّوْحِيدِ، لِيَعْفُ بَعْضُكُمْ عَنْ بَعْضٍ، وَعَلَى اللَّهِ الثَّوَابُ" .

---

## 29:26-27 — verses 26-27 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing about Ibrahim, that Lut believed in him. It is said that he was Ibrahim's nephew. They say he was Lut son of Haran son of Azar, meaning that none of his people believed in him except him, and Sarah, wife of Ibrahim the Khalil (intimate friend of God).

But it may be asked: how can this verse be reconciled with the hadith reported in the Sahih, that when Ibrahim passed by that tyrant, and the tyrant asked Ibrahim about Sarah, what she was to him, he said, "She is my sister," then he came to her and said to her, "I have told him that you are my sister, so do not contradict me, for there is no believer on the face of the earth other than you and me, so you are my sister in religion." It seems that what is meant by this, and God knows best, is that there was no married couple on the face of the earth upon Islam other than myself and you, for Lut (peace be upon him) had believed in him from among his own people, and emigrated with him to the lands of Sham. Then he was sent, during the lifetime of the Khalil, to the people of Sodom and its region, and what happened regarding their affair was as has already been mentioned and as will come.

Concerning His statement, {And he said, "Indeed I am emigrating to my Lord"}, the pronoun in {and he said} could refer back to Lut, since he is the nearer of the two mentioned, or it could refer back to Ibrahim. Ibn Abbas and al-Dahhak said it refers to him, the one alluded to by His statement {so Lut believed in him}, meaning from among his people.

Then He informed about him that he chose to emigrate from among them, seeking to manifest religion and to be firmly established in it. Hence He said, {Indeed He is the Mighty}, meaning that might belongs to Him, to His messenger, and to those who believe in Him, {the Wise} in His sayings, His actions, and His decrees, both the decreed and the legislative.

Qatadah said: they both emigrated together from Kutha, which is in the Sawad of Kufa, to Sham. He said: it was mentioned to us that the Prophet of God ﷺ said: "There will be emigration after emigration; the people of the earth will gather toward the place of Ibrahim's emigration, and the worst of the earth's inhabitants will remain in the land, until their land spits them out, and the Spirit of God finds them repugnant, and the Fire gathers them together with the apes and swine, spending the night with them when they sleep, resting with them at midday when they rest, and eating whatever falls from them."

Imam Ahmad connected this hadith with a chain, narrating it at length from the hadith of Abdullah ibn Amr ibn al-As, who said: [chain] Abd al-Razzaq told us, Ma'mar informed us, from Qatadah, from Shahr ibn Hawshab, who said: When the pledge of allegiance to Yazid ibn Mu'awiyah came to us, I came to Sham, and I was told of a gathering held by Nawf al-Bikali, so I went to him. Then a man came and set himself apart from the people, wearing a khamisa (a woolen garment), and it turned out to be Abdullah ibn Amr ibn al-As. When Nawf saw him, he stopped speaking. Abdullah said: I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say: "There will be emigration after emigration; people will gather toward the place of Ibrahim's emigration; none will remain in the land except the worst of its inhabitants; their lands will spit them out, the Soul of the Most Merciful will find them repugnant, the Fire will gather them together with the apes and swine, spending the night with them when they sleep, resting with them at midday when they rest, and eating from among them whoever remains behind." He said: And I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say: "People will emerge from my nation from the direction of the east, reciting the Qur'an, but it will not pass beyond their collarbones. Every time a generation of them emerges, it will be cut off, every time a generation of them emerges, it will be cut off," until he counted it more than twenty times, "every time a generation of them emerges, it will be cut off, until the Dajjal emerges from among what remains of them."

Ahmad also narrated it from Abu Dawud and Abd al-Samad, both from Hisham al-Dastuwa'i, from Qatadah, with the same chain.

Abu Dawud also narrated it in his Sunan, in the Book of Jihad, chapter on what has come regarding residing in Sham:

[chain] Ubaydullah ibn Umar told us, Mu'adh ibn Hisham told us, my father told me, from Qatadah, from Shahr ibn Hawshab, from Abdullah ibn Amr, who said: I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say: "There will be emigration after emigration; the best of the earth's inhabitants will be those most attached to the place of Ibrahim's emigration, and the worst of the earth's inhabitants will remain in the land; their land will spit them out, the Soul of the Most Merciful will find them repugnant, and the Fire will gather them together with the apes and swine."

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] Yazid told us, Abu Janab Yahya ibn Abi Hayya informed us, from Shahr ibn Hawshab, who said: I heard Abdullah ibn Umar say: I have seen a time among us when the owner of a dinar or dirham was no more deserving than his Muslim brother, then I have seen us recently now, when the dinar and dirham are dearer to one of us than his Muslim brother. And I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say: "If you follow the tails of cattle, and engage in transactions of 'inah (a form of usurious sale), and abandon jihad in the way of God, God will impose upon you a humiliation around your necks, which will not be removed from you until you return to what you were upon, and repent to God, the Mighty and Majestic." And I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say: "There will surely be emigration after emigration to the place of emigration of your father Ibrahim, until none remain in the lands except the worst of their inhabitants; their lands will spit them out, the Spirit of the Most Merciful will find them repugnant, and the Fire will gather them together with the apes and swine, resting at midday where they rest, spending the night where they spend the night, and whatever falls from them belongs to it." And I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say: "A people will emerge from my nation who do evil deeds, reciting the Qur'an but it will not pass beyond their throats." Yazid said: I only know that he said, "one of you will consider his own knowledge insignificant compared to their knowledge. They will kill the people of Islam. So when they emerge, kill them, then when they emerge, kill them, then when they emerge, kill them. Glad tidings to whoever kills them, and glad tidings to whoever is killed by them. Every time a generation of them arises, God will cut it off." The Messenger of God ﷺ repeated that twenty times or more, while I was listening.

Al-Hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bayhaqi said: [chain] Abu al-Husayn ibn al-Fadl informed us, Abdullah ibn Ja'far informed us, Ya'qub ibn Sufyan told us, Abu al-Nadr Ishaq ibn Yazid and Hisham ibn Ammar al-Dimashqiyyan told us, they said: Yahya ibn Hamza told us, al-Awza'i told us, from Nafi', and Abu al-Nadr said, from one who narrated to him, from Nafi', from Abdullah ibn Umar: that the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "The people of the earth will emigrate, emigration after emigration, to the place of Ibrahim's emigration, until none remain except the worst of its inhabitants; the lands will spit them out and the Soul of the Most Merciful will find them repugnant, and the Fire will gather them together with the apes and swine, spending the night with them wherever they spend the night, resting with them wherever they rest, having for itself whatever falls from them."

This is gharib (singular) from the hadith of Nafi'. It appears that al-Awza'i narrated it from a weak shaykh of his, and God knows best. His narration of it from the hadith of Abdullah ibn Amr ibn al-As is closer to being reliably preserved.

Concerning His statement, {And We granted him Ishaq and Ya'qub}, this is like His statement, the Almighty: {So when he had withdrawn from them and what they worshipped besides God, We granted him Ishaq and Ya'qub, and each We made a prophet} [Maryam: 49], meaning that when he separated from his people, God brought comfort to his eye by the existence of a righteous, prophetic child, and a righteous child was born to him during his father's lifetime. Likewise God said, {And We granted him Ishaq and Ya'qub, as an additional gift} [al-Anbiya: 72], meaning as an increase, just as He said, {So We gave her glad tidings of Ishaq, and after Ishaq, of Ya'qub}, meaning that a child would be born to this child during your two lifetimes, by which your eyes would find comfort. That Ya'qub was the son of Ishaq is stated explicitly in the Qur'an, and the Prophetic Sunnah confirms it. God said: {Or were you witnesses when death approached Ya'qub, when he said to his sons, "What will you worship after me?" They said, "We will worship your God and the God of your fathers, Ibrahim, Isma'il, and Ishaq, one God, and to Him we submit"} [al-Baqarah: 133]. And in the two Sahihs: "Indeed the noble one, son of the noble one, son of the noble one, son of the noble one, Yusuf son of Ya'qub son of Ishaq son of Ibrahim."

As for what al-Awfi narrated from Ibn Abbas concerning His statement, {And We granted him Ishaq and Ya'qub, as an additional gift}, that he said, "They are both sons of Ibrahim," its meaning is that the child of one's child holds the status of one's own child, for this is a matter that would hardly be hidden from anyone below the rank of Ibn Abbas.

Concerning His statement, {And We placed in his descendants prophethood and the Book}, this is a magnificent and noble bestowal, along with God's taking him as an intimate friend (Khalil) and making him an imam for people, that He placed prophethood and the Book among his descendants. No prophet was found after Ibrahim (peace be upon him) except that he was from his lineage. All the prophets of the Children of Israel were from the lineage of Ya'qub son of Ishaq son of Ibrahim, until the last of them was Isa son of Maryam, who arose among his people bringing glad tidings of the Arab Prophet, of Quraysh, of Hashim, the Seal of the Messengers absolutely, and the master of the children of Adam in this world and the next, whom God chose from the very core of the pure Arabs, from the lineage of Isma'il son of Ibrahim (peace be upon them). No prophet was found from the lineage of Isma'il other than him, upon him be the most excellent prayers and peace from God the Almighty.

Concerning His statement, {And We gave him his reward in this world, and indeed in the Hereafter he is among the righteous}, meaning that God combined for him the happiness of this world joined to the happiness of the Hereafter. So he had in this world abundant and pleasant provision, a spacious dwelling, sweet water sources, a good and righteous wife, beautiful praise, and a good remembrance, so that everyone loved him and held him in loyalty, as Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, Qatadah, and others said, along with his fulfillment of obedience to God in every respect, as the Almighty said: {And Ibrahim, who fulfilled} [al-Najm: 37], meaning he carried out everything he was commanded, and perfected obedience to his Lord. Hence the Almighty said, {And We gave him his reward in this world, and indeed in the Hereafter he is among the righteous}, just as the Almighty said: {Indeed, Ibrahim was a nation, devoutly obedient to God, upright, and he was not of those who associate partners with God. Grateful for His favors; He chose him and guided him to a straight path. And We gave him good in this world, and indeed in the Hereafter he is among the righteous} [al-Nahl: 120-121].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ: أَنَّهُ آمَنُ لَهُ لُوطٌ، يُقَالُ: إِنَّهُ ابْنُ أَخِي إِبْرَاهِيمَ، يَقُولُونَ هُوَ: لُوطُ بْنُ هَارَانَ بْنِ آزَرَ، يَعْنِي: وَلَمْ يُؤْمِنْ بِهِ مِنْ قَوْمِهِ سِوَاهُ، وَسَارَّةُ امْرَأَةُ [إِبْرَاهِيمَ] الْخَلِيلِ. لَكِنْ يُقَالُ: كَيْفَ الْجَمْعُ بَيْنَ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ، وَبَيْنَ الْحَدِيثِ الْوَارِدِ فِي الصَّحِيحِ : أَنَّ إِبْرَاهِيمَ حِينَ مَرّ عَلَى ذَلِكَ الْجَبَّارِ، فَسَأَلَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ عَنْ سَارَّةَ: مَا هِيَ مِنْهُ؟ فَقَالَ: [هِيَ] أُخْتِي، ثُمَّ جَاءَ إِلَيْهَا فَقَالَ لَهَا: إِنِّي قَدْ قُلْتُ لَهُ: "إِنَّكِ: أُخْتِي"، فَلَا تُكَذِّبِينِي، فَإِنَّهُ لَيْسَ عَلَى وَجْهِ الْأَرْضِ [أَحَدٌ] مُؤْمِنٌ غَيْرُكِ وَغَيْرِي ، فَأَنْتِ أُخْتِي فِي الدِّينِ. وَكَأَنَّ الْمُرَادَ مِنْ هَذَا -والله أعلم -أنه ليس على وجه الْأَرْضِ زَوْجَانِ عَلَى الْإِسْلَامِ غَيْرِي وَغَيْرُكِ، فَإِنَّ لُوطًا عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، آمَنَ بِهِ مِنْ قَوْمِهِ، وَهَاجَرَ مَعَهُ إِلَى بِلَادِ الشَّامِ، ثُمَّ أرسِل فِي حَيَاةِ الْخَلِيلِ إِلَى أَهْلِ "سَدوم" وَإِقْلِيمِهَا، وَكَانَ مِنْ أَمْرِهِمْ مَا تَقَدَّمَ وَمَا سَيَأْتِي.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَقَالَ إِنِّي مُهَاجِرٌ إِلَى رَبِّي﴾ يَحْتَمِلُ عَوْدَ الضَّمِيرِ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَقَالَ﴾ ، عَلَى لُوطٍ، لِأَنَّهُ أَقْرَبُ الْمَذْكُورَيْنِ، وَيَحْتَمِلُ عُودَهُ إِلَى إِبْرَاهِيمَ -قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَالضَّحَاكُ: وَهُوَ الْمُكَنَّى عَنْهُ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَآمَنَ لَهُ لُوطٌ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ قَوْمِهِ.

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ عَنْهُ بِأَنَّهُ اخْتَارَ الْمُهَاجَرَةَ مِنْ بَيْنِ أَظْهُرِهِمُ، ابْتِغَاءَ إِظْهَارِ الدِّينِ وَالتَّمَكُّنِ مِنْ ذَلِكَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿إِنَّهُ هُوَ الْعَزِيزُ﴾ أَيْ: لَهُ الْعِزَّةُ وَلِرَسُولِهِ وَلِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ بِهِ، ﴿الْحَكِيمُ﴾ فِي أَقْوَالِهِ وَأَفْعَالِهِ وَأَحْكَامِهِ الْقَدَرِيَّةِ وَالشَّرْعِيَّةِ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: هَاجَرَا جَمِيعًا مِنْ "كَوْثَى"، وَهِيَ مِنْ سَوَادِ الْكُوفَةِ إِلَى الشَّامِ. قَالَ: وذُكر لَنَا أَنَّ نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّهَا سَتَكُونُ هِجْرَةٌ بَعْدَ هِجْرَةٍ، يَنْحَازُ أَهْلُ الْأَرْضِ إِلَى مُهَاجَر إِبْرَاهِيمَ، وَيَبْقَى فِي الْأَرْضِ شرار أهلها، حتى تلفظهم أرضهم وتقذرُهم رُوحُ اللَّهِ، وَتَحْشُرهُمُ النَّارُ مَعَ الْقِرَدَةِ وَالْخَنَازِيرِ، تَبِيتُ مَعَهُمْ إِذَا بَاتُوا، وتَقِيل مَعَهُمْ إِذَا قَالُوا، وَتَأْكُلُ مَا سَقَطَ مِنْهُمْ".

وَقَدْ أَسْنَدَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ هَذَا الْحَدِيثَ، فَرَوَاهُ مُطَوَّلًا مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ الْعَاصِ، قَالَ : حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، أَخْبَرَنَا مَعْمَر، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنْ شَهْر بْنِ حَوْشَب قَالَ: لَمَّا جَاءَتْنَا بَيْعَةُ يَزِيدَ بْنِ مُعَاوِيَةَ، قَدِمْتُ الشَّامَ فَأُخْبِرْتُ بِمَقَامٍ يَقُومُهُ نَوْفٌ البِكَالي، فَجِئْتُهُ؛ إِذْ جَاءَ رَجُلٌ، فانتبذَ النَّاسَ وَعَلَيْهِ خَمِيصة، وَإِذَا هُوَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عَمْرِو بْنِ الْعَاصِ. فَلَمَّا رَآهُ نَوْفٌ أَمْسَكَ عَنِ الْحَدِيثِ، فَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "إِنَّهَا سَتَكُونُ هِجْرَةٌ بَعْدَ هِجْرَةٍ، فَيَنْحَازُ النَّاسُ إِلَى مُهَاجرَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، لَا يَبْقَى فِي الْأَرْضِ إِلَّا شَرَارُ أَهْلِهَا، فَتَلْفِظُهُمْ أَرَضُوهُمْ، تقْذَرهم نفسُ الرَّحْمَنِ، تَحْشُرُهُمُ النَّارُ مَعَ الْقِرَدَةِ وَالْخَنَازِيرِ فَتَبِيتُ مَعَهُمْ إِذَا بَاتُوا، وتَقِيل مَعَهُمْ إِذَا قَالُوا، وَتَأْكُلُ مِنْهُمْ مَنْ تَخَلَّف". قَالَ: وَسَمِعَتْ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "سَيَخْرُجُ أُنَاسٌ مِنْ أُمَّتِي من قبل المشرق، يقرؤون الْقُرْآنَ لَا يُجَاوِزُ تَرَاقِيهم، كُلَّمَا خَرَجَ مِنْهُمْ قَرْنٌ قُطع، كُلَّمَا خَرَجَ مِنْهُمْ قَرْنٌ قُطِعَ" حَتَّى عَدّها زِيَادَةً عَلَى عِشْرِينَ مَرَّةً "كُلَّمَا خَرَجَ مِنْهُمْ قَرْنٌ قُطِعَ، حَتَّى يَخْرُجَ الدَّجَّالُ فِي بَقِيَّتِهِمْ" .

وَرَوَاهُ أَحْمَدُ عَنْ أَبِي دَاوُدَ، وَعَبْدِ الصَّمَدِ، كِلَاهُمَا عَنْ هِشَامٍ الدَّسْتُوائي، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، بِهِ 

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ فِي سُنَنِهِ، فَقَالَ فِي كِتَابِ الْجِهَادِ، بَابُ مَا جَاءَ فِي سُكْنَى الشَّامِ:

حَدَّثَنَا عُبَيْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عُمَرَ، حَدَّثَنَا مُعَاذُ بْنُ هِشَامٍ، حَدَّثَنِي [أَبِي] ، عَنْ قتادة، عن شهر بن حَوْشَبٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم يَقُولُ: "سَتَكُونُ هِجْرَةٌ بَعْدَ هِجْرَةٍ، فَخِيَارُ أَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ أَلْزَمُهُمْ مُهاجَر إِبْرَاهِيمَ، وَيَبْقَى فِي الْأَرْضِ شِرَارُ أَهْلِهَا تَلْفِظُهُمْ أَرْضُهُمْ وتَقْذرهم نَفْسُ الرَّحْمَنِ، وَتَحْشُرُهُمُ النَّارُ مَعَ الْقِرَدَةِ وَالْخَنَازِيرِ" .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ، أَخْبَرَنَا أَبُو جَنَاب يَحْيَى بْنُ أَبِي حيَّة، عَنْ شَهْرُ بْنُ حَوْشَبٍ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ عُمَر يَقُولُ لَقَدْ رأيتُنا وَمَا صَاحِبُ الدِّينَارِ وَالدِّرْهَمِ بِأَحَقِّ مِنْ أَخِيهِ الْمُسْلِمِ، ثُمَّ لَقَدْ رَأَيْتُنَا بآخِرَة الْآنَ، وَالدِّينَارُ وَالدِّرْهَمُ أَحَبُّ إِلَى أَحَدِنَا مِنْ أَخِيهِ الْمُسْلِمِ، وَلَقَدْ سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "لَئِنْ أَنْتُمُ اتَّبَعْتُمْ أَذْنَابَ الْبَقَرِ، وَتَبَايَعْتُمْ بِالْعِينَةِ، وَتَرَكْتُمُ الْجِهَادَ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، لَيُلْزِمَنَّكُمُ اللَّهُ مذلَّة فِي أَعْنَاقِكُمْ، ثُمَّ لَا تُنْزَعُ مِنْكُمْ حَتَّى تَرْجِعُوا إِلَى مَا كُنْتُمْ عَلَيْهِ، وَتَتُوبُوا إِلَى اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ". وَسَمِعَتْ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "لَتَكُونَنَّ هِجْرَةٌ بَعْدَ هِجْرَةٍ إِلَى مُهاجر أَبِيكُمْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ حَتَّى لَا يَبْقَى فِي الْأَرَضِينَ إِلَّا شِرَارُ أَهْلِهَا وَتَلْفِظُهُمْ أَرَضُوهُمْ، وتقذرهم روح الرحمن، وتحشرهم النار مع القردة وَالْخَنَازِيرِ، تَقِيلُ حَيْثُ يَقِيلُونَ ، وَتَبِيتُ حَيْثُ يَبِيتُونَ، وَمَا سَقَطَ مِنْهُمْ فَلَهَا". وَلَقَدْ سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "يَخْرُجُ من أمتي قوم يسيئون الأعمال، يقرؤون الْقُرْآنَ لَا يُجَاوِزُ حَنَاجِرَهُمْ -قَالَ يَزِيدُ: لَا أَعْلَمُهُ إِلَّا قَالَ -يَحْقِرُ أَحَدُكُمْ عِلْمَهُ مَعَ عِلْمِهِمْ، يَقْتُلُونَ أَهْلَ الْإِسْلَامِ، فَإِذَا خَرَجُوا فَاقْتُلُوهُمْ، ثُمَّ إِذَا خَرَجُوا فَاقْتُلُوهُمْ، ثُمَّ إِذَا خَرَجُوا فَاقْتُلُوهُمْ، فَطُوبَى لِمَنْ قَتَلَهُمْ، وَطُوبَى لِمَنْ قَتَلُوهُ. كُلَّمَا طَلَعَ مِنْهُمْ قَرْنٌ قَطعَه اللَّهُ". فَرَدَّدَ ذَلِكَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ عِشْرِينَ مَرَّةً، أَوْ أَكْثَرَ، وَأَنَا أَسْمَعُ .

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَيْهَقِيُّ: أَخْبَرَنَا أَبُو الحُسَيْن بْنُ الْفَضْلٍ، أَخْبَرَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا يَعْقُوبُ بْنُ سُفْيَانَ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو النَّضْرِ إِسْحَاقُ بْنُ يَزِيدَ وَهِشَامُ بْنُ عَمَّارٍ الدِّمَشْقِيَّانِ قَالَا حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ حَمْزَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَوْزَاعِيُّ، عَنْ نَافِعٍ -وَقَالَ أَبُو النَّضْرِ، عَمَّنْ حدَّثه، عَنْ نَافِعٍ -عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صلى الله عليه وسلم قَالَ: "سَيُهَاجِرُ أَهْلُ الْأَرْضِ هِجْرَةً بَعْدَ هِجْرَةٍ، إِلَى مهاجَر إِبْرَاهِيمَ، حَتَّى لَا يَبْقَى إِلَّا شَرَارُ أَهْلِهَا، تَلْفِظُهُمُ الْأَرَضُونَ وَتَقْذَرُهُمْ رُوحُ الرَّحْمَنِ، وتحشرهم النار مع القردة والخنازير، تبيت معهم حَيْثُ بَاتُوا، وَتَقِيلُ مَعَهُمْ حَيْثُ قَالُوا، لَهَا مَا سَقَطَ مِنْهُمْ".

غَرِيبٌ مِنْ حَدِيثِ نَافِعٍ. وَالظَّاهِرُ أَنَّ الْأَوْزَاعِيَّ قَدْ رَوَاهُ عَنْ شَيْخٍ لَهُ مِنَ الضُّعَفَاءِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ. وَرِوَايَتُهُ مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ الْعَاصِ أَقْرَبُ إِلَى الْحِفْظِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَوَهَبْنَا لَهُ إِسْحَاقَ وَيَعْقُوبَ﴾ ، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَلَمَّا اعْتَزَلَهُمْ وَمَا يَعْبُدُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ وَهَبْنَا لَهُ إِسْحَاقَ وَيَعْقُوبَ وَكُلا جَعَلْنَا نَبِيًّا﴾ [مَرْيَمَ: ٤٩] أَيْ: إِنَّهُ لَمَّا فَارَقَ قومَه أَقَرَّ اللَّهُ عَيْنَهُ بِوُجُودِ وَلَدٍ صَالِحٍ نَبِيٍّ [وَوُلِدَ لَهُ وَلَدٌ صَالِحٌ] فِي حَيَاةِ جَدِّهِ. وَكَذَلِكَ قَالَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَوَهَبْنَا لَهُ إِسْحَاقَ وَيَعْقُوبَ نَافِلَةً﴾ [الأنبياء: ٧٢] أَيْ: زِيَادَةً، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿فَبَشَّرْنَاهَا بِإِسْحَاقَ وَمِنْ وَرَاءِ إِسْحَاقَ يَعْقُوبَ﴾ أَيْ: ويولَد لِهَذَا الْوَلَدِ وَلَدٌ فِي حَيَاتِكُمَا، تَقَرُّ بِهِ أَعْيُنُكُمَا. وَكَوْنُ يَعْقُوبَ وَلَدٌ لِإِسْحَاقَ نَصَّ عَلَيْهِ الْقُرْآنُ، وَثَبَتَتْ بِهِ السُّنَّةُ النَّبَوِيَّةُ، قَالَ اللَّهُ: ﴿أَمْ كُنْتُمْ شُهَدَاءَ إِذْ حَضَرَ يَعْقُوبَ الْمَوْتُ إِذْ قَالَ لِبَنِيهِ مَا تَعْبُدُونَ مِنْ بَعْدِي قَالُوا نَعْبُدُ إِلَهَكَ وَإِلَهَ آبَائِكَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ وَإِسْمَاعِيلَ وَإِسْحَاقَ إِلَهًا وَاحِدًا وَنَحْنُ لَهُ مُسْلِمُونَ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ١٣٣] ، وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ: "إِنَّ الْكَرِيمَ ابنَ الْكَرِيمِ ابنِ الْكَرِيمِ ابْنِ الْكَرِيمِ يوسفُ بنَ يعقوبَ بْنِ إسحاقَ بْنِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ" .

فَأَمَّا مَا رَوَاهُ الْعَوْفِيُّ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَوَهَبْنَا لَهُ إِسْحَاقَ وَيَعْقُوبَ [نَافِلَةً] ﴾ ، قَالَ: "هُمَا وَلَدَا إِبْرَاهِيمَ". فَمَعْنَاهُ: أَنَّ وَلَدَ الْوَلَدِ بِمَنْزِلَةِ الْوَلَدِ؛ فَإِنَّ هَذَا أَمْرٌ لَا يَكَادُ يَخْفَى عَلَى مَنْ هُوَ دُونَ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَجَعَلْنَا فِي ذُرِّيَّتِهِ النُّبُوَّةَ وَالْكِتَابَ﴾ ، هَذِهِ خِلْعَة سَنية عَظِيمَةٌ، مَعَ اتِّخَاذِ اللَّهِ إِيَّاهُ خَلِيلًا وَجَعْلِهِ لِلنَّاسِ إِمَامًا، أَنْ جَعَلَ فِي ذُرِّيَّتِهِ النُّبُوَّةَ وَالْكِتَابَ، فَلَمْ يُوجَدْ نَبِيٌّ بَعْدَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، إِلَّا وَهُوَ مِنْ سُلَالَتِهِ، فَجَمِيعُ أَنْبِيَاءِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ مِنْ سُلالة يَعْقُوبَ بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ بْنِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، حَتَّى كَانَ آخِرُهُمْ عِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ، فَقَامَ فِي مَلَئِهِمْ مُبَشِّرًا بِالنَّبِيِّ الْعَرَبِيِّ الْقُرَشِيِّ الْهَاشِمِيِّ، خَاتَمِ الرُّسُلِ عَلَى الْإِطْلَاقِ، وَسَيِّدِ وَلَدِ آدَمَ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، الَّذِي اصْطَفَاهُ اللَّهُ مِنْ صَمِيمِ الْعَرَبِ العَرْباء، مِنْ سُلَالَةِ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَلَيْهِمُ السَّلَامُ: وَلَمْ يُوجَدْ نَبِيٌّ مِنْ سُلَالَةِ إِسْمَاعِيلَ سِوَاهُ، عَلَيْهِ أَفْضَلُ الصَّلَاةِ وَالسَّلَامِ [مِنَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى] .

* *
