وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَآتَيْنَاهُ أَجْرَهُ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَإِنَّهُ فِي الآخِرَةِ لَمِنَ الصَّالِحِينَ﴾ أَيْ: جَمَعَ اللَّهُ لَهُ بَيْنَ سَعَادَةِ الدُّنْيَا الْمَوْصُولَةِ بِسَعَادَةِ الْآخِرَةِ، فَكَانَ لَهُ فِي الدُّنْيَا الرِّزْقُ الْوَاسِعُ الهنيَّ وَالْمَنْزِلُ الرَّحْب، وَالْمَوْرِدُ الْعَذْبُ، وَالزَّوْجَةُ الْحَسَنَةُ الصَّالِحَةُ، وَالثَّنَاءُ الْجَمِيلُ، وَالذِّكْرُ الْحَسَنُ، فَكُلُّ أَحَدٍ يُحِبُّهُ وَيَتَوَلَّاهُ، كَمَا قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ وَمُجَاهِدٌ وقَتَادَةُ وَغَيْرُهُمْ، مَعَ الْقِيَامِ بِطَاعَةِ اللَّهِ مِنْ جَمِيعِ الْوُجُوهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِبْرَاهِيمَ الَّذِي وَفَّى﴾ [النَّجْمِ: ٣٧] ، أَيْ: قَامَ بِجَمِيعِ مَا أُمِرَ بِهِ، وَكَمَّلَ طَاعَةَ رَبِّهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَآتَيْنَاهُ أَجْرَهُ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَإِنَّهُ فِي الآخِرَةِ لَمِنَ الصَّالِحِينَ﴾ ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ إِبْرَاهِيمَ كَانَ أُمَّةً قَانِتًا لِلَّهِ حَنِيفًا وَلَمْ يَكُ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ. شَاكِرًا لأنْعُمِهِ اجْتَبَاهُ وَهَدَاهُ إِلَى صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ. وَآتَيْنَاهُ فِي الدُّنْيَا حَسَنَةً وَإِنَّهُ فِي الآخِرَةِ لَمِنَ الصَّالِحِينَ﴾ [النحل: ١٢٠-١٢١] .

---

## 29:28-30 — verses 28-30 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing about His Prophet Lot (peace be upon him), that he denounced his people for their evil conduct and the shameful acts they used to commit in approaching males from among the worlds, an act in which no one among the sons of Adam had preceded them. Along with this they disbelieved in Allah, denied His messenger, opposed him, and cut off the road, meaning they would lie in wait along people's paths, killing them and taking their wealth. {And you commit in your gathering place the reprehensible act}, meaning they did what was unbecoming of speech and deeds in their assemblies where they gathered, with none of them denouncing any of that from another. Some said they used to have intercourse with one another in public gatherings, this was said by Mujahid. Others said they used to break wind and laugh at it, this was said by A'isha, may Allah be pleased with her, and by al-Qasim. Others said they used to make rams butt each other and set roosters to fight, and all of that used to issue from them, and they were worse than that.

Imam Ahmad said: Hammad ibn Usama narrated to us, Hatim ibn Abi Saghira informed me, Simak ibn Harb narrated to us, from Abu Salih, the freed slave of Umm Hani, from Umm Hani who said: I asked the Messenger of Allah ﷺ about His saying, Mighty and Majestic is He: {And you commit in your gathering place the reprehensible act}. He said: "They would pelt travelers on the road with pebbles and mock them, and that is the reprehensible act which they used to commit."

Al-Tirmidhi, Ibn Jarir, and Ibn Abi Hatim narrated it from the hadith of Abu Usama Hammad ibn Usama, from Abu Yunus al-Qushayri, Hatim ibn Abi Saghira, with the same chain. Then al-Tirmidhi said: This is a hasan (good) hadith, we do not know it except from the hadith of Hatim ibn Abi Saghira from Simak.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: al-Hasan ibn Arafa narrated to us, Muhammad ibn Kathir narrated to us, from Amr ibn Qays, from al-Hakam, from Mujahid regarding {And you commit in your gathering place the reprehensible act}: he said, it means whistling, playing with pigeons and the sling for throwing pebbles, asking [improper] questions in gatherings, and undoing the buttons of the qaba (cloak).

Concerning His saying, {But the only answer of his people was that they said, "Bring us the punishment of Allah, if you should be of the truthful"}, this stemmed from their disbelief, their mockery, and their obstinacy. It was because of this that the Prophet of Allah sought help against them, saying: {My Lord, grant me victory over the people who cause corruption}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ نَبِيِّهِ لُوطٍ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، إِنَّهُ أَنْكَرَ عَلَى قَوْمِهِ سُوء صَنِيعِهِمْ، وَمَا كَانُوا يَفْعَلُونَهُ مِنْ قَبِيحِ الْأَعْمَالِ، فِي إِتْيَانِهِمُ الذُّكْرَانَ مِنَ الْعَالَمِينَ، وَلَمْ يَسْبِقْهُمْ إِلَى هَذِهِ الْفِعْلَةِ أَحَدٌ مِنْ بَنِي آدَمَ قَبْلَهُمْ. وَكَانُوا مَعَ هَذَا يَكْفُرُونَ بِاللَّهِ، وَيُكَذِّبُونَ رَسُولَهُ وَيُخَالِفُونَهُ وَيَقْطَعُونَ السَّبِيلَ، أَيْ: يَقِفُونَ فِي طَرِيقِ النَّاسِ يَقْتُلُونَهُمْ وَيَأْخُذُونَ أَمْوَالَهُمْ، ﴿وَتَأْتُونَ فِي نَادِيكُمُ الْمُنْكَرَ﴾ أَيْ: يَفْعَلُونَ مَا لَا يَلِيقُ مِنَ الْأَقْوَالِ وَالْأَفْعَالِ فِي مَجَالِسِهِمُ الَّتِي يَجْتَمِعُونَ فِيهَا، لَا يُنْكِرُ بَعْضُهُمْ عَلَى بَعْضٍ شَيْئًا مِنْ ذَلِكَ، فَمِنْ قَائِلٍ: كَانُوا يَأْتُونَ بَعْضَهُمْ بَعْضًا فِي الْمَلَأِ قَالَهُ مُجَاهِدٌ. وَمِنْ قَائِلٍ: كَانُوا يَتَضَارَطُونَ وَيَتَضَاحَكُونَ؛ قَالَتْهُ عَائِشَةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، وَالْقَاسِمُ. وَمِنْ قَائِلٍ: كَانُوا يُنَاطِحُونَ بَيْنَ الْكِبَاشِ، وَيُنَاقِرُونَ بَيْنَ الدُّيُوكِ، وَكُلُّ ذَلِكَ كَانَ يَصْدُرُ عَنْهُمْ، وَكَانُوا شَرًّا مِنْ ذَلِكَ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ أُسَامَةَ، أَخْبَرَنِي حَاتِمُ بْنُ أَبِي صَغِيرَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا سِمَاك بْنُ حَرْبٍ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ -مَوْلَى أُمِّ هَانِئٍ -عَنْ أُمِّ هَانِئٍ قَالَتْ: سَأَلْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ، عَنْ قَوْلِهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿وَتَأْتُونَ فِي نَادِيكُمُ الْمُنْكَرَ﴾ ، قَالَ: "يَحْذِفُونَ أَهْلَ الطَّرِيقِ، وَيَسْخَرُونَ مِنْهُمْ، وَذَلِكَ الْمُنْكَرُ الَّذِي كَانُوا يَأْتُونَهُ".

وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ، وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي أُسَامَةَ حَمَّادِ بْنِ أُسَامَةَ عَنْ أَبِي يُونُسَ القُشَيري، حَاتِمِ بْنِ أَبِي صَغِيرة بِهِ . ثُمَّ قَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: هَذَا حَدِيثٌ حَسَنٌ لَا نَعْرِفُهُ إِلَّا مِنْ حَدِيثِ حَاتِمِ بْنِ أَبِي صَغِيرَةَ عَنْ سِمَاك.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ عَرَفَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَثِيرٍ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ قَيْسٍ، عَنِ الْحَكَمِ ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿وَتَأْتُونَ فِي نَادِيكُمُ الْمُنْكَرَ﴾ قَالَ: الصَّفِيرُ، وَلَعِبُ الْحَمَّامِ والجُلاهق، وَالسُّؤَالُ فِي الْمَجْلِسِ، وَحَلُّ أَزْرَارِ الْقِبَاءِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَمَا كَانَ جَوَابَ قَوْمِهِ إِلا أَنْ قَالُوا ائْتِنَا بِعَذَابِ اللَّهِ إِنْ كُنْتَ مِنَ الصَّادِقِينَ﴾ ، وَهَذَا مِنْ كُفْرِهِمْ وَاسْتِهْزَائِهِمْ وَعِنَادِهِمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا اسْتَنْصَرَ عَلَيْهِمْ نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ فَقَالَ: ﴿رَبِّ انْصُرْنِي عَلَى الْقَوْمِ الْمُفْسِدِينَ﴾ .

---

## 29:31-35 — verses 31-35 (shared commentary)

### Translation

When Lot (peace be upon him) sought God's aid against his people, God sent angels for his support, and they passed by Abraham (peace be upon him) in the guise of guests. He brought them what befits a guest, but when he saw that they had no inclination toward the food, he found them strange and felt a fear of them. They then set about putting him at ease and giving him glad tidings of a righteous son from his wife Sarah, who was present, and she was amazed at that, as has already been explained in Surah Hud and Surah al-Hijr.

When they brought Abraham the glad tidings and informed him that they had been sent to destroy the people of Lot, he began to plead on their behalf, hoping that they might be given respite, hoping that God might guide them. When they said, {We are indeed going to destroy the people of this town}, {he said, Indeed, Lot is in it. They said, We know best who is in it. We will surely save him and his family, except his wife; she was among those who remained behind}, that is, among those who were destroyed, because she used to support them in their disbelief, their transgression, and their treachery against him.

Then they journeyed on from him and came to Lot in the form of handsome young men. When he saw them thus, {he was distressed on their account and felt his strength unequal to protecting them}, that is, he became deeply concerned about their situation. If he sheltered them as guests, he feared for them from his people, and if he did not shelter them, he feared for them from his people as well, and he did not yet know what would happen to them within the present hour.

{They said, Do not fear and do not grieve. We shall save you and your family, except your wife; she was among those who remained behind. We are about to bring down upon the people of this town a punishment from heaven because of the wickedness they used to commit.} This was because Gabriel (peace be upon him) uprooted their towns from the depths of the earth, then lifted them up to the height of the sky, then overturned them upon them. And God sent down upon them stones of baked clay, layered one upon another, {marked by your Lord, and it is not far from the wrongdoers}. God made in their place a foul, stinking lake, and made them a lesson until the Day of Mutual Calling, and they are among the people who will suffer the most severe punishment on the Day of Resurrection.

Therefore the Exalted said: {And We have indeed left of it a clear sign}, that is, an evident one, {for a people who reason}, just as He said: {And indeed you pass by them in the morning, and by night. Do you not then reason?} [al-Saffat: 137-138].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لِمَا اسْتَنْصَرَ لُوطٌ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، اللَّهَ عَلَيْهِمْ، بَعَثَ اللَّهُ لِنُصْرَتِهِ مَلَائِكَةً فَمَرُّوا عَلَى إِبْرَاهِيمَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فِي هَيْئَةِ أَضْيَافٍ، فَجَاءَهُمْ بِمَا يَنْبَغِي لِلضَّيْفِ، فَلَمَّا رَأَى أَنَّهُ لَا همَّة لَهُمْ إِلَى الطَّعَامِ نَكِرَهم، وَأَوْجَسَ مِنْهُمْ خِيفَةً، فَشَرَعُوا يُؤَانِسُونَهُ وَيُبَشِّرُونَهُ بِوُجُودِ وَلَدٍ صَالِحٍ مِنَ امْرَأَتِهِ سَارَّةَ -وَكَانَتْ حَاضِرَةً -فَتَعَجَّبَتْ مِنْ ذَلِكَ، كَمَا تَقَدَّمَ بَيَانُهُ فِي سُورَةِ "هُودٍ" وَ"الْحِجْرِ". فَلَمَّا جَاءَتْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ بِالْبُشْرَى، وَأَخْبَرُوهُ بِأَنَّهُمْ أُرْسِلُوا لِهَلَاكِ قَوْمِ لُوطٍ، أَخَذَ يُدَافِعُ لَعَلَّهُمْ يُنظَرون، لَعَلَّ اللَّهَ أَنْ يَهْدِيَهُمْ، وَلَمَّا قَالُوا: ﴿إِنَّا مُهْلِكُو أَهْلِ هَذِهِ الْقَرْيَةِ﴾ ، ﴿قَالَ إِنَّ فِيهَا لُوطًا قَالُوا نَحْنُ أَعْلَمُ بِمَنْ فِيهَا لَنُنَجِّيَنَّهُ وَأَهْلَهُ إِلا امْرَأَتَهُ كَانَتْ مِنَ الْغَابِرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْهَالِكِينَ؛ لِأَنَّهَا كَانَتْ تُمَالِئُهُمْ عَلَى كُفْرِهِمْ وَبَغْيِهِمْ وَدُبُرِهِمْ. ثُمَّ سَارُوا مِنْ عِنْدِهِ فَدَخَلُوا عَلَى لُوطٍ فِي صُورَةِ شَبَابٍ حِسَانٍ، فَلَمَّا رَآهُمْ كَذَلِكَ، ﴿سِيءَ بِهِمْ وَضَاقَ بِهِمْ ذَرْعًا﴾ أَيْ: اهتمَّ بِأَمْرِهِمْ، إِنْ هُوَ أَضَافَهُمْ خَافَ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ قَوْمِهِ، وَإِنْ لَمْ يُضِفْهُمْ خَشِيَ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْهُمْ، وَلَمْ يَعْلَمْ بِأَمْرِهِمْ فِي السَّاعَةِ الرَّاهِنَةِ. ﴿قَالُوا لَا تَخَفْ وَلا تَحْزَنْ إِنَّا مُنَجُّوكَ وَأَهْلَكَ إِلا امْرَأَتَكَ كَانَتْ مِنَ الْغَابِرِينَ. إِنَّا مُنزلُونَ عَلَى أَهْلِ هَذِهِ الْقَرْيَةِ رِجْزًا مِنَ السَّمَاءِ بِمَا كَانُوا يَفْسُقُونَ﴾ ، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ جِبْرِيلَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ اقْتَلَعَ قُرَاهُمْ مِنْ قَرَارِ الْأَرْضِ، ثُمَّ رَفَعَهَا إِلَى عَنَان السَّمَاءِ، ثُمَّ قَلَبَهَا عَلَيْهِمْ. وَأَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ حِجَارَةً مِنْ سِجِّيلٍ مَنْضُودٍ، مُسَوَّمَةً عِنْدَ رَبِّكَ وَمَا هِيَ مِنَ الظَّالِمِينَ بِبَعِيدٍ، وَجَعَلَ [اللَّهُ] مَكَانَهَا بُحَيْرَةً خَبِيثَةً مُنْتِنَةً، وَجَعَلَهُمْ عِبْرَةً إِلَى يَوْمِ التَّنَادِ ، وَهُمْ مِنْ أَشَدِّ النَّاسِ عَذَابًا يَوْمَ الْمَعَادِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ تَرَكْنَا مِنْهَا آيَةً بَيِّنَةً﴾ أَيْ: وَاضِحَةً، ﴿لِقَوْمٍ يَعْقِلُونَ﴾ ، كَمَا قَالَ ﴿وَإِنَّكُمْ لَتَمُرُّونَ عَلَيْهِمْ مُصْبِحِينَ * وَبِاللَّيْلِ أَفَلا تَعْقِلُونَ﴾ [الصَّافَّاتِ: ١٣٧، ١٣٨] .

---

## 29:36-37 — verses 36-37 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted informs us about His servant and messenger Shu'ayb (peace be upon him), that he warned his people, the people of Madyan. He commanded them to worship God alone, having no partner, and to fear God's might, His vengeance, and His seizure on the Day of Resurrection. He said: {O my people, worship God and hope for the Last Day}.

Ibn Jarir said: some of them said its meaning is: and fear the Last Day. This is like His saying, the Exalted: {for whoever hopes for God and the Last Day} [al-Mumtahanah: 6].

Then he forbade them from ranging through the earth causing corruption, which is striving in it and transgressing against its people. This was because they used to give short measure in the scale and the measure, and they would waylay people on the road, this being alongside their disbelief in God and His messenger. So God destroyed them with a mighty tremor that shook their land, and a cry that tore hearts from their throats, and the punishment of the day of the shadow, which took away their souls from where they dwelt. It was indeed the punishment of a mighty day. Their story has already been related at length in the surahs of al-A'raf, Hud, and al-Shu'ara.

His saying: {So they became, in their homes, fallen prostrate}: Qatadah said, dead. Others said, they were thrown one upon another.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ عَبْدِهِ وَرَسُولِهِ شُعَيْبٍ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، أَنَّهُ أَنْذَرَ قَوْمَهُ أَهْلَ مَدين، فَأَمَرَهُمْ بِعِبَادَةِ اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، وَأَنْ يَخَافُوا بَأْسَ اللَّهِ وَنِقْمَتَهُ وَسَطْوَتَهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿يَا قَوْمِ اعْبُدُوا اللَّهَ وَارْجُوا الْيَوْمَ الآخِرَ﴾ .

. قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: قَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: مَعْنَاهُ: وَاخْشَوُا الْيَوْمَ الْآخِرَ، وَهَذَا كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿لِمَنْ كَانَ يَرْجُو اللَّهَ وَالْيَوْمَ الآخِرَ﴾ [الْمُمْتَحَنَةِ: ٦] .

ثُمَّ نَهَاهُمْ عَنِ الْعَيْثِ فِي الْأَرْضِ بِالْفَسَادِ، وَهُوَ السَّعْيُ فِيهَا وَالْبَغْيُ عَلَى أَهْلِهَا، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا يُنْقِصُونَ الْمِكْيَالَ وَالْمِيزَانَ، وَيَقْطَعُونَ الطَّرِيقَ عَلَى النَّاسِ، هَذَا مَعَ كَفْرِهِمْ بِاللَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ، فَأَهْلَكَهُمُ اللَّهُ بِرَجْفَةٍ عَظِيمَةٍ زَلْزَلَتْ عَلَيْهِمْ بِلَادَهُمْ، وَصَيْحَةٍ أَخْرَجَتِ الْقُلُوبَ مِنْ حَنَاجِرِهَا . وَعَذَابِ يَوْمِ الظُّلَّةِ الَّذِي أَزْهَقَ الْأَرْوَاحَ مِنْ مُسْتَقَرِّهَا، إِنَّهُ كَانَ عَذَابَ يَوْمٍ عَظِيمٍ. وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَتْ قِصَّتُهُمْ مَبْسُوطَةً فِي سُورَةِ "الْأَعْرَافِ، وَهُودٍ، وَالشُّعَرَاءِ".

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَأَصْبَحُوا فِي دَارِهِمْ جَاثِمِينَ﴾ ، قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: مَيِّتِينَ. وَقَالَ غَيْرُهُ: قَدْ أُلْقِيَ بَعْضُهُمْ عَلَى بَعْضٍ.

---

## 29:38-40 — verses 38-40 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty tells us about these nations that denied the messengers, how He destroyed them and varied their punishment, seizing them in retribution. Ad were the people of Hud, and they used to dwell in al-Ahqaf, which is near Hadramawt, the lands of Yemen. Thamud were the people of Salih, and they used to dwell in al-Hijr, near Wadi al-Qura. The Arabs knew the dwellings of both of these peoples well and passed by them often. Qarun was the possessor of abundant wealth and the keys to heavy treasures. Pharaoh was the king of Egypt in the time of Musa (peace be upon him), and his minister Haman, the two Coptic disbelievers in Allah and His Messenger.

{So each We seized for his sin}, meaning: his punishment was fitting for him. {And of them was he upon whom We sent a hasib (violent storm of stones)}, and they were Ad. That was because they said, "Who is stronger than us in might?" So there came upon them a bitterly cold, roaring wind, extremely violent in its blowing, carrying against them the pebbles of the earth and hurling them upon them, uprooting them from the ground so that it would lift a man of them up to the clouds of the sky, then turn him upside down onto the crown of his head and smash it, so that he remained a body without a head, as though they were trunks of uprooted palm trees.

{And of them was he whom the Sayha (Blast) seized}, and they were Thamud. The proof had been established against them and the sign had appeared to them, from that she-camel which the rock split open to bring forth, exactly as they had asked, precisely so. Yet despite this they did not believe; rather they persisted in their transgression and disbelief, and threatened the Prophet of Allah, Salih (peace be upon him), and those who believed with him, vowing to drive them out and stone them. So there came upon them a Blast that silenced their voices and stilled their movements.

{And of them was he whom We caused the earth to swallow}, and this was Qarun, who transgressed, oppressed, and was insolent, and disobeyed the Most High Lord, and walked upon the earth exultantly, rejoicing and reveling, losing himself in arrogance, believing himself better than others, and swaggering in his gait. So Allah caused the earth to swallow him and his house, and he sinks down into it continually until the Day of Resurrection.

{And of them was he whom We drowned}, and they were Pharaoh and his minister Haman, and his soldiers, every last one of them. They were drowned in a single morning, and not one survivor remained among them to give report. {And Allah would not have wronged them}, meaning: in what He did to them, {but it was they who used to wrong themselves}, meaning: He only did that to them as a fitting recompense for what their hands had earned.

What we have mentioned is the apparent sense of the flow of the verse, and it follows the pattern of laff and nashr (interweaving and unfolding), namely that He mentioned the denying nations, then said: {So each We seized for his sin} [the verse], meaning: from among those mentioned. I have drawn attention to this because it has been related that Ibn Jurayj said: Ibn Abbas said regarding His statement, {And of them was he upon whom We sent a hasib}: "The people of Lut." {And of them was he whom We drowned}: "The people of Nuh."

But this chain is disconnected (munqati) from Ibn Abbas, for Ibn Jurayj did not meet him. Moreover, this surah already mentions the destruction of the people of Nuh by the Flood, and the people of Lut by the sending down of the punishment (rijz) from the sky, and the account is long, and there is a great distance between that passage and this one.

Qatada said: {And of them was he upon whom We sent a hasib}: "the people of Lut." {And of them was he whom the Sayha seized}: "the people of Shuayb." This too is far-fetched, for the reasons given above. And Allah knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ هَؤُلَاءِ الْأُمَمِ الْمُكَذِّبَةِ لِلرُّسُلِ كَيْفَ أَبَادَهُمْ وَتَنَوَّعَ فِي عَذَابِهِمْ، فَأَخَذَهُمْ بِالِانْتِقَامِ مِنْهُمْ، فَعَادٌ قَوْمُ هُودٍ، وَكَانُوا يَسْكُنُونَ الْأَحْقَافَ وَهِيَ قَرِيبَةٌ مِنْ حَضْرَمَوْتَ بِلَادِ الْيَمَنِ، وَثَمُودُ قَوْمُ صَالِحٍ، وَكَانُوا يَسْكُنُونَ الْحِجْرَ قَرِيبًا مِنْ وَادِي الْقُرَى. وَكَانَتِ الْعَرَبُ تَعْرِفُ مَسَاكِنَهُمَا جَيِّدًا، وَتَمُرُّ عَلَيْهَا كَثِيرًا. وَقَارُونُ صَاحِبُ الْأَمْوَالِ الْجَزِيلَةِ وَمَفَاتِيحِ الْكُنُوزِ الثَّقِيلَةِ. وَفِرْعَوْنُ مَلِكُ مِصْرَ فِي زَمَانِ مُوسَى وَوَزِيرُهُ هَامَانَ الْقِبْطِيَّانِ الْكَافِرَانِ بِاللَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ.

﴿فَكُلا أَخَذْنَا بِذَنْبِهِ﴾ أَيْ: كَانَتْ عُقُوبَتُهُ بِمَا يُنَاسِبُهُ، ﴿فَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ أَرْسَلْنَا عَلَيْهِ حَاصِبًا﴾ ، وَهُمْ عَادٌ، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّهُمْ قَالُوا: مَنْ أشدُّ مِنَّا قُوَّةً؟ فَجَاءَتْهُمْ رِيحٌ صَرْصَرٌ بَارِدَةٌ شَدِيدَةُ الْبَرْدِ، عَاتِيَةٌ شَدِيدَةُ الْهُبُوبِ جِدًّا، تَحْمِلُ عَلَيْهِمْ حَصْبَاءَ الْأَرْضِ فَتَقْلِبُهَا عَلَيْهِمْ، وَتَقْتَلِعُهُمْ مِنَ الْأَرْضِ فَتَرْفَعُ الرَّجُلَ مِنْهُمْ إِلَى عَنَان السَّمَاءِ، ثُمَّ تُنَكِّسُهُ عَلَى أُمِّ رَأْسِهِ فَتَشْدَخُهُ فَيَبْقَى بَدَنًا بِلَا رَأْسٍ، كَأَنَّهُمْ أَعْجَازُ نَخْلٍ مُنْقَعِرٍ . ﴿وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ أَخَذَتْهُ الصَّيْحَةُ﴾ ، وَهُمْ ثَمُودُ، قَامَتْ عَلَيْهِمُ الْحُجَّةُ وَظَهَرَتْ لَهُمُ الدَّلَالَةُ، مِنْ تِلْكَ النَّاقَةِ الَّتِي انْفَلَقَتْ عَنْهَا الصَّخْرَةُ، مِثْلَ مَا سَأَلُوا سَوَاءً بِسَوَاءٍ، وَمَعَ هَذَا مَا آمَنُوا بَلِ اسْتَمَرُّوا عَلَى طُغْيَانِهِمْ وَكُفْرِهِمْ، وَتَهَدَّدُوا نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ صَالِحًا ومَنْ آمَنَ مَعَهُ، وتوعَّدوهُم بِأَنْ يُخْرِجُوهُمْ وَيَرْجُمُوهُمْ، فَجَاءَتْهُمْ صَيْحَةٌ أَخَمَدَتِ الْأَصْوَاتَ مِنْهُمْ وَالْحَرَكَاتِ. ﴿وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ خَسَفْنَا بِهِ الأرْضَ﴾ ، وَهُوَ قَارُونُ الَّذِي طَغَى وَبَغَى وَعَتَا، وَعَصَى الرَّبَّ الْأَعْلَى، وَمَشَى فِي الْأَرْضِ مَرَحًا، وَفَرِحَ وَمَرِحَ وَتَاهَ بِنَفْسِهِ، وَاعْتَقَدَ أَنَّهُ أَفْضَلُ مِنْ غَيْرِهِ، وَاخْتَالَ فِي مِشْيَتِهِ، فَخَسَفَ اللَّهُ بِهِ وَبِدَارِهِ الْأَرْضَ، فَهُوَ يَتَجَلْجَلُ فِيهَا إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ. ﴿وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ أَغْرَقْنَا﴾ ، وَهُمْ فِرْعَوْنُ وَوَزِيرُهُ هَامَانُ، وَجُنُودُهُ عَنْ آخِرِهِمْ، أُغْرِقُوا فِي صَبِيحَةٍ وَاحِدَةٍ، فَلَمْ يَنْجُ مِنْهُمْ مُخْبِرٌ، ﴿وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيَظْلِمَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: فِيمَا فَعَلَ بِهِمْ، ﴿وَلَكِنْ كَانُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ يَظْلِمُونَ﴾ أي: إنما فعل ذلك بِهِمْ جَزَاءً وِفَاقًا بِمَا كَسَبَتْ أَيْدِيهِمْ.

وَهَذَا الَّذِي ذَكَرْنَاهُ ظَاهِرُ سِيَاقِ الْآيَةِ، وَهُوَ مِنْ بَابِ اللَّفِّ وَالنَّشْرِ، وَهُوَ أَنَّهُ ذَكَرَ الْأُمَمَ الْمُكَذِّبَةَ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿فَكُلا أَخَذْنَا بِذَنْبِهِ﴾ [الْآيَةَ] ، أَيْ: مِنْ هَؤُلَاءِ الْمَذْكُورِينَ، وَإِنَّمَا نبهتُ عَلَى هَذَا لِأَنَّهُ قَدْ رُوِيَ أَنَّ ابْنَ جُرَيْجٍ قَالَ: قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ أَرْسَلْنَا عَلَيْهِ حَاصِبًا﴾ ، قَالَ: قَوْمُ لُوطٍ. ﴿وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ أَغْرَقْنَا﴾ ، قَالَ: قَوْمُ نُوحٍ.

وَهَذَا مُنْقَطِعٌ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ؛ فَإِنَّ ابْنَ جُرْيَج لَمْ يُدْرِكْهُ. ثُمَّ قَدْ ذُكِرَ فِي هَذِهِ السُّورَةِ إِهْلَاكُ قَوْمِ نُوحٍ بِالطُّوفَانِ، وَقَوْمِ لُوطٍ بِإِنْزَالِ الرِّجْزِ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ، وَطَالَ السياقُ والفصلُ بَيْنَ ذَلِكَ وَبَيْنَ هَذَا السِّيَاقِ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ﴿فَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ أَرْسَلْنَا عَلَيْهِ حَاصِبًا﴾ قَالَ: قَوْمُ لُوطٍ، ﴿وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ أَخَذَتْهُ الصَّيْحَةُ﴾ ، قَوْمُ شُعَيْبٍ. وَهَذَا بَعِيدٌ أَيْضًا لِمَا تَقَدَّمَ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

---

## 29:41-43 — verses 41-43 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is a parable that God, exalted is He, coined for the polytheists regarding their taking of gods besides God, hoping for their help and provision, and clinging to them in times of hardship. They are in that state like the house of the spider in its weakness and frailty. What these people have in the hands of their gods is nothing but like one who clings to the house of a spider, which avails him nothing at all. Had they known this true state of affairs, they would not have taken protectors besides God. This is unlike the Muslim believer whose heart belongs to God, and who, along with that, does good deeds in following the divine law. Such a person holds fast to the firm handhold that has no breaking, because of its strength and steadfastness.

Then God, exalted is He, said, threatening whoever worships other than Him and associates partners with Him: that He, exalted is He, knows what deeds they are engaged in, and knows what rivals they associate with Him, and He will requite them according to their description. Indeed He is Wise, All-Knowing.

Then God, exalted is He, said: {And these examples We put forward for the people, but none grasp them except those who possess knowledge}, meaning: none understand them and reflect upon them deeply except those firmly grounded in knowledge, those thoroughly steeped in it.

Imam Ahmad said: Ishaq ibn Isa related to us, Ibn Lahi'ah related to me, from Abu Qabil, from Amr ibn al-As, may God be pleased with him, who said: "I have grasped and retained a thousand parables from the Messenger of God ﷺ."

This is a great distinction for Amr ibn al-As, may God be pleased with him, in light of the statement of God, exalted is He: {And these examples We put forward for the people, but none grasp them except those who possess knowledge}.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: Ali ibn al-Husayn related to us, Ahmad ibn Abd al-Rahman related to us, my father related to me, Ibn Sinan related to us, from Amr ibn Murrah, who said: "I never passed by a verse from the Book of God that I did not understand without it grieving me, because I heard God, exalted is He, saying: {And these examples We put forward for the people, but none grasp them except those who possess knowledge}."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا مَثَلٌ ضَرَبَهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى لِلْمُشْرِكِينَ فِي اتِّخَاذِهِمْ آلِهَةً مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ، يَرْجُونَ نَصْرَهُمْ وَرِزْقَهُمْ، وَيَتَمَسَّكُونَ بِهِمْ فِي الشَّدَائِدِ، فَهُمْ فِي ذَلِكَ كَبَيْتِ الْعَنْكَبُوتِ فِي ضَعْفِهِ وَوَهَنِهِ فَلَيْسَ فِي أَيْدِي هَؤُلَاءِ مِنْ آلِهَتِهِمْ إِلَّا كمَنْ يَتَمَسَّكُ بِبَيْتِ الْعَنْكَبُوتِ، فَإِنَّهُ لَا يُجْدِي عَنْهُ شَيْئًا، فَلَوْ عَلموا هَذَا الْحَالَ لَمَا اتَّخَذُوا مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ أَوْلِيَاءَ، وَهَذَا بِخِلَافِ الْمُسْلِمِ الْمُؤْمِنِ قَلْبُهُ لِلَّهِ، وَهُوَ مَعَ ذَلِكَ يُحْسِنُ الْعَمَلَ فِي اتِّبَاعِ الشَّرْعِ فَإِنَّهُ مُسْتَمْسِكٌ بِالْعُرْوَةِ الْوُثْقَى لَا انْفِصَامَ لَهَا، لِقُوَّتِهَا وَثَبَاتِهَا.

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى مُتَوَعِّدًا لِمَنْ عَبَدَ غَيْرَهُ وَأَشْرَكَ بِهِ: إِنَّهُ تَعَالَى يَعْلَمُ مَا هُمْ عَلَيْهِ مِنَ الْأَعْمَالِ، وَيَعْلَمُ مَا يُشْرِكُونَ بِهِ مِنَ الْأَنْدَادِ، وَسَيَجْزِيهِمْ وَصْفَهُمْ إِنَّهُ حَكِيمٌ عَلِيمٌ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَتِلْكَ الأمْثَالُ نَضْرِبُهَا لِلنَّاسِ وَمَا يَعْقِلُهَا إِلا الْعَالِمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: وَمَا يَفْهَمُهَا وَيَتَدَبَّرُهَا إِلَّا الرَّاسِخُونَ فِي الْعِلْمِ الْمُتَضَلِّعُونَ مِنْهُ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْحَاقُ بْنُ عِيسَى، حَدَّثَنِي ابْنُ لَهِيعة، عَنْ أَبِي قَبِيل ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ الْعَاصِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: عَقَلْتُ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَلْفَ مَثَلٍ .

وَهَذِهِ مَنْقَبَةٌ عَظِيمَةٌ لِعَمْرِو بْنِ الْعَاصِ -رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عنه -حيث يقول [الله] تعالى: ﴿وَتِلْكَ الأمْثَالُ نَضْرِبُهَا لِلنَّاسِ وَمَا يَعْقِلُهَا إِلا الْعَالِمُونَ﴾ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ سِنَانٍ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ مُرَّةَ قَالَ: مَا مَرَرْتُ بِآيَةٍ مِنْ كِتَابِ اللَّهِ لَا أَعْرِفُهَا إِلَّا أَحْزَنَنِي، لِأَنِّي سَمِعْتُ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى يَقُولُ: ﴿وَتِلْكَ الأمْثَالُ نَضْرِبُهَا لِلنَّاسِ وَمَا يَعْقِلُهَا إِلا الْعَالِمُونَ﴾ .

---

## 29:44-45 — verses 44-45 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says, informing of His tremendous power, that He created the heavens and the earth in truth, meaning: not for the sake of futility and play, {so that every soul may be recompensed for what it strives} [Ta Ha: 15], {so that He may recompense those who did evil for what they did, and recompense those who did good with the best reward} [al-Najm: 31].

His saying, {Indeed in that is a sign for the believers}, means: a clear proof that He, the Exalted, is the sole one possessed of creation, governance, and divinity.

Then the Exalted, commanding His Messenger and the believers to recite the Qur'an, meaning: to read it and convey it to the people, says: {And establish prayer. Indeed, prayer prevents immorality and wrongdoing, and the remembrance of Allah is greater} meaning: that prayer encompasses two things: the abandonment of immoralities and wrongdoings, that is, its constant observance drives one to abandon these. It has come in the hadith, from the narration of Imran and Ibn Abbas, as a raised report (marfu): "Whoever's prayer does not prevent him from immorality and wrongdoing, it increases him only in distance from Allah."

[Mention of the reports transmitted concerning this]:

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Imran ibn Husayn said: The Prophet ﷺ was asked about the saying of Allah, {Indeed, prayer prevents immorality and wrongdoing}. He said: "Whoever's prayer does not prevent him from immorality and wrongdoing, he has no prayer."

[chain] Ibn Abbas said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Whoever's prayer does not prevent him from immorality and wrongdoing, it increases him only in distance from Allah." Al-Tabarani also transmitted it through the hadith of Abu Mu'awiyah.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] regarding Ibn Abbas's statement on His saying, {Indeed, prayer prevents immorality and wrongdoing}: he said: whoever's prayer does not command him to good and prevent him from wrongdoing, his prayer increases him only in distance from Allah. This is a mawquf (halted report, attributed only to a Companion rather than the Prophet ﷺ).

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] from Ibn Mas'ud, from the Prophet ﷺ, that he said: "There is no prayer for one who does not obey the prayer, and obedience of the prayer is that it prevent immorality and wrongdoing." He said: and Sufyan said regarding {They said, O Shu'ayb, does your prayer command you} [Hud: 87]: Sufyan said: yes, by Allah, it commands him and forbids him.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from Abdullah, he said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, and Abu Khalid once said "from Abdullah" (meaning as a statement of Abdullah himself): "There is no prayer for one who does not obey the prayer, and obedience of the prayer is that it prevent him from immorality and wrongdoing."

The mawquf version is more authentic, as al-A'mash related from Malik ibn al-Harith, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Yazid, who said: it was said to Abdullah: so-and-so prolongs his prayer. He said: prayer benefits only the one who obeys it.

Ibn Jarir said: Ali said: [chain] from al-Hasan, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Whoever prays a prayer that does not prevent him from immorality and wrongdoing, it increases him only in distance from Allah."

The most authentic view in all of this is that these are mawquf reports from Ibn Mas'ud, Ibn Abbas, al-Hasan, Qatadah, al-A'mash, and others. And Allah knows best.

The hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bazzar said: [chain] Abu Salih said, I think from Jabir, al-A'mash being uncertain, he said: a man said to the Prophet ﷺ: so-and-so prays, yet when morning comes he steals. He said: "What he says will restrain him."

[chain] from Jabir, from the Prophet ﷺ, similarly, without doubt this time. Then he said: this hadith has been related by more than one from al-A'mash, and they differed regarding its chain. More than one related it from al-A'mash, from Abu Salih, from Abu Hurayrah or someone else. Qays said, from al-A'mash, from Abu Sufyan, from Jabir. Jarir and Ziyad said: from Abdullah, from al-A'mash, from Abu Salih, from Jabir.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Abu Hurayrah, who said: a man came to the Prophet ﷺ and said: so-and-so prays at night, yet when morning comes he steals. He said: "What he says will indeed restrain him."

Prayer also encompasses the remembrance of Allah the Exalted, which is the greatest objective sought. This is why the Exalted said: {and the remembrance of Allah is greater}, meaning: greater than the first matter mentioned. {And Allah knows what you do}, meaning: He knows all your words and deeds.

Abu al-Aliyah said regarding His saying, {Indeed, prayer prevents immorality and wrongdoing}: prayer contains three qualities, and any prayer lacking any of these qualities is not a true prayer: sincerity (ikhlas), fear (khashyah), and remembrance of Allah. Sincerity commands one to good, fear prevents one from wrongdoing, and the remembrance found in the Qur'an both commands and forbids.

Ibn Awn al-Ansari said: when you are in prayer, you are engaged in something good, and it has restrained you from immorality and wrongdoing, and what you are engaged in of the remembrance of Allah is greater still.

Hammad ibn Abi Sulayman said: {Indeed, prayer prevents immorality and wrongdoing}, meaning: as long as you remain within it.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah related from Ibn Abbas regarding His saying, {and the remembrance of Allah is greater}: he says: and Allah's remembrance of His servants is greater than their remembrance of Him, when they remember Him.

More than one narrator related the same from Ibn Abbas, and Mujahid and others said likewise.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from a man, from Ibn Abbas regarding {and the remembrance of Allah is greater}: he said: the remembrance of Allah at your food and at your sleep. I said: but a companion of mine at home says something other than what you say. He said: what does he say? I said: he says, Allah says, {So remember Me, and I will remember you} [al-Baqarah: 152], so Allah's remembrance of us is greater than our remembrance of Him. He said: he spoke truly.

He said: [chain] from Ibn Abbas regarding His saying, {and the remembrance of Allah is greater}: he said: it has two aspects: he said: the remembrance of Allah when it comes to what He has forbidden, he said: and Allah's remembrance of you is greater than your remembrance of Him.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] from Abdullah ibn Rabi'ah, who said: Ibn Abbas said to me: do you know what His saying, {and the remembrance of Allah is greater} means? I said: yes. He said: what is it then? I said: glorification (tasbih), praise (tahmid), and magnification (takbir) in prayer, and recitation of the Qur'an, and the like of that. He said: you have said something remarkable, but it is not so. Rather, it means: Allah's remembrance of you regarding what He commanded or forbade, when you remember it, is greater than your remembrance of Him.

This has been related through more than one route from Ibn Abbas, and it has also been related from Ibn Mas'ud, Abu al-Darda, Salman al-Farisi, and others. Ibn Jarir preferred this view.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى [مُخْبِرًا] عَنْ قُدْرَتِهِ الْعَظِيمَةِ: أَنَّهُ خَلَقَ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ بِالْحَقِّ، يَعْنِي: لَا عَلَى وَجْهِ الْعَبَثِ وَاللَّعِبِ، ﴿لِتُجْزَى كُلُّ نَفْسٍ بِمَا تَسْعَى﴾ [طَهَ: ١٥] ، ﴿لِيَجْزِيَ الَّذِينَ أَسَاءُوا بِمَا عَمِلُوا وَيَجْزِيَ الَّذِينَ أَحْسَنُوا بِالْحُسْنَى﴾ [النَّجْمِ: ٣١] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ فِي ذَلِكَ لآيَةً لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ أَيْ: لَدَلَالَةً وَاضِحَةً عَلَى أَنَّهُ تَعَالَى الْمُتَفَرِّدُ بِالْخَلْقِ وَالتَّدْبِيرِ وَالْإِلَهِيَّةِ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى آمِرًا رَسُولَهُ وَالْمُؤْمِنِينَ بِتِلَاوَةِ الْقُرْآنِ، وَهُوَ قِرَاءَتُهُ وَإِبْلَاغُهُ لِلنَّاسِ: ﴿وَأَقِمِ الصَّلاةَ إِنَّ الصَّلاةَ تَنْهَى عَنِ الْفَحْشَاءِ وَالْمُنْكَرِ وَلَذِكْرُ اللَّهِ أَكْبَرُ﴾ يَعْنِي: أَنَّ الصَّلَاةَ تَشْتَمِلُ عَلَى شَيْئَيْنِ: عَلَى تَرْكِ الْفَوَاحِشِ وَالْمُنْكَرَاتِ، أَيْ: إِنَّ مُوَاظَبَتَهَا تَحْمِلُ عَلَى تَرْكِ ذَلِكَ. وَقَدْ جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ مِنْ رِوَايَةِ عِمْرَانَ، وَابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ مَرْفُوعًا: "مَنْ لَمْ تَنْهَهُ صَلَاتُهُ عَنِ الْفَحْشَاءِ وَالْمُنْكَرِ، لَمْ تَزِدْهُ مِنَ اللَّهِ إِلَّا بُعْدًا" .

[ذِكْرُ الْآثَارِ الْوَارِدَةِ فِي ذَلِكَ] :

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ هَارُونَ الْمُخَرِّمِيُّ الْفَلَّاسُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ نَافِعٍ أَبُو زِيَادٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عُمَرُ بْنُ أَبِي عُثْمَانَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ، عَنْ عِمْرَانَ بْنِ حُصَيْنٍ قَالَ: سُئِل النَّبِيُّ ﷺ عَنْ قَوْلِ اللَّهِ: ﴿إِنَّ الصَّلاةَ تَنْهَى عَنِ الْفَحْشَاءِ وَالْمُنْكَرِ﴾ قَالَ: "مَنْ لَمْ تَنْهَهُ صَلَاتُهُ عَنِ الفحشاء والمنكر، فلا صلاة له" .

وَحَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ الْيَرْبُوعِيُّ حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ، عَنْ لَيْثٍ، عَنْ طَاوُسٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم: "مَنْ لَمْ تَنْهَهُ صَلَاتُهُ عَنِ الْفَحْشَاءِ وَالْمُنْكَرِ، لَمْ يَزْدَدْ بِهَا مِنَ اللَّهِ إِلَّا بُعْدًا". وَرَوَاهُ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي مُعَاوِيَةَ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا الْقَاسِمُ، حَدَّثَنَا الْحُسَيْنُ، حَدَّثَنَا خَالِدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، عَنِ الْعَلَاءِ بْنِ الْمُسَيَّبِ، عَمَّنْ ذَكَرَهُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنَّ الصَّلاةَ تَنْهَى عَنِ الْفَحْشَاءِ وَالْمُنْكَرِ﴾ قَالَ: فَمَنْ لَمْ تَأْمُرْهُ صَلَاتُهُ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ وَتَنْهَهُ عَنِ الْمُنْكَرِ، لَمْ يَزْدَدْ بِصَلَاتِهِ مِنَ اللَّهِ إِلَّا بُعْدًا. فَهَذَا مَوْقُوفٌ 

. قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَحَدَّثَنَا الْقَاسِمُ، حَدَّثَنَا الْحُسَيْنُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ هَاشِمِ بْنِ الْبَرِيدِ، عَنْ جُوَيْبِرٍ، عَنِ الضَّحَاكِ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "لَا صَلَاةَ لِمَنْ لَمْ يُطِعِ الصَّلَاةَ، وَطَاعَةُ الصَّلَاةِ أَنْ تَنْهَى عَنِ الْفَحْشَاءِ وَالْمُنْكَرِ". قَالَ: وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ: ﴿قَالُوا يَا شُعَيْبُ أَصَلاتُكَ تَأْمُرُكَ﴾ [هُودٍ: ٨٧] قَالَ: فَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ: أَيْ وَاللَّهِ، تَأْمُرُهُ وَتَنْهَاهُ. 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَعِيدٍ الأشَجّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو خَالِدٍ، عَنْ جُوَيْبِرٍ، عَنِ الضَّحَّاكِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ -وَقَالَ أَبُو خَالِدٍ مَرَّة: عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ -: "لَا صَلَاةَ لِمَنْ لَمْ يُطِعِ الصَّلَاةَ، وَطَاعَةُ الصَّلَاةِ تَنْهَاهُ عَنِ الْفَحْشَاءِ وَالْمُنْكَرِ" .

وَالْمَوْقُوفُ أَصَحُّ، كَمَا رَوَاهُ الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ مَالِكِ بْنِ الْحَارِثِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ يَزِيدَ قَالَ: قِيلَ لِعَبْدِ اللَّهِ: إِنَّ فُلَانًا يُطِيلُ الصَّلَاةَ؟ قَالَ: إِنَّ الصَّلَاةَ لَا تَنْفَعُ إِلَّا مَنْ أَطَاعَهَا .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: قَالَ عَلِيٌّ: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَنْ صَلَّى صَلَاةً لَمْ تَنْهَهُ عَنِ الفحشاء والمنكر، لم يزدد بها من الله إِلَّا بُعْدا" .

وَالْأَصَحُّ فِي هَذَا كُلِّهِ الْمَوْقُوفَاتُ عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، وَابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَالْحَسَنِ وقَتَادَةَ، وَالْأَعْمَشِ وَغَيْرِهِمْ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَزَّارُ: حَدَّثَنَا يُوسُفُ بْنُ مُوسَى، حَدَّثَنَا جَرِيرٌ -يَعْنِي ابْنَ عَبْدِ الْحَمِيدِ -عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ قَالَ: أُرَاهُ عَنْ جَابِرٍ -شَكَّ الْأَعْمَشُ -قَالَ: قَالَ رَجُلٌ لِلنَّبِيِّ ﷺ: إِنَّ فُلَانًا يُصَلِّي فَإِذَا أصبح سرق، قال: "سينهاه ما يقول" .

وَحَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ مُوسَى الحَرشي حَدَّثَنَا زِيَادُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ بِنَحْوِهِ -وَلَمْ يَشُكَّ -ثُمَّ قَالَ: وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ قَدْ رَوَاهُ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ وَاخْتَلَفُوا فِي إِسْنَادِهِ، فَرَوَاهُ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ أَوْ غَيْرِهِ، وَقَالَ قَيْسٌ عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ أَبِي سُفْيَانَ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ، وَقَالَ جَرِيرٌ وَزِيَادٌ: عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيع، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ قَالَ: أَنْبَأَنَا أَبُو صَالِحٍ عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: جَاءَ رَجُلٌ إِلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فَقَالَ: إِنَّ فُلَانًا يُصَلِّي بِاللَّيْلِ فَإِذَا أَصْبَحَ سَرَقَ؟ فَقَالَ: "إِنَّهُ سَيَنْهَاهُ مَا يَقُولُ ".

وَتَشْتَمِلُ الصَّلَاةُ أَيْضًا عَلَى ذِكْرِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى، وَهُوَ الْمَطْلُوبُ الْأَكْبَرُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَذِكْرُ اللَّهِ أَكْبَرُ﴾ أَيْ: أَعْظَمُ مِنَ الْأَوَّلِ، ﴿وَاللَّهُ يَعْلَمُ مَا تَصْنَعُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يَعْلَمُ جَمِيعَ أَقْوَالِكُمْ وَأَعْمَالِكُمْ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنَّ الصَّلاةَ تَنْهَى عَنِ الْفَحْشَاءِ وَالْمُنْكَرِ﴾ ، قَالَ: إِنَّ الصَّلَاةَ فِيهَا ثَلَاثُ خِصَالٍ فَكُلُّ صَلَاةٍ لَا يَكُونُ فِيهَا شَيْءٌ مِنْ هَذِهِ الْخِلَالِ فَلَيْسَتْ بِصَلَاةٍ: الْإِخْلَاصُ، وَالْخَشْيَةُ، وَذِكْرُ اللَّهِ. فَالْإِخْلَاصُ يَأْمُرُهُ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ، وَالْخَشْيَةُ تَنْهَاهُ عَنِ الْمُنْكَرِ، وَذِكْرُ الْقُرْآنِ يَأْمُرُهُ وَيَنْهَاهُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَوْن الْأَنْصَارِيُّ: إِذَا كُنْتَ فِي صَلَاةٍ فَأَنْتَ فِي مَعْرُوفٍ، وَقَدْ حَجَزَتْكَ عَنِ الْفَحْشَاءِ وَالْمُنْكَرِ، وَالَّذِي أَنْتَ فِيهِ مِنْ ذِكْرِ اللَّهِ أَكْبَرُ.

وَقَالَ حَمَّادُ بْنُ أَبِي سُلَيْمَانَ: ﴿إِنَّ الصَّلاةَ تَنْهَى عَنِ الْفَحْشَاءِ وَالْمُنْكَرِ﴾ يَعْنِي: مَا دُمْتَ فِيهَا.

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلَذِكْرُ اللَّهِ أَكْبَرُ﴾ ، يَقُولُ: وَلَذِكْرُ اللَّهِ لِعِبَادِهِ أَكْبَرُ، إِذَا ذَكَرُوهُ مِنْ ذِكْرِهُمْ إِيَّاهُ.

وَكَذَا رَوَى غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ. وَبِهِ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَغَيْرُهُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَعِيدٍ الْأَشَجُّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو خَالِدٍ الْأَحْمَرُ، عَنْ دَاوُدَ بْنِ أَبِي هِنْدٍ، عَنْ رَجُلٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَلَذِكْرُ اللَّهِ أَكْبَرُ﴾ قَالَ: ذِكْرُ اللَّهِ عِنْدَ طَعَامِكَ وَعِنْدَ مَنَامِكَ. قُلْتُ: فَإِنَّ صَاحِبًا لِي فِي الْمَنْزِلِ يَقُولُ غَيْرَ الَّذِي تَقُولُ: قَالَ: وَأَيَّ شَيْءٍ يَقُولُ؟ قُلْتُ: قَالَ: يَقُولُ اللَّهُ: ﴿فَاذْكُرُونِي أَذْكُرْكُمْ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ١٥٢] ، فَلَذِكْرُ اللَّهِ إِيَّانَا أَكْبَرُ مِنْ ذِكْرِنَا إِيَّاهُ. قَالَ: صَدَقَ.

قَالَ: وَحَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا النُّفَيْلِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ، عَنْ خَالِدٍ، عَنْ عِكْرِمة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلَذِكْرُ اللَّهِ أَكْبَرُ﴾ قَالَ: لَهَا وَجْهَانِ، قَالَ: ذِكْرُ اللَّهِ عِنْدَمَا حَرَّمَهُ، قَالَ: وَذِكْرُ اللَّهِ إِيَّاكُمْ أَعْظَمُ مِنْ ذِكْرِكُمْ إِيَّاهُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي يَعْقُوبُ بْنُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، حدَّثنا هُشَيْم، أَخْبَرَنَا عَطَاءِ بْنِ السَّائِبِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ رَبِيعَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ لِي ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: هَلْ تَدْرِي مَا قَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَذِكْرُ اللَّهِ أَكْبَرُ﴾ ؟ قَالَ: قُلْتُ: نَعَمْ. قَالَ: فَمَا هُوَ؟ قُلْتُ: التَّسْبِيحُ وَالتَّحْمِيدُ وَالتَّكْبِيرُ فِي الصَّلَاةِ، وَقِرَاءَةُ الْقُرْآنِ، وَنَحْوُ ذَلِكَ. قَالَ: لَقَدْ قُلْتَ قَوْلًا عَجَبًا، وَمَا هُوَ كَذَلِكَ، وَلَكِنَّهُ إِنَّمَا يَقُولُ: ذِكْرُ اللَّهِ إِيَّاكُمْ عِنْدَمَا أَمَرَ بِهِ أَوْ نَهَى عَنْهُ إِذَا ذَكَرْتُمُوهُ، أَكْبَرُ مِنْ ذِكْرِكُمْ إِيَّاهُ 

. وَقَدْ رُوِيَ هَذَا مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ. وَرُوِيَ أَيْضًا عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، وَأَبِي الدَّرْدَاءِ، وَسَلْمَانَ الْفَارِسِيِّ، وغيرهم. واختاره ابن جرير.

---

## 29:46 — verse 46

### Translation

Qatada and others said: this verse is abrogated by the verse of the sword, and no more disputation was left with them, but rather it is Islam, or the jizya, or the sword.

Others said: rather it remains valid and stands as a firm ruling for whoever among them wishes to seek clarity in religion, so one disputes with him in the best manner, so that it may be more effective with him, just as the Almighty said: {Call to the way of your Lord with wisdom and good preaching, and dispute with them in the manner that is best. Indeed your Lord knows best who has strayed from His way, and He knows best those who are guided} [al-Nahl: 125]. And the Almighty said to Musa and Harun (peace be upon them) when He sent them to Pharaoh: {So speak to him gentle speech, that perhaps he may be reminded or fear} [Ta Ha: 44]. This view was chosen by Ibn Jarir, who related it from Ibn Zayd.

His saying: {Except those among them who do wrong}, meaning: they turned away from the face of truth, went blind to the clear path, and were obstinate and arrogant. In that case one moves from disputation to combat, and they are fought with what deters and restrains them. The Almighty said: {We have already sent Our messengers with clear proofs and sent down with them the Book and the Balance, so that the people may maintain justice. And We sent down iron, in which there is great strength and benefits for the people, and so that Allah may know who supports Him and His messengers unseen. Indeed Allah is Strong, Mighty} [al-Hadid: 25].

Jabir said: We have been commanded that whoever opposes the Book of Allah, we strike him with the sword.

Mujahid said: {Except those among them who do wrong}, meaning: the people at war, and those among them who refuse to pay the jizya.

His saying: {And say: we believe in what has been sent down to us and what has been sent down to you}, meaning: when they report something whose truth or falsehood is not known, we do not rush to reject it as false, for it may be true, nor do we rush to affirm it as true, for it may be false. Rather we believe in it with a general belief, conditioned upon it being something genuinely revealed, not altered and not subjected to false interpretation.

Al-Bukhari, may Allah have mercy on him, said: [chain] Abu Hurairah, may Allah be pleased with him, said: the People of the Book used to recite the Torah in Hebrew and explain it in Arabic to the people of Islam. So the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Do not believe the People of the Book nor disbelieve them, but say: we believe in Allah and what has been sent down to us and what has been sent down to you, and our God and your God is one, and to Him we submit." Al-Bukhari alone narrated this hadith.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Namla al-Ansari reported that while he was sitting with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, a man from the Jews came to him and said: O Muhammad, does this funeral bier speak? The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Allah knows best." The Jew said: I bear witness that it speaks. So the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "When the People of the Book speak to you, do not believe them nor disbelieve them, but say: we believe in Allah, His messengers, and His books. If it is true, you will not have rejected it, and if it is false, you will not have affirmed it."

I say: this Abu Namla is Umara, and it is also said Ammar, and it is also said Amr ibn Muadh ibn Zurara al-Ansari, may Allah be pleased with him.

Then let it be known that most of what they report is largely lies and falsehood, because distortion, alteration, change, and false interpretation have entered into it, and how little truth remains in it. Then how little benefit much of it would even have, were it authentic.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Abdullah, that is Ibn Masud, said: do not ask the People of the Book about anything, for they will never guide you, having themselves gone astray. Either you would reject something true or affirm something false. There is not one of the People of the Book but has in his heart a lingering attachment calling him to his religion, like the lingering attachment to wealth.

Al-Bukhari said: [chain] Ibn Abbas said: how can you ask the People of the Book about anything, when your Book which was sent down upon His Messenger ﷺ is the most recent, and you recite it pure, unmixed with anything, and it has told you that the People of the Book altered the Book of Allah and changed it, and wrote the book with their own hands and said, this is from Allah, in order to sell it for a small price? Does not what has come to you of knowledge forbid you from asking them? No, by Allah, we have not seen any man among them ask you about what has been sent down to you.

Al-Bukhari said: Abu al-Yaman said: [chain] Humaid ibn Abd al-Rahman said that he heard Muawiya speaking to a group of Quraysh in Madina, and he mentioned Kaab al-Ahbar, and said: he was among the most truthful of these narrators who report from the People of the Book, yet even so we used to detect falsehood in what he said.

I say: its meaning is that falsehood occurred from him linguistically, without intention, because he would report from scriptures he held a good opinion of, while they contained things fabricated and false, since there were no meticulous, precise memorizers preserving their religion as there were in this great nation. And despite that, and despite the closeness in time, many fabricated hadiths arose within this nation, known only to Allah and to whomever Allah has granted knowledge of them, each according to his capacity. To Allah belongs praise and grace.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ: هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ مَنْسُوخَةٌ بِآيَةِ السَّيْفِ، وَلَمْ يَبْقَ مَعَهُمْ مُجَادَلَةٌ، وَإِنَّمَا هُوَ الْإِسْلَامُ أَوِ الْجِزْيَةُ أَوِ السَّيْفُ.

وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: بَلْ هِيَ بَاقِيَةٌ أَوْ مُحْكَمَةٌ لِمَنْ أَرَادَ الِاسْتِبْصَارَ مِنْهُمْ فِي الدِّينِ، فَيُجَادِلُ بِالَّتِي هِيَ أَحْسَنُ، لِيَكُونَ أَنْجَعَ فِيهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿ادْعُ إِلَى سَبِيلِ رَبِّكَ بِالْحِكْمَةِ وَالْمَوْعِظَةِ الْحَسَنَةِ وَجَادِلْهُمْ بِالَّتِي هِيَ أَحْسَنُ إِنَّ رَبَّكَ هُوَ أَعْلَمُ بِمَنْ ضَلَّ عَنْ سَبِيلِهِ وَهُوَ أَعْلَمُ بِالْمُهْتَدِينَ﴾ [النَّحْلِ: ١٢٥] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى لِمُوسَى وَهَارُونَ حِينَ بَعَثَهُمَا إِلَى فِرْعَوْنَ: ﴿فَقُولا لَهُ قَوْلا لَيِّنًا لَعَلَّهُ يَتَذَكَّرُ أَوْ يَخْشَى﴾ [طَهَ: ٤٤] . وَهَذَا الْقَوْلُ اخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ ، وَحَكَاهُ عَنِ ابْنِ زَيْدٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِلا الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا مِنْهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: حَادُوا عَنْ وَجْهِ الْحَقِّ ، وعَمُوا عَنْ وَاضِحِ الْمَحَجَّةِ، وَعَانَدُوا وَكَابَرُوا، فَحِينَئِذٍ يُنْتَقَلُ مِنَ الْجِدَالِ إِلَى الْجِلَادِ، وَيُقَاتَلُونَ بِمَا يَرْدَعُهُمْ وَيَمْنَعُهُمْ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَقَدْ أَرْسَلْنَا رُسُلَنَا بِالْبَيِّنَاتِ وَأَنزلْنَا مَعَهُمُ الْكِتَابَ وَالْمِيزَانَ لِيَقُومَ النَّاسُ بِالْقِسْطِ وَأَنزلْنَا الْحَدِيدَ فِيهِ بَأْسٌ شَدِيدٌ وَمَنَافِعُ لِلنَّاسِ وَلِيَعْلَمَ اللَّهُ مَنْ يَنْصُرُهُ وَرُسُلَهُ بِالْغَيْبِ إِنَّ اللَّهَ قَوِيٌّ عَزِيزٌ﴾ [الْحَدِيدِ: ٢٥] .

قَالَ جَابِرٌ: أمرْنَا مَنْ خَالَفَ كِتَابَ اللَّهِ أَنْ نَضْرِبَهُ بِالسَّيْفِ.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: ﴿إِلا الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا مِنْهُمْ﴾ يَعْنِي: أَهْلَ الْحَرْبِ، وَمَنِ امْتَنَعَ مِنْهُمْ عَنْ أَدَاءِ الْجِزْيَةِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَقُولُوا آمَنَّا بِالَّذِي أُنزلَ إِلَيْنَا وَأُنزلَ إِلَيْكُمْ﴾ ، يَعْنِي: إِذَا أَخْبَرُوا بِمَا لَا يُعْلَمُ صِدْقُهُ وَلَا كَذِبُهُ، فَهَذَا لَا نُقدم عَلَى تَكْذِيبِهِ لِأَنَّهُ قَدْ يَكُونُ حَقًّا، وَلَا عَلَى تَصْدِيقِهِ، فَلَعَلَّهُ أَنْ يكون باطلا وَلَكِنْ نُؤْمِنُ بِهِ إِيمَانًا مُجْمَلًا مُعَلَّقًا عَلَى شَرْطٍ وَهُوَ أَنْ يَكُونَ مُنْزَلًا لَا مُبَدَّلًا وَلَا مُؤَوَّلًا.

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بَشَّارٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عُثْمَانُ بْنُ عُمَر، أَخْبَرَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ، عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ أَبِي كَثِيرٍ، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ قَالَ: كَانَ أَهْلُ الكتاب يقرؤون التَّوْرَاةَ بِالْعِبْرَانِيَّةِ، وَيُفَسِّرُونَهَا بِالْعَرَبِيَّةِ لِأَهْلِ الْإِسْلَامِ، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لا تُصَدِّقُوا أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ وَلَا تُكَذِّبُوهُمْ، وَقُولُوا: آمَنَّا بِاللَّهِ وَمَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْنَا وَمَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْكُمْ، وَإِلَهُنَا وَإِلَهُكُمْ وَاحِدٌ، وَنَحْنُ لَهُ مُسْلِمُونَ". وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ تفرَّد بِهِ الْبُخَارِيُّ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عُثْمَانُ بْنُ عُمَر، أَخْبَرَنَا يُونُسُ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، أَخْبَرَنِي ابْنُ أَبِي نَمْلَةَ أَنَّ أَبَا نَمْلَةَ الْأَنْصَارِيَّ أَخْبَرَهُ، أَنَّهُ بَيْنَمَا هُوَ جَالِسٌ عِنْدَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، جَاءَهُ رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْيَهُودِ، فَقَالَ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، هَلْ تَتَكَلَّمُ هَذِهِ الْجِنَازَةُ؟ قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "اللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ". قَالَ الْيَهُودِيُّ: أَنَا أَشْهَدُ أَنَّهَا تَتَكَلَّمُ. فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِذَا حَدَّثَكُمْ أَهْلُ الْكِتَابِ فَلَا تُصَدِّقُوهُمْ وَلَا تُكَذِّبُوهُمْ، وَقُولُوا: آمَنَّا بِاللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ وَكُتُبِهِ، فَإِنْ كَانَ حَقًّا لَمْ تُكَذِّبُوهُمْ، وَإِنْ كَانَ بَاطِلًا لَمْ تُصَدِّقُوهُمْ" 

قَلَّتْ: وَأَبُو نَمْلَةَ هَذَا هُوَ: عُمَارة. وَقِيلَ: عَمَّارٌ. وَقِيلَ: عَمْرُو بْنُ مُعَاذِ بْنِ زُرَارة الْأَنْصَارِيُّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ.

ثُمَّ لِيُعْلَمَ أَنَّ أَكْثَرَ مَا يُحدّثون بِهِ غالبُه كَذِبٌ وَبُهْتَانٌ؛ لِأَنَّهُ قَدْ دَخَلَهُ تَحْرِيفٌ وَتَبْدِيلٌ وَتَغْيِيرٌ وَتَأْوِيلٌ، وَمَا أَقَلَّ الصِّدْقَ فِيهِ، ثُمَّ مَا أَقَلَّ فَائِدَةَ كَثِيرٍ مِنْهُ لَوْ كَانَ صَحِيحًا.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ بَشَّارٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَاصِمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنْ سُلَيْمَانَ بْنِ عَامِرٍ، عَنْ عُمَارَةَ بْنِ عُمَيْرٍ، عَنْ حُرَيْث بْنِ ظُهَيْرٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ -هُوَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ -قَالَ: لَا تَسْأَلُوا أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ عَنْ شَيْءٍ، فَإِنَّهُمْ لَنْ يَهْدُوكُمْ وَقَدْ ضَلُّوا، إِمَّا أَنْ تُكَذِّبُوا بِحَقٍّ أَوْ تُصَدِّقُوا بِبَاطِلٍ، فَإِنَّهُ لَيْسَ أَحَدٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ إِلَّا وَفِي قَلْبِهِ تَالِيَةٌ، تَدْعُوهُ إِلَى دِينِهِ كَتَالِيَةِ الْمَالِ .

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا مُوسَى بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، أَخْبَرَنَا ابْنِ شِهَابٍ، عَنْ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: كَيْفَ تَسْأَلُونَ أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ عَنْ شَيْءٍ، وَكِتَابُكُمُ الَّذِي أُنْزِلَ عَلَى رَسُولِهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عليه وسلم أحدث تقرؤونه مَحْضًا لَمْ يُشَب، وَقَدْ حدَثَكم أَنَّ أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ بدَّلوا كِتَابَ اللَّهِ، وَغَيَّرُوهُ وَكَتَبُوا بِأَيْدِيهِمُ الْكِتَابَ، وَقَالُوا: هُوَ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ، لِيَشْتَرُوا بِهِ ثَمَنًا قَلِيلًا؟ أَلَا يَنْهَاكُمْ مَا جَاءَكُمْ مِنَ الْعِلْمِ عَنْ مَسْأَلَتِهِمْ؟ لَا وَاللَّهِ مَا رَأَيْنَا مِنْهُمْ رَجُلًا يَسْأَلُكُمْ عَنِ الَّذِي أُنْزِلَ عليكم .

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: وَقَالَ أَبُو الْيَمَانِ: أَخْبَرَنَا شُعَيْبٌ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، أَخْبَرَنِي حُمَيد بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ: أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ مُعَاوِيَةَ يُحَدِّثُ رَهْطًا مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ بِالْمَدِينَةِ -وذكرَ كعبَ الْأَحْبَارِ -فَقَالَ: إِنْ كَانَ مِنْ أَصْدَقِ هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُحَدِّثِينَ الَّذِينَ يُحَدِّثُونَ عَنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ، وَإِنْ كُنَّا مَعَ ذَلِكَ لَنَبْلُو عَلَيْهِ الْكَذِبَ .

قُلْتُ: مَعْنَاهُ أَنَّهُ يَقَعُ مِنْهُ الْكَذِبُ لُغَةً مِنْ غَيْرِ قَصْدٍ؛ لِأَنَّهُ يُحَدِّثُ عَنْ صُحُفٍ هُوَ يُحْسِنُ بِهَا الظَّنَّ، وَفِيهَا أَشْيَاءُ مَوْضُوعَةٌ وَمَكْذُوبَةٌ؛ لِأَنَّهُمْ لَمْ يَكُنْ فِي مِلَّتِهِمْ حُفَّاظٌ مُتْقِنُونَ كَهَذِهِ الْأُمَّةِ الْعَظِيمَةِ، وَمَعَ ذَلِكَ وَقُرْبَ الْعَهْدِ وُضِعَتْ أَحَادِيثُ كَثِيرَةٌ فِي هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةِ، لَا يَعْلَمُهَا إِلَّا اللَّهُ وَمَنْ مَنَحَهُ اللَّهُ عِلْمًا بِذَلِكَ، كُلٌّ بِحَسْبِهِ، وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ وَالْمِنَّةُ.

---

## 29:47-49 — verses 47-49 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Ibn Jarir said: God Most High is saying: just as We sent down the Books upon those before you, O Muhammad, from among the messengers, likewise We have sent down to you this Book.

What he has said here is sound, and forms a good connection and relation.

His saying, {So those to whom We gave the Book believe in it}, means: those who took it and recited it with its due recitation, from among their scholars, the learned and discerning ones, like Abdullah ibn Salam, Salman al-Farisi, and those like them.

His saying, {And among these there are those who believe in it}, refers to the Arabs, from Quraysh and others. {And none reject Our signs except the disbelievers}, meaning: none deny them and reject their truth except one who conceals the truth with falsehood and tries to cover the light of the sun with thin veils, and how far from possible that is.

Then God Most High said: {And you did not recite before it any book, nor did you inscribe one with your right hand}, meaning: you remained among your people, O Muhammad, before bringing this Qur'an, for a lifetime during which you did not read any book nor were you skilled in writing. Rather, everyone among your people and others knew that you were an unlettered man who could neither read nor write. Such was his description in the earlier Books, as God Most High said: {Those who follow the Messenger, the unlettered Prophet, whom they find written down with them in the Torah and the Gospel, who commands them to what is right and forbids them from what is wrong} [al-A'raf: 157]. And so it was: the prayers and peace of God be upon him always, forever, until the Day of Resurrection, he was not skilled in writing, nor did he trace a single line or letter with his own hand. Rather, he had scribes who wrote down the revelation and the letters to the various regions in front of him.

As for those among the later jurists, such as Qadi Abu al-Walid al-Baji and those who followed him, who claimed that he, peace be upon him, wrote on the Day of Hudaybiyyah: "This is what Muhammad ibn Abdullah has agreed to," what led him to that was a narration in Sahih al-Bukhari: "then he took it and wrote," but this is to be understood in light of the other narration: "then he commanded, and it was written." For this reason, strong condemnation arose among the jurists of the Maghrib and the Mashriq against whoever adopted al-Baji's view, and they disassociated themselves from him, and composed verses about it and delivered sermons about it in their gatherings. What the man, meaning al-Baji, apparently intended, was that he wrote that as a miraculous sign, not that he was actually skilled in writing, just as he, peace and blessings be upon him, said concerning the Dajjal: "Written between his eyes is 'disbeliever,'" and in another narration: "K-F-R, every believer will read it." And what some have cited as a hadith, that he, peace be upon him, did not die until he had learned to write, is weak and has no basis. God Most High said: {And you did not recite}, meaning: you did not read, {before it any book}, for emphasis of the negation, {nor did you inscribe one with your right hand}, also for emphasis, and this is expressed in the manner of what is usual, like His saying: {nor any bird that flies with its two wings} [al-An'am: 38].

His saying, {In that case the falsifiers would have doubted}, means: had you been skilled in writing, some of the ignorant among the people would have doubted, and would have said: he only learned this from books before him, transmitted from the prophets, even though they said that while knowing that he was unlettered and could not write: {And they say, "Legends of the ancients that he has had written down, so they are dictated to him morning and evening"} [al-Furqan: 5]. God Most High said: {Say, "It has been sent down by He who knows the secret in the heavens and the earth. Indeed, He is ever Forgiving, Merciful"} [al-Furqan: 6]. And He said here: {Rather, it is clear signs in the breasts of those who have been given knowledge}, meaning: this Qur'an consists of clear, evident signs pointing to the truth, in command, prohibition, and report, which the scholars memorize. God has made it easy for them to memorize, recite, and interpret, just as He said: {And We have certainly made the Qur'an easy for remembrance, so is there any who will remember?} [al-Qamar: 17]. The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "There is no prophet but that he was given something the like of which people came to believe in. What I was given was revelation which God revealed to me, so I hope that I will be the one with the most followers among them."

In the hadith of Iyad ibn Himar, in Sahih Muslim: "God Most High says: I am about to try you, and try others through you, and I am about to send down upon you a Book which water cannot wash away, which you will recite sleeping and waking." That is: even if water were to wash the place in which it was written, there would be no need for that physical place, as it comes in another hadith: "If the Qur'an were in a piece of leather, fire would not burn it," because it is preserved in the breasts, made easy upon the tongues, and dominant over the hearts, miraculous in wording and meaning. For this reason it comes in the earlier Books, in the description of this community: "Their gospels are in their breasts."

Ibn Jarir preferred the view that the meaning of His saying, {Rather, it is clear signs in the breasts of those who have been given knowledge}, is: rather, the knowledge that you did not recite, before this Book, any book, nor did you inscribe one with your right hand, is clear signs in the breasts of those given knowledge from among the People of the Book. He transmitted this from Qatadah and Ibn Jurayj, and related the first view from al-Hasan al-Basri alone.

I say: this is what al-Awfi narrated from Abdullah ibn Abbas, and it is what al-Dahhak said, and it is the more apparent view. God knows best.

His saying, {And none reject Our signs except the wrongdoers}, means: none denies them, diminishes their due right, and rejects them except the wrongdoers, meaning the transgressors, the arrogant, those who know the truth yet turn away from it, as God Most High said: {Indeed, those upon whom the word of your Lord has come into effect will not believe. Even if every sign should come to them, until they see the painful punishment} [Yunus: 96-97].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: كَمَا أَنْزَلْنَا الكُتُب عَلَى مَنْ قَبْلَكَ -يَا مُحَمَّدُ -مِنَ الرُّسُلِ، كَذَلِكَ أَنْزَلْنَا إِلَيْكَ هَذَا الْكِتَابَ.

وَهَذَا الَّذِي قَالَهُ حَسَنٌ وَمُنَاسَبَةٌ وَارْتِبَاطٌ جَيِّدٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَالَّذِينَ آتَيْنَاهُمُ الْكِتَابَ يُؤْمِنُونَ بِهِ﴾ أَيِ: الَّذِينَ أَخَذُوهُ فتلَوْه حَقَّ تِلَاوَتِهِ مِنْ أَحْبَارِهِمُ الْعُلَمَاءِ الْأَذْكِيَاءِ، كَعَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ سَلَامٍ، وَسَلْمَانَ الْفَارِسِيِّ، وَأَشْبَاهِهِمَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمِنْ هَؤُلاءِ مَنْ يُؤْمِنُ بِهِ﴾ ، يَعْنِي الْعَرَبَ مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ وَغَيْرِهِمْ، ﴿وَمَا يَجْحَدُ بِآيَاتِنَا إِلا الْكَافِرُونَ﴾ ، أَيْ: مَا يُكَذِّبُ بِهَا وَيَجْحَدُ حَقَّهَا إِلَّا مَنْ يَسْتُرُ الْحَقَّ بِالْبَاطِلِ، وَيُغَطِّي ضَوْءَ الشَّمْسِ بِالْوَصَائِلِ، وَهَيْهَاتَ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا كُنْتَ تَتْلُو مِنْ قَبْلِهِ مِنْ كِتَابٍ وَلا تَخُطُّهُ بِيَمِينِكَ﴾ ، أَيْ: قَدْ لَبِثْتَ فِي قَوْمِكَ -يَا مُحَمَّدُ -وَمِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ تَأْتِيَ بِهَذَا الْقُرْآنِ عُمرا لَا تَقْرَأُ كِتَابًا وَلَا تُحْسِنُ الْكِتَابَةَ، بَلْ كُلُّ أَحَدٍ مِنْ قَوْمِكَ وَغَيْرِهِمْ يَعْرِفُ أَنَّكَ رَجُلٌ أُمِّيٌّ لَا تَقْرَأُ وَلَا تَكْتُبُ . وَهَكَذَا صِفَتُهُ فِي الْكُتُبِ الْمُتَقَدِّمَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿الَّذِينَ يَتَّبِعُونَ الرَّسُولَ النَّبِيَّ الأمِّيَّ الَّذِي يَجِدُونَهُ مَكْتُوبًا عِنْدَهُمْ فِي التَّوْرَاةِ وَالإنْجِيلِ يَأْمُرُهُمْ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ وَيَنْهَاهُمْ عَنِ الْمُنْكَرِ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٥٧] . وَهَكَذَا كَانَ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ [دَائِمًا أَبَدًا] إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ ، لَا يُحْسِنُ الْكِتَابَةَ وَلَا يَخُطُّ سَطْرًا وَلَا حَرْفًا بِيَدِهِ، بَلْ كَانَ لَهُ كُتَّابٌ يَكْتُبُونَ بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ الْوَحْيَ وَالرَّسَائِلَ إِلَى الْأَقَالِيمِ. وَمَنْ زَعَمَ مِنْ مُتَأَخَّرِي الْفُقَهَاءِ، كَالْقَاضِي أَبِي الْوَلِيدِ الْبَاجِيِّ وَمَنْ تَابَعَهُ أَنَّهُ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ ، كَتَبَ يَوْمَ الْحُدَيْبِيَةِ: "هَذَا مَا قَاضَى عَلَيْهِ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ" فَإِنَّمَا حَمَلَهُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ رِوَايَةٌ فِي صَحِيحِ الْبُخَارِيِّ: "ثُمَّ أَخَذَ فَكَتَبَ": وَهَذِهِ مَحْمُولَةٌ عَلَى الرِّوَايَةِ الْأُخْرَى: "ثُمَّ أَمَرَ فَكَتَبَ". وَلِهَذَا اشْتَدَّ النَّكِيرُ بَيْنَ فُقَهَاءِ الْمَغْرِبِ وَالْمَشْرِقِ على من قال بقول الباجي، وتبرؤوا مِنْهُ، وَأَنْشَدُوا فِي ذَلِكَ أَقْوَالًا وَخَطَبُوا بِهِ فِي مَحَافِلِهِمْ: وَإِنَّمَا أَرَادَ الرَّجُلُ -أَعْنِي الْبَاجِيَّ، فِيمَا يَظْهَرُ عَنْهُ -أَنَّهُ كَتَبَ ذَلِكَ عَلَى وَجْهِ الْمُعْجِزَةِ، لَا أَنَّهُ كَانَ يُحْسِنُ الْكِتَابَةَ، كَمَا قَالَ، عَلَيْهِ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ إِخْبَارًا عَنِ الدَّجَّالِ: "مَكْتُوبٌ بَيْنَ عَيْنَيْهِ كَافِرٌ" وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: "ك ف ر، يَقْرَؤُهَا كُلُّ مُؤْمِنٍ" ، وَمَا أَوْرَدَهُ بَعْضُهُمْ مِنَ الْحَدِيثِ أَنَّهُ لَمْ يَمُتْ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ حَتَّى تَعَلَّمَ الْكِتَابَةَ، فَضَعِيفٌ لَا أَصْلَ لَهُ؛ قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا كُنْتَ تَتْلُو﴾ أَيْ: تَقْرَأُ ﴿مِنْ قَبْلِهِ مِنْ كِتَابٍ﴾ لِتَأْكِيدِ النَّفْيِ، ﴿وَلا تَخُطُّهُ بِيَمِينِكَ﴾ تَأْكِيدٌ أَيْضًا، وَخَرَجَ مَخْرَجَ الْغَالِبِ، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلا طَائِرٍ يَطِيرُ بِجَنَاحَيْهِ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٣٨] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِذًا لارْتَابَ الْمُبْطِلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَوْ كُنْتَ تُحْسِنُهَا لَارْتَابَ بَعْضُ الْجَهَلَةِ مِنَ النَّاسِ فَيَقُولُ: إِنَّمَا تَعَلَّمَ هَذَا مِنْ كُتب قَبْلَهُ مَأْثُورَةٍ عَنِ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ، مَعَ أَنَّهُمْ قَالُوا ذَلِكَ مَعَ عِلْمِهِمْ بِأَنَّهُ أُمِّيٌّ لَا يُحْسِنُ الْكِتَابَةَ: ﴿وَقَالُوا أَسَاطِيرُ الأوَّلِينَ اكْتَتَبَهَا فَهِيَ تُمْلَى عَلَيْهِ بُكْرَةً وَأَصِيلا﴾ [الْفُرْقَانِ: ٥] ،قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلْ أَنزلَهُ الَّذِي يَعْلَمُ السِّرَّ فِي السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ إِنَّهُ كَانَ غَفُورًا رَحِيمًا﴾ [الْفُرْقَانِ: ٦] ، وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿بَلْ هُوَ آيَاتٌ بَيِّنَاتٌ فِي صُدُورِ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْعِلْمَ﴾ أَيْ: [هَذَا] الْقُرْآنُ آيَاتٌ بَيِّنَةٌ وَاضِحَةٌ فِي الدَّلَالَةِ عَلَى الْحَقِّ، أَمْرًا وَنَهْيًا وَخَبَرًا، يَحْفَظُهُ الْعُلَمَاءُ، يَسَّره اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ حِفْظًا وَتِلَاوَةً وَتَفْسِيرًا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ يَسَّرْنَا الْقُرْآنَ لِلذِّكْرِ فَهَلْ مِنْ مُدَّكِرٍ﴾ [الْقَمَرِ: ١٧] ، وَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَا مِنْ نَبِيٍّ إِلَّا وَقَدْ أُعْطِيَ مَا آمَنَ عَلَى مِثْلِهِ الْبَشَرُ وَإِنَّمَا كَانَ الَّذِي أُوتِيتُهُ وَحْيًا أَوْحَاهُ اللَّهُ إليَّ، فَأَرْجُو أَنْ أَكُونَ أَكْثَرَهُمْ تَابِعًا" .

وَفِي حَدِيثِ عِيَاضِ بْنِ حِمَارٍ ، فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ: "يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: إِنِّي مُبْتَلِيكَ وَمُبْتَلٍ بِكَ، وَمُنْزِلٌ عَلَيْكَ كِتَابًا لَا يَغْسِلُهُ الْمَاءُ، تَقْرَؤُهُ نَائِمًا وَيَقْظَانَ" . أَيْ: لَوْ غَسَلَ الْمَاءُ المحلَّ الْمَكْتُوبَ فِيهِ لَمَا احْتِيجَ إِلَى ذَلِكَ الْمَحَلِّ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ الْآخَرِ: "لَوْ كَانَ الْقُرْآنُ فِي إِهَابٍ، مَا أَحْرَقَتْهُ النَّارُ" ، لِأَنَّهُ مَحْفُوظٌ فِي الصُّدُورِ، مُيَسَّرٌ عَلَى الْأَلْسِنَةِ، مُهَيْمِنٌ عَلَى الْقُلُوبِ، مُعْجِزٌ لَفْظًا وَمَعْنَى؛ وَلِهَذَا جَاءَ فِي الْكُتُبِ الْمُتَقَدِّمَةِ، فِي صِفَةِ هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةِ: "أَنَاجِيلُهُمْ فِي صدورهم".

وَاخْتَارَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَنَّ الْمَعْنَى فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿بَلْ هُوَ آيَاتٌ بَيِّنَاتٌ فِي صُدُورِ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْعِلْمَ﴾ ، بَلِ الْعِلْمُ بِأَنَّكَ مَا كُنْتَ تَتْلُو مِنْ قَبْلِ هَذَا الْكِتَابِ كِتَابًا وَلَا تَخُطُّهُ بِيَمِينِكَ، آيَاتٌ بَيِّنَاتٌ فِي صُدُورِ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْعَلَمَ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ . وَنَقَلَهُ عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، وَابْنِ جُرَيْجٍ. وَحَكَى الْأَوَّلَ عَنِ الْحَسَنِ [الْبَصْرِيِّ] فَقَطْ.

قُلْتُ: وَهُوَ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ الْعَوْفِيُّ عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَقَالَهُ الضَّحَّاكُ، وَهُوَ الْأَظْهَرُ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا يَجْحَدُ بِآيَاتِنَا إِلا الظَّالِمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: مَا يُكَذِّبُ بِهَا وَيَبْخَسُ حَقَّهَا وَيَرُدُّهَا إِلَّا الظَّالِمُونَ، أَيِ: الْمُعْتَدُونَ الْمُكَابِرُونَ، الَّذِينَ يَعْلَمُونَ الْحَقَّ وَيَحِيدُونَ عَنْهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ حَقَّتْ عَلَيْهِمْ كَلِمَةُ رَبِّكَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ. وَلَوْ جَاءَتْهُمْ كُلُّ آيَةٍ حَتَّى يَرَوُا الْعَذَابَ الألِيمَ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ٩٦، ٩٧] .

---

## 29:50-52 — verses 50-52 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says, informing about the polytheists in their obstinacy and their demanding of signs, meaning signs that would guide them to the fact that Muhammad is the Messenger of God, just as Salih (peace be upon him) came with his she-camel. God the Exalted says: {Say}, O Muhammad, {The signs are only with God}, meaning: the matter of that rests with God. For if He knew that you would be guided, He would have answered your request, since that is easy for Him, simple in His sight. But He knows from you that your intent is only obstinacy and testing, so He will not grant you that. As He the Exalted said: {And nothing has kept Us from sending the signs except that the former peoples denied them. And We gave Thamud the she-camel as a visible sign, but they wronged themselves through it} [al-Isra: 59].

His saying: {I am only a clear warner}, meaning: I have only been sent as a warner to you, plain in warning. It is upon me to convey to you God's message, and {whomever God guides is the rightly guided, and whomever He leaves astray you will never find for him a guiding protector} [al-Kahf: 17]. And He the Exalted said: {Their guidance is not upon you, but God guides whom He wills} [al-Baqarah: 272].

Then God the Exalted says, clarifying the extent of their ignorance and the feebleness of their minds, in that they demanded signs to indicate to them the truthfulness of Muhammad in what he brought them, when he had already brought them the Mighty Book, which falsehood cannot approach from before it or behind it, a revelation from One who is Wise and Praiseworthy, which is greater than every miracle, since the most eloquent and articulate of speakers were powerless to match it, indeed powerless to match even ten surahs like it, indeed powerless to match even a single surah of it. So He the Exalted said: {Is it not sufficient for them that We have sent down to you the Book which is recited to them?}, meaning: is it not sufficient for them as a sign that We sent down to you this magnificent Book, which contains news of what came before them, tidings of what comes after them, and judgment concerning what is between them, while you are an unlettered man who can neither read nor write, and who never mixed with any of the People of the Book? Yet you brought them news of what is in the earlier scriptures, with a clarification of the truth concerning that over which they differed, and with the clear, manifest, evident truth. As He the Exalted said: {Was it not a sign for them that the scholars of the Children of Israel recognized it?} [al-Shu'ara: 197]. And He the Exalted said: {And they say, "Why does he not bring us a sign from his Lord?" Has there not come to them clear evidence of what is in the earlier scriptures?} [Ta Ha: 133].

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said, "There is no prophet among the prophets except that he was given signs the like of which people believed in. What I was given was only revelation which God revealed to me, so I hope that I will be the one with the most followers on the Day of Resurrection." Both [al-Bukhari and Muslim] narrated it from the hadith of Layth.

God the Exalted said: {Indeed in that is a mercy and a reminder for a people who believe}, meaning: indeed in this Qur'an is {a mercy}, that is, a clarification of the truth and a dispelling of falsehood, and {a reminder}, by what it contains of the descending of afflictions and the falling of punishment upon those who deny and those who disobey. {A mercy and a reminder for a people who believe}.

Then He the Exalted said: Say, {Sufficient is God as a witness between me and you}, meaning: He knows best what you engage in of denial, and He knows what I say to you in informing you on His behalf, that He has sent me. For if I were lying against Him, He would have taken vengeance upon me, as He the Exalted said: {And if he had attributed to Us some fabricated sayings, We would have seized him by the right hand, then We would have cut off his life vein, and not one of you could have held Us back from him} [al-Haqqah: 44-47]. Rather, I am truthful concerning Him in what I have informed you, and it is for this reason that He has supported me with clear miracles and decisive proofs.

{He knows what is in the heavens and the earth}, meaning: no hidden thing is concealed from Him.

{And those who believe in falsehood and disbelieve in God, those are the losers}, meaning: on the Day of their Return He will requite them for what they did, and repay them for what they wrought, of their denial of the truth and their following of falsehood. They denied the messengers of God despite the establishment of proofs of their truthfulness, and they believed in false gods and idols without any proof. He will requite them for that. Indeed, He is Wise, All-Knowing.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ فِي تَعَنُّتِهِمْ وَطَلَبِهِمْ آيَاتٍ -يَعْنُونَ -تُرْشِدُهُمْ إِلَى أَنَّ مُحَمَّدًا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ كَمَا جَاءَ صَالِحٌ بِنَاقَتِهِ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلْ﴾ يَا مُحَمَّدُ: ﴿إِنَّمَا الآيَاتُ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّمَا أَمْرُ ذَلِكَ إِلَى اللَّهِ، فَإِنَّهُ لَوْ عَلِمَ أَنَّكُمْ تَهْتَدُونَ لَأَجَابَكُمْ إِلَى سُؤَالِكُمْ؛ لَأَنَّ ذَلِكَ سَهْلٌ عَلَيْهِ، يَسِيرٌ لَدَيْهِ، وَلَكِنَّهُ يَعْلَمُ مِنْكُمْ أَنَّمَا قَصْدُكُمُ التَّعَنُّتُ وَالِامْتِحَانُ، فَلَا يُجِيبُكُمْ إِلَى ذَلِكَ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا مَنَعَنَا أَنْ نُرْسِلَ بِالآيَاتِ إِلا أَنْ كَذَّبَ بِهَا الأوَّلُونَ وَآتَيْنَا ثَمُودَ النَّاقَةَ مُبْصِرَةً فَظَلَمُوا بِهَا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٥٩] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنَّمَا أَنَا نَذِيرٌ مُبِينٌ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّمَا بُعِثْتُ نَذِيرًا لَكُمْ بَيِّنَ النِّذَارَةِ فَعَليَّ أَنْ أُبَلِّغَكُمْ رِسَالَةَ اللَّهِ وَ ﴿مَنْ يَهْدِ اللَّهُ فَهُوَ الْمُهْتَدِ وَمَنْ يُضْلِلْ فَلَنْ تَجِدَ لَهُ وَلِيًّا مُرْشِدًا﴾ [الْكَهْفِ: ١٧] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَيْسَ عَلَيْكَ هُدَاهُمْ وَلَكِنَّ اللَّهَ يَهْدِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٧٢] .

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى مُبَيِّنًا كَثْرَةَ جَهْلِهِمْ، وَسَخَافَةَ عَقْلِهِمْ، حَيْثُ طَلَبُوا آيَاتٍ تَدُلُّهُمْ عَلَى صِدْقِ مُحَمَّدٍ فِيمَا جَاءَهُمْ [بِهِ] -وَقَدْ جَاءَهُمْ بِالْكِتَابِ الْعَزِيزِ الَّذِي لَا يَأْتِيهِ الْبَاطِلُ مِنْ بَيْنِ يَدَيْهِ، وَلَا مِنْ خَلْفِهِ تَنْزِيلٌ مِنْ حَكِيمٍ حَمِيدٍ، الَّذِي هُوَ أَعْظَمُ مِنْ كُلِّ مُعْجِزَةٍ، إِذْ عَجَزَتِ الْفُصَحَاءُ وَالْبُلَغَاءُ عَنْ مُعَارَضَتِهِ، بَلْ عَنْ مُعَارَضَةِ عَشْرِ سُورٍ مِنْ مَثَلِهِ، بَلْ عَنْ مُعَارَضَةِ سُورَةٍ مِنْهُ -فَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَكْفِهِمْ أَنَّا أَنزلْنَا عَلَيْكَ الْكِتَابَ يُتْلَى عَلَيْهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: أَوْلَمَ يَكْفِهِمْ آيَةً أَنَّا أَنْزَلْنَا عَلَيْكَ هَذَا الْكِتَابَ الْعَظِيمَ، الَّذِي فِيهِ خَبَرُ مَا قَبْلَهُمْ، وَنَبَأُ مَا بَعْدَهُمْ، وَحُكْمُ مَا بَيْنَهُمْ، وَأَنْتَ رَجُلٌ أُمِّيٌّ لَا تَقْرَأُ وَلَا تَكْتُبُ، وَلَمْ تُخَالِطْ أَحَدًا مِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ، فَجِئْتَهُمْ بِأَخْبَارِ مَا فِي الصُّحُفِ الْأُولَى، بِبَيَانِ الصَّوَابِ مِمَّا اخْتَلَفُوا فِيهِ، وَبِالْحَقِّ الْوَاضِحِ الْبَيِّنِ الْجَلِيِّ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُمْ آيَةً أَنْ يَعْلَمَهُ عُلَمَاءُ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ﴾ [الشُّعَرَاءِ: ١٩٧] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَقَالُوا لَوْلا يَأْتِينَا بِآيَةٍ مِنْ رَبِّهِ أَوَلَمْ تَأْتِهِمْ بَيِّنَةُ مَا فِي الصُّحُفِ الأولَى﴾ [طَهَ: ١٣٣] .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا حَجَّاجٌ، حَدَّثَنَا لَيْثٌ، حَدَّثَنِي سَعِيدُ بن أبي سعيد، عَنْ أَبِيهِ عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عليه وسلم: "ما من الْأَنْبِيَاءِ مِنْ نَبِيٍّ إِلَّا قَدْ أُعْطِيَ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ مَا مِثْلُهُ آمَنَ عَلَيْهِ الْبَشَرُ، وَإِنَّمَا كَانَ الَّذِي أُوتِيتُهُ وَحْيًا أَوْحَاهُ اللَّهُ إِلَيَّ، فَأَرْجُو أَنْ أَكُونَ أَكْثَرَهُمْ تَابِعًا يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ". أَخْرَجَاهُ مِنْ حَدِيثِ اللَّيْثِ .

وَقَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ فِي ذَلِكَ لَرَحْمَةً وَذِكْرَى لِقَوْمٍ يُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّ فِي هَذَا الْقُرْآنِ: ﴿لَرَحْمَةً﴾ أَيْ: بَيَانًا لِلْحَقِّ، وَإِزَاحَةً لِلْبَاطِلِ وَ ﴿ذِكْرَى﴾ بِمَا فِيهِ حُلُولُ النِّقَمَاتِ وَنُزُولُ الْعِقَابِ بِالْمُكَذِّبِينَ وَالْعَاصِينَ، ﴿لَرَحْمَةً وَذِكْرَى لِقَوْمٍ يُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ .

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: قُلْ: ﴿كَفَى بِاللَّهِ بَيْنِي وَبَيْنَكُمْ شَهِيدًا﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ أَعْلَمُ بِمَا تُفِيضُونَ فِيهِ مِنَ التَّكْذِيبِ، وَيَعْلَمُ مَا أَقُولُ لَكُمْ مِنْ إِخْبَارِي عَنْهُ، بِأَنَّهُ أَرْسَلَنِي، فَلَوْ كُنْتُ كَاذِبًا عَلَيْهِ لَانْتَقَمَ مِنِّي، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ تَقَوَّلَ عَلَيْنَا بَعْضَ الأقَاوِيلِ. لأخَذْنَا مِنْهُ بِالْيَمِينِ. ثُمَّ لَقَطَعْنَا مِنْهُ الْوَتِينَ. فَمَا مِنْكُمْ مِنْ أَحَدٍ عَنْهُ حَاجِزِينَ﴾ [الْحَاقَّةِ: ٤٤-٤٧] ، وَإِنَّمَا أَنَا صَادِقٌ عَلَيْهِ فِيمَا أَخْبَرْتُكُمْ بِهِ، وَلِهَذَا أَيَّدَنِي بِالْمُعْجِزَاتِ الْوَاضِحَاتِ، وَالدَّلَائِلِ الْقَاطِعَاتِ.

﴿يَعْلَمُ مَا فِي السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ [أَيْ] : لَا تَخْفَى عَلَيْهِ خَافِيَةٌ.

﴿وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا بِالْبَاطِلِ وَكَفَرُوا بِاللَّهِ أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْخَاسِرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ مَعَادِهِمْ سَيَجْزِيهِمْ عَلَى مَا فَعَلُوا، وَيُقَابِلُهُمْ عَلَى مَا صَنَعُوا، مِنْ تَكْذِيبِهِمْ بِالْحَقِّ وَاتِّبَاعِهِمُ الْبَاطِلَ، كَذَّبُوا بِرُسُلِ اللَّهِ مَعَ قِيَامِ الْأَدِلَّةِ عَلَى صِدْقِهِمْ، وَآمَنُوا بِالطَّوَاغِيتِ وَالْأَوْثَانِ بِلَا دَلِيلٍ، سَيُجَازِيهِمْ على ذلك، إنه حكيم عليم.

---

## 29:53-55 — verses 53-55 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says, informing of the ignorance of the polytheists in their seeking to hasten the punishment of God to befall them, and the might of God to descend upon them, as He, the Exalted, said: {And when they said, "O God, if this is indeed the truth from You, then rain down upon us stones from the sky or bring us a painful punishment"} [al-Anfal: 32]. And He said here: {And they seek to hasten you with the punishment. And if not for a specified term, the punishment would have come to them}, meaning: were it not for what God has decreed of delaying the punishment until the Day of Resurrection, the punishment would have come to them near and swift, just as they sought to hasten it.

Then He said: {And it will surely come to them suddenly}, that is, unexpectedly, {while they do not perceive. They seek to hasten you with the punishment, and indeed Hell will surely encompass the disbelievers}, meaning: they seek to hasten the punishment, while it will inevitably befall them.

Shu'bah said, from Simak, from Ikrimah, regarding His saying: {And indeed Hell will surely encompass the disbelievers}, he said: it is the sea.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ali ibn al-Husayn told us... Umar ibn Isma'il ibn Mujalid told us, my father told us, from Mujalid, from al-Sha'bi, that he heard Ibn Abbas say: {And indeed Hell will surely encompass the disbelievers}: Hell is this green sea. The stars are scattered into it, and the sun and moon are rolled up into it, then it is kindled and becomes Hell.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Asim told us, Abdullah ibn Umayyah told us, Muhammad ibn Huyay told me, Safwan ibn Ya'la told us, from his father, that the Prophet ﷺ said: "The sea, it is Hell." They said this to Ya'la, so he said: Do you not see that God says: {A fire whose walls will encompass them} [al-Kahf: 29]? He said: No, by the One in whose hand is the soul of Ya'la, I will never enter it until I am presented before God, and not a drop of it will touch me until I am presented before God, Mighty and Majestic.

This is a gharib (singular) interpretation, and a hadith that is extremely gharib (singular). And God knows best.

Then the Exalted said: {On the Day the punishment will cover them from above them and from beneath their feet}, similar to His saying, the Exalted: {For them is a resting place of Hell, and over them coverings} [al-A'raf: 41], and He said: {For them are canopies of fire from above them and from below them, canopies} [al-Zumar: 16], and He said: {If only those who disbelieved knew the time when they will not avert the fire from their faces or from their backs} [al-Anbiya: 39]. So the fire covers them from every direction, and this is more emphatic in the sensory punishment.

His saying: {And He will say, "Taste what you used to do"} is a threat, a rebuke, and a reproach, and this is a punishment upon the souls in meaning, similar to His saying: {The Day they are dragged into the Fire upon their faces, "Taste the touch of Saqar. Indeed, all things We created with predestination"} [al-Qamar: 48-49]. And He said: {The Day they are pushed toward the fire of Hell with a violent push. "This is the Fire which you used to deny. Then is this magic, or do you not see? Burn in it, and whether you are patient or impatient, it is all the same for you. You are only being recompensed for what you used to do"} [al-Tur: 13-16].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ جَهْلِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ فِي اسْتِعْجَالِهِمْ عَذَابَ اللَّهِ أَنْ يَقَعَ بِهِمْ، وَبَأْسَ اللَّهِ أَنْ يَحِلَّ عَلَيْهِمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِذْ قَالُوا اللَّهُمَّ إِنْ كَانَ هَذَا هُوَ الْحَقَّ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ فَأَمْطِرْ عَلَيْنَا حِجَارَةً مِنَ السَّمَاءِ أَوِ ائْتِنَا بِعَذَابٍ أَلِيمٍ﴾ [الْأَنْفَالِ: ٣٢] ، وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿وَيَسْتَعْجِلُونَكَ بِالْعَذَابِ وَلَوْلا أَجَلٌ مُسَمًّى لَجَاءَهُمُ الْعَذَابُ﴾ أَيْ: لَوْلَا مَا حَتَّم اللَّهُ مِنْ تَأْخِيرِ الْعَذَابِ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ لَجَاءَهُمُ الْعَذَابُ قَرِيبًا سَرِيعًا كَمَا اسْتَعْجَلُوهُ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿وَلَيَأْتِيَنَّهُمْ بَغْتَةً﴾ أَيْ: فَجْأَةً، ﴿وَهُمْ لَا يَشْعُرُونَ. يَسْتَعْجِلُونَكَ بِالْعَذَابِ وَإِنَّ جَهَنَّمَ لَمُحِيطَةٌ بِالْكَافِرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: يَسْتَعْجِلُونَ بِالْعَذَابِ، وَهُوَ وَاقِعٌ بِهِمْ لَا مَحَالَةَ.

قَالَ شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ سِمَاك، عَنْ عِكْرِمة قَالَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَإِنَّ جَهَنَّمَ لَمُحِيطَةٌ بِالْكَافِرِينَ﴾ ، قَالَ: الْبَحْرُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ. حَدَّثَنَا عُمَرُ بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ مُجَالِدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي عَنْ مُجَالِدٍ، عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ؛ أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ يَقُولُ: ﴿وَإِنَّ جَهَنَّمَ لَمُحِيطَةٌ بِالْكَافِرِينَ﴾ : وَجَهَنَّمُ هُوَ هَذَا الْبَحْرُ الْأَخْضَرُ، تُنْتَثَرُ الْكَوَاكِبُ فِيهِ، وتُكور فِيهِ الشَّمْسُ وَالْقَمَرُ، ثُمَّ يُسْتَوْقَدُ فَيَكُونُ هُوَ جَهَنَّمَ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَاصِمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أُمَيَّةَ، حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ حُيَي، حَدَّثَنَا صَفْوَانُ بْنُ يَعْلَى، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ قَالَ: "الْبَحْرُ هُوَ جَهَنَّمُ". قَالُوا: لِيَعْلَى، فَقَالَ: أَلَا تَرَوْنَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ يَقُولُ: ﴿نَارًا أَحَاطَ بِهِمْ سُرَادِقُهَا﴾ [الْكَهْفِ: ٢٩] ، قَالَ: لَا وَالَّذِي نَفْسُ يَعْلَى بِيَدِهِ لَا أَدْخُلُهَا أَبَدًا حَتَّى أُعْرَضَ عَلَى اللَّهِ، وَلَا يُصِيبُنِي مِنْهَا قَطْرَةٌ حَتَّى أُعْرَضَ عَلَى اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ .

هَذَا تَفْسِيرٌ غَرِيبٌ، وَحَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ جِدًّا، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ يَغْشَاهُمُ الْعَذَابُ مِنْ فَوْقِهِمْ وَمِنْ تَحْتِ أَرْجُلِهِمْ﴾ ، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَهُمْ مِنْ جَهَنَّمَ مِهَادٌ وَمِنْ فَوْقِهِمْ غَوَاشٍ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٤١] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿لَهُمْ مِنْ فَوْقِهِمْ ظُلَلٌ مِنَ النَّارِ وَمِنْ تَحْتِهِمْ ظُلَلٌ﴾ [الزُّمَرِ: ١٦] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿لَوْ يَعْلَمُ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا حِينَ لَا يَكُفُّونَ عَنْ وُجُوهِهِمُ النَّارَ وَلا عَنْ ظُهُورِهِمْ﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ: ٣٩] ، فَالنَّارُ تَغْشَاهُمْ مِنْ سَائِرِ جِهَاتِهِمْ، وَهَذَا أَبْلَغُ فِي الْعَذَابِ الْحِسِّيِّ.

* *
