وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَيَقُولُ ذُوقُوا مَا كُنْتُمْ تَعْمَلُونَ﴾ ، تَهْدِيدٌ وَتَقْرِيعٌ وَتَوْبِيخٌ، وَهَذَا عَذَابٌ مَعْنَوِيٌّ عَلَى النُّفُوسِ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿يَوْمَ يُسْحَبُونَ فِي النَّارِ عَلَى وُجُوهِهِمْ ذُوقُوا مَسَّ سَقَرَ. إِنَّا كُلَّ شَيْءٍ خَلَقْنَاهُ بِقَدَرٍ﴾ [الْقَمَرِ: ٤٨، ٤٩] ، وَقَالَ ﴿يَوْمَ يُدَعُّونَ إِلَى نَارِ جَهَنَّمَ دَعًّا. هَذِهِ النَّارُ الَّتِي كُنْتُمْ بِهَا تُكَذِّبُونَ. أَفَسِحْرٌ هَذَا أَمْ أَنْتُمْ لَا تُبْصِرُونَ. اصْلَوْهَا فَاصْبِرُوا أَوْ لَا تَصْبِرُوا سَوَاءٌ عَلَيْكُمْ إِنَّمَا تُجْزَوْنَ مَا كُنْتُمْ تَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [الطور: ١٣-١٦] .

---

## 29:56-60 — verses 56-60 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is a command from Allah to His believing servants to migrate from a land in which they cannot establish the religion, to the vast earth of Allah, where establishing the religion becomes possible, by affirming the oneness of Allah and worshiping Him as He has commanded them. Hence He said: {O My servants who believe, indeed My earth is vast, so worship Me alone}.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Yahya, the freedman of al-Zubayr ibn al-Awwam, said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The lands are the lands of Allah, and the servants are the servants of Allah, so wherever you find good, settle there."

For this reason, when their situation in Mecca became too constrained for the oppressed believers to remain there, they went out migrating to the land of Abyssinia, so that they might be safe there for their religion. There they found the better of the two dwellings: Ashamah al-Najashi, the king of Abyssinia, may Allah have mercy on him, sheltered them and supported them with his aid, and made them respected residents in his land. Then after that, the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and the rest of his companions migrated to the Prophetic city, purified Yathrib, Medina. Then He said: {Every soul will taste death, then to Us you will be returned}, meaning: wherever you may be, death will overtake you, so be in obedience to Allah and wherever Allah commands you, for that is better for you. Death is inevitable and there is no escaping it. Then to Allah is the return and the final destination. Whoever is obedient to Him, He will reward him with the best reward and grant him the most complete recompense. Hence He said: {And those who believe and do righteous deeds, We will surely settle them in lofty dwellings of Paradise beneath which rivers flow}, meaning: We will surely house them in elevated dwellings in Paradise, beneath which rivers flow, of various kinds, water, wine, honey, and milk, which they direct and channel wherever they wish, {abiding therein eternally}, meaning: remaining there forever, never desiring to leave it, {excellent is the reward of the workers}: excellent are these dwellings as a reward for the deeds of the believers.

{Those who are patient}, meaning: patient upon their religion, who migrated to Allah, who cast off their enemies, and who separated from their families and relatives, seeking the countenance of Allah, hoping for what is with Him, and believing in His promise.

Ibn Abi Hatim, may Allah have mercy on him, said: [chain] Abu Malik al-Ash'ari related to him that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ told him: "In Paradise there are chambers whose outside can be seen from the inside, and whose inside can be seen from the outside, which Allah has prepared for one who feeds people food, speaks good words, observes fasting freely, and prays at night while people are asleep."

His saying: {and upon their Lord they rely}, in all their states, in their religion and their worldly affairs.

Then He, exalted, informs them that provision is not confined to a particular locality. Rather, His provision, exalted is He, is general for His creation wherever they are and wherever they may be. Indeed, the provisions of the emigrants, in the places to which they emigrated, were more abundant, more expansive, and more wholesome, for after a short time they became the rulers of the lands in all regions and cities. Hence He said: {And how many a creature carries not its own provision}, meaning: it is not able to gather and acquire it, nor does it hold anything back for tomorrow, {Allah provides for it and for you}, meaning: Allah arranges its provision for it despite its weakness, and makes it easy for it. He sends to every creature from provision what sustains it, even to the tiny ant in the depths of the earth, the bird in the air, and the fish in the water. Allah, exalted is He, said: {And there is no creature on earth but that upon Allah is its provision, and He knows its dwelling place and place of storage; all is in a clear register} [Hud: 6].

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ibn Umar said: I went out with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ until he entered one of the walled gardens of Medina, and he began picking dates and eating. He said to me: "O son of Umar, what is wrong with you that you do not eat?" I said: I do not desire it, O Messenger of Allah. He said: "But I desire it, and this is the morning of the fourth day since I have tasted no food and found none, though if I wished I could call upon my Lord and He would give me the like of the kingdom of Caesar and Chosroes. So how will it be with you, O son of Umar, if you remain among a people who store up the provision of their year out of weak certainty?" He said: By Allah, we did not move from our place until there was revealed: {And how many a creature carries not its own provision, Allah provides for it and for you, and He is the Hearing, the Knowing}. Then the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Allah has not commanded me to hoard the world, nor to follow desires. Whoever hoards his worldly wealth desiring thereby a lasting life, then indeed life is in the hand of Allah. Behold, I do not hoard a dinar or a dirham, nor do I store provision for tomorrow."

This is a gharib (singular) hadith, and Abu al-Atuf al-Jazari is weak.

It has been mentioned that when the crow's eggs hatch, its chicks emerge white. When the parents see them like that, they flee from them for some days until the feathers turn black. The chick remains with its mouth open, seeking its parents, so Allah arranges for it small flying insects like gnats which come over it, and it feeds on them during those days until its feathers turn black. Meanwhile the parents check on it constantly; whenever they see it with white feathers they flee from it, but when they see that its feathers have turned black, they turn back to it with care and provision. Hence the poet said:

O Provider of the crow in its nest, and Mender of the broken, shattered bone...

Al-Shafi'i said, in the course of some remarks of his on commands, citing the saying of the Prophet ﷺ: "Travel, that you may be healthy and be provided for."

Al-Bayhaqi said: [chain] Ibn Umar said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Travel, that you may be healthy and gain spoils." He said: We have also related it from Ibn Abbas.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Travel, that you may profit; fast, that you may be healthy; and go out for war, that you may gain spoils."

Something similar to the hadith of Ibn Umar has come from Ibn Abbas as a marfu' (elevated) report, and from Mu'adh ibn Jabal as a mawquf (halted) report. In one wording: "Travel with those of means and ease."

The saying of Allah, exalted is He: {and He is the Hearing, the Knowing}, meaning: Hearing of the words of His servants, Knowing of their movements and their stillness.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا أَمْرٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ لِعِبَادِهِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ بِالْهِجْرَةِ مِنَ الْبَلَدِ الَّذِي لَا يَقْدِرُونَ فِيهِ عَلَى إِقَامَةِ الدِّينِ، إِلَى أَرْضِ اللَّهِ الْوَاسِعَةِ، حَيْثُ يُمْكِنُ إِقَامَةُ الدِّينِ، بِأَنْ يُوَحِّدُوا اللَّهَ وَيَعْبُدُوهُ كَمَا أمرهم؛ ولهذا قال: ﴿يَا عِبَادِيَ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا إِنَّ أَرْضِي وَاسِعَةٌ فَإِيَّايَ فَاعْبُدُونِ﴾ .

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ رَبِّهِ، حَدَّثَنَا بَقِيَّةُ بْنُ الْوَلِيدِ، حَدَّثَنِي جُبَيْر بْنُ عَمْرٍو الْقُرَشِيُّ، حَدَّثَنِي أَبُو سَعْدٍ الْأَنْصَارِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي يَحْيَى مَوْلَى الزُّبَيْرِ بْنِ الْعَوَّامِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "الْبِلَادُ بِلَادُ اللَّهِ، وَالْعِبَادُ عِبَادُ اللَّهِ، فَحَيْثُمَا أصبتَ خَيْرًا فَأَقِمْ" .

وَلِهَذَا لَمَّا ضَاقَ عَلَى الْمُسْتَضْعَفِينَ بِمَكَّةَ مُقَامَهُمْ بِهَا، خَرَجُوا مُهَاجِرِينَ إِلَى أَرْضِ الْحَبَشَةِ، لِيَأْمَنُوا، عَلَى دِينِهِمْ هُنَاكَ، فَوَجَدُوا هُنَاكَ خَيْرَ الْمَنْزِلَيْنِ، أَصْحَمَةَ النَّجَاشِيَّ مَلِكَ الْحَبَشَةِ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، آوَاهُمْ وَأَيَّدَهُمْ بِنَصْرِهِ، وَجَعَلَهُمْ شُيُوما بِبِلَادِهِ. ثُمَّ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ هَاجَرَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَأَصْحَابُهُ الْبَاقُونَ إِلَى المدينة النبوية يثرب المطهرة ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿كُلُّ نَفْسٍ ذَائِقَةُ الْمَوْتِ ثُمَّ إِلَيْنَا تُرْجَعُونَ﴾ أَيْ: أَيْنَمَا كُنْتُمْ يُدْرِكْكُمُ الْمَوْتُ، فَكُونُوا فِي طَاعَةِ اللَّهِ وَحَيْثُ أَمَرَكُمُ اللَّهُ، فَهُوَ خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ، فَإِنَّ الْمَوْتَ لَا بُدَّ مِنْهُ، وَلَا مَحِيدَ عَنْهُ، ثُمَّ إِلَى اللَّهِ الْمَرْجِعُ [وَالْمَآبُ] ، فَمَنْ كَانَ مُطِيعًا لَهُ جَازَاهُ أَفْضَلَ الْجَزَاءِ، وَوَافَاهُ أتمَّ الثَّوَابِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ لَنُبَوِّئَنَّهُمْ مِنَ الْجَنَّةِ غُرَفًا تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الأنْهَارُ﴾ أَيْ: لَنُسْكِنَنَّهُمْ مَنَازِلَ عَالِيَةً فِي الْجَنَّةِ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الْأَنْهَارُ، عَلَى اخْتِلَافِ أَصْنَافِهَا، مِنْ مَاءٍ وَخَمْرٍ، وعسل ولبن، يصرفونها ويجرونها حيث شاؤوا، ﴿خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا﴾ أَيْ: مَاكِثِينَ فِيهَا أَبَدًا لَا يَبْغُونَ عَنْهَا حِوَلًا ﴿نِعْمَ أَجْرُ الْعَامِلِينَ﴾ : نِعْمَتْ هَذِهِ الغرفُ أَجْرًا عَلَى أَعْمَالِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ.

﴿الَّذِينَ صَبَرُوا﴾ أَيْ: عَلَى دِينِهِمْ، وَهَاجَرُوا إِلَى اللَّهِ، وَنَابَذُوا الْأَعْدَاءَ، وَفَارَقُوا الْأَهْلَ وَالْأَقْرِبَاءَ، ابْتِغَاءَ وَجْهِ اللَّهِ، وَرَجَاءَ مَا عِنْدَهُ وَتَصْدِيقَ مَوْعُودِهِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: حَدَّثَنِي أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا صَفْوَانُ المؤذِنَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْوَلِيدُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا مُعَاوِيَةَ بْنِ سَلَّامٍ، عَنْ أَخِيهِ زَيْدِ بْنِ سَلَّامٍ، عَنْ جَدِّهِ أَبِي سَلَّامٍ الْأَسْوَدِ، حَدَّثَنِي أَبُو معَاتق الْأَشْعَرِيُّ، أَنَّ أَبَا مَالِكٍ الْأَشْعَرِيَّ حَدَّثَهُ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ حَدَّثَهُ: أَنَّ فِي الْجَنَّةِ غُرَفا يُرى ظَاهِرُهَا مِنْ بَاطِنِهَا، وَبَاطِنُهَا مِنْ ظَاهِرِهَا، أعدَّها اللَّهُ لِمَنْ أَطْعَمَ الطَّعَامَ، وَأَطَابَ الْكَلَامَ، وَأَبَاحَ الصِّيَامَ، وَأَقَامَ الصَّلَاةَ وَالنَّاسُ نِيَامٌ .

[وَقَوْلُهُ] : ﴿وَعَلَى رَبِّهِمْ يَتَوَكَّلُونَ﴾ ، فِي أَحْوَالِهِمْ كُلِّهَا، فِي دِينِهِمْ وَدُنْيَاهُمْ.

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَهُمْ تَعَالَى أَنَّ الرِّزْقَ لَا يُخْتَصُّ بِبُقْعَةٍ، بَلْ رِزْقُهُ تَعَالَى عَامٌّ لِخَلْقِهِ حَيْثُ كَانُوا وَأَيْنَ كَانُوا، بَلْ كَانَتْ أَرْزَاقُ الْمُهَاجِرِينَ حَيْثُ هَاجَرُوا أَكْثَرَ وَأَوْسَعَ وَأَطْيَبَ، فَإِنَّهُمْ بَعْدَ قَلِيلٍ صَارُوا حُكَّامَ الْبِلَادِ فِي سَائِرِ الْأَقْطَارِ وَالْأَمْصَارِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَكَأَيِّنْ مِنْ دَابَّةٍ لَا تَحْمِلُ رِزْقَهَا﴾ أَيْ: لَا تُطِيقُ جَمْعَهُ وَتَحْصِيلَهُ وَلَا تُؤَخِّرُ شَيْئًا لِغَدٍ، ﴿اللَّهُ يَرْزُقُهَا وَإِيَّاكُمْ﴾ أَيِ: اللَّهُ يُقَيِّضُ لَهَا رِزْقَهَا عَلَى ضَعْفِهَا، وَيُيَسِّرُهُ عَلَيْهَا، فَيَبْعَثُ إِلَى كُلِّ مَخْلُوقٍ مِنَ الرِّزْقِ مَا يُصْلِحُهُ، حَتَّى الذَّرِّ فِي قَرَارِ الْأَرْضِ، وَالطَّيْرِ فِي الْهَوَاءِ وَالْحِيتَانِ فِي الْمَاءِ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا مِنْ دَابَّةٍ فِي الأرْضِ إِلا عَلَى اللَّهِ رِزْقُهَا وَيَعْلَمُ مُسْتَقَرَّهَا وَمُسْتَوْدَعَهَا كُلٌّ فِي كِتَابٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ [هُودٍ: ٦] .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ الْهَرَوِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ -يَعْنِي ابْنَ هَارُونَ -حَدَّثَنَا الْجَرَّاحُ بْنُ مِنْهَال الْجَزَرِيُّ -هُوَ أَبُو الْعَطُوفِ -عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ رَجُلٍ ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ قَالَ: خَرَجْتُ مَعَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ حَتَّى دَخَلَ بَعْضَ حِيطَانِ الْمَدِينَةِ، فَجَعَلَ يَلْتَقِطُ مِنَ التَّمْرِ ويأكل، فقال لي: "يا بن عُمَرَ، مَا لَكَ لَا تَأْكُلُ؟ " قَالَ: قُلْتُ: لَا أَشْتَهِيهِ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، قَالَ: "لَكِنِّي أشتهيه، وَهَذِهِ صُبْحُ رَابِعَةٍ مُنْذُ لَمْ أَذُقْ طَعَامًا وَلَمْ أَجِدْهُ، وَلَوْ شِئْتُ لَدَعَوْتُ رَبِّي فَأَعْطَانِي مِثْلَ مُلْكِ قَيْصَرَ وَكِسْرَى فَكَيْفَ بِكَ يَا بن عُمَرَ إِذَا بَقِيتَ فِي قَوْمٍ يُخَبِّئُونَ رِزْقَ سَنَتِهِمْ بِضَعْفِ الْيَقِينِ؟ ". قَالَ: فَوَاللَّهِ مَا بَرِحْنَا وَلَا رِمْنا حَتَّى نَزَلَتْ: ﴿وَكَأَيِّنْ مِنْ دَابَّةٍ لَا تَحْمِلُ رِزْقَهَا اللَّهُ يَرْزُقُهَا وَإِيَّاكُمْ وَهُوَ السَّمِيعُ الْعَلِيمُ﴾ فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَمْ يَأْمُرْنِي بِكَنْزِ الدُّنْيَا، وَلَا بِاتِّبَاعِ الشَّهَوَاتِ، فَمَنْ كَنَزَ دُنْيَاهُ يُرِيدُ بِهَا حَيَاةً بَاقِيَةً فَإِنَّ الْحَيَاةَ بِيَدِ اللَّهِ، أَلَا وَإِنِّي لَا أَكْنِزُ دِينَارًا وَلَا دِرْهَمًا، وَلَا أُخَبِّئُ رِزْقًا لِغَدٍ " .

وَهَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ، وَأَبُو الْعَطُوفِ الْجَزَرِيُّ ضَعِيفٌ.

وَقَدْ ذَكَرُوا أَنَّ الْغُرَابَ إِذَا فَقسَ عَنْ فِرَاخِهِ البَيض، خَرَجُوا وَهُمْ بيضٌ فَإِذَا رَآهُمْ أَبَوَاهُمْ كَذَلِكَ، نَفَرَا عَنْهُمْ أَيَّامًا حَتَّى يَسْوَدَّ الرِّيشُ، فَيَظَلُّ الْفَرْخُ فَاتِحًا فَاهُ يَتَفَقَّدُ أَبَوَيْهِ، فَيُقَيِّضُ اللَّهُ لَهُ طَيْرًا صِغَارًا كالبَرغَش فَيَغْشَاهُ فَيَتَقَوَّتُ مِنْهُ تِلْكَ الْأَيَّامَ حَتَّى يَسْوَدَّ رِيشُهُ، وَالْأَبَوَانِ يَتَفَقَّدَانِهِ كُلَّ وَقْتٍ، فَكُلَّمَا رَأَوْهُ أَبْيَضَ الرِّيشِ نَفَرَا عَنْهُ، فَإِذَا رَأَوْهُ قَدِ اسْوَدَّ رِيشُهُ عَطَفَا عَلَيْهِ بِالْحَضَانَةِ وَالرِّزْقِ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ الشَّاعِرُ:

يَا رَازِقَ النعَّاب في عُشه ... وجَابر العَظْم الكَسِير الْمَهِيضِ ...

وَقَدْ قَالَ الشَّافِعِيُّ فِي جُمْلَةِ كَلَامٍ لَهُ فِي الْأَوَامِرِ، كَقَوْلِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ "سَافِرُوا تَصِحُّوا وَتُرْزَقُوا".

قَالَ الْبَيْهَقِيُّ أَخْبَرَنَا إِمْلَاءً أَبُو الْحَسَنِ عَلِيُّ بْنُ عَبْدَانَ، أَخْبَرَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عُبَيْدٍ، أَخْبَرَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ غَالِبٍ، حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ سِنان، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ رَدّاد -شَيْخٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْمَدِينَةِ -حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ دِينَارٍ عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "سَافِرُوا تَصِحُّوا وَتَغْنَمُوا". قَالَ: وَرُوِّينَاهُ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا قُتَيْبَةُ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ لَهِيعة، عَنْ دَرّاج، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ حُجَيرة، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "سَافِرُوا تَرْبَحُوا، وَصُومُوا تَصِحُّوا، وَاغْزُوا تَغْنَمُوا" .

وَقَدْ وَرَدَ مِثْلُ حَدِيثِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ مَرْفُوعًا، وَعَنْ مُعَاذِ بن جبل موقوفا . وفي لَفْظٍ: "سَافِرُوا مَعَ ذَوِي الْجُدُودِ وَالْمَيْسَرَةِ" 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَهُوَ السَّمِيعُ الْعَلِيمُ﴾ أَيِ: السَّمِيعُ لِأَقْوَالِ عِبَادِهِ، الْعَلِيمُ بِحَرَكَاتِهِمْ وَسَكَنَاتِهِمْ.

---

## 29:61-63 — verses 61-63 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty is affirming that there is no god but Him, because the polytheists, those who worship others alongside Him, acknowledge that He alone creates the heavens and the earth, the sun and the moon, and subjects the night and day to their courses, and that He is the Creator and the Provider of His servants, the One who determines their lifespans and their varying durations, and their varying provisions, allotting between them differently, so that among them are the rich and the poor. He is the One who knows what is fitting for each of them, and who deserves wealth as against who deserves poverty. So He mentions that He alone controls the creation of all things and is unique in managing their affairs. Since this is the case, why should other than Him be worshipped? Why should reliance be placed upon other than Him? Just as He is One in His dominion, so let Him be One in the worship due to Him.

The Almighty very often establishes the station of divinity (uluhiyyah) by means of acknowledgment of the oneness of lordship (rububiyyah). The polytheists used to acknowledge this, just as they used to say in their talbiyah (pilgrimage invocation): "Here I am, at Your service, You have no partner, except a partner who is Yours, You possess him and whatever he possesses."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُقَرِّرًا أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ؛ لِأَنَّ الْمُشْرِكِينَ -الَّذِينَ يَعْبُدُونَ مَعَهُ غَيْرَهُ -مُعْتَرِفُونَ أَنَّهُ الْمُسْتَقِلُّ بِخَلْقِ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ وَالشَّمْسِ وَالْقَمَرِ، وَتَسْخِيرِ اللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ، وَأَنَّهُ الْخَالِقُ الرَّازِقُ لِعِبَادِهِ، وَمُقَدِّرٌ آجَالَهُمْ، وَاخْتِلَافَهَا وَاخْتِلَافَ أَرْزَاقِهِمْ فَفَاوَتَ بَيْنَهُمْ، فَمِنْهُمُ الْغَنِيُّ وَالْفَقِيرُ، وَهُوَ الْعَلِيمُ بِمَا يُصْلِحُ كُلا مِنْهُمْ، ومَنْ يَسْتَحِقُّ الْغِنَى مِمَّنْ يَسْتَحِقُّ الْفَقْرَ، فَذَكَرَ أَنَّهُ المستبدُّ بِخَلْقِ الْأَشْيَاءِ الْمُتَفَرِّدِ بِتَدْبِيرِهَا، فَإِذَا كَانَ الْأَمْرُ كَذَلِكَ فَلِمَ يُعبد غَيْرُهُ؟ وَلِمَ يُتَوَكَّلُ عَلَى غَيْرِهِ؟ فَكَمَا أَنَّهُ الْوَاحِدُ فِي مُلْكِهِ فَلْيَكُنِ الْوَاحِدَ فِي عِبَادَتِهِ، وَكَثِيرًا مَا يُقَرِّرُ تَعَالَى مَقَامَ الْإِلَهِيَّةِ بِالِاعْتِرَافِ بِتَوْحِيدِ الرُّبُوبِيَّةِ. وَقَدْ كَانَ الْمُشْرِكُونَ يَعْتَرِفُونَ بِذَلِكَ، كَمَا كَانُوا يَقُولُونَ فِي تَلْبِيَتِهِمْ: "لَبَّيْكَ لَا شَرِيكَ لَكَ، إِلَّا شَرِيكًا هُوَ لَكَ، تَمْلِكُهُ وَمَا مَلَكَ".

---

## 29:64-66 — verses 64-66 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing about the paltriness of this world, its passing away and its coming to an end, that it has no permanence, and that the utmost that is in it is diversion and play: {And indeed, the abode of the Hereafter, that is truly the life} that is, the everlasting, true life which has neither passing away nor ending, rather it continues forever and ever.

His saying: {If only they knew} means, they would have preferred what remains over what perishes.

Then the Almighty informs about the polytheists, that at the time of dire need they call upon Him alone, without any partner, so why is it that this is not so from them at all times? {So when they embark on a ship, they call upon Allah, sincere to Him in religion} as in His saying: {And when affliction touches you at sea, lost are those you call upon except Him. But when He delivers you to the land, you turn away} [al-Isra: 67]. And He says here: {But when He delivers them to the land, at once they associate partners with Him}.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq has mentioned, from Ikrimah ibn Abi Jahl, that when the Messenger of Allah ﷺ conquered Mecca, he fled from it. When he boarded a ship to go to Abyssinia, the ship shook violently with them, and its crew said, "O people, be sincere in your supplication to your Lord, for nothing can save you here except Him." Ikrimah said, "By Allah, if nothing can save at sea except Him, then nothing else can save on land either. O Allah, I make a covenant with You: if I get out of this, I will surely go and place my hand in the hand of Muhammad, and I will surely find him gentle and merciful." And so it was.

His saying: {That they may disbelieve in what We have given them and that they may enjoy themselves} this lam (the particle "li") is called by many scholars of Arabic grammar, tafsir, and the principles of jurisprudence "the lam of consequence," because they themselves did not intend that outcome. There is no doubt that this is the case with respect to them. But with respect to Allah's decree over them and His having prepared them for that, it is "the lam of causation." We have already established this point in explaining His saying: {That he might become to them an enemy and a source of grief} [al-Qasas: 8].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ حَقَارَةِ الدُّنْيَا وَزَوَالِهَا وَانْقِضَائِهَا، وَأَنَّهَا لَا دَوَامَ لَهَا، وَغَايَةُ مَا فِيهَا لَهْوٌ وَلَعِبٌ: ﴿وَإِنَّ الدَّارَ الآخِرَةَ لَهِيَ الْحَيَوَانُ﴾ أَيْ: الْحَيَاةُ الدَّائِمَةُ الْحَقُّ الَّذِي لَا زَوَالَ لَهَا وَلَا انْقِضَاءَ، بَلْ هِيَ مُسْتَمِرَّةٌ أَبَدَ الْآبَادِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَوْ كَانُوا يَعْلَمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَآثَرُوا مَا يَبْقَى عَلَى مَا يَفْنَى.

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى عَنِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ أَنَّهُمْ عِنْدَ الِاضْطِرَارِ يَدْعُونَهُ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، فَهَلَّا يَكُونُ هَذَا مِنْهُمْ دَائِمًا، ﴿فَإِذَا رَكِبُوا فِي الْفُلْكِ دَعَوُا اللَّهَ مُخْلِصِينَ لَهُ الدِّينَ﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ ﴿وَإِذَا مَسَّكُمُ الضُّرُّ فِي الْبَحْرِ ضَلَّ مَنْ تَدْعُونَ إِلا إِيَّاهُ فَلَمَّا نَجَّاكُمْ إِلَى الْبَرِّ أَعْرَضْتُمْ﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ::٦٧] . وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿فَلَمَّا نَجَّاهُمْ إِلَى الْبَرِّ إِذَا هُمْ يُشْرِكُونَ﴾ .

وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ بْنِ أَبِي جَهْلٍ: أَنَّهُ لَمَّا فَتَحَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ مَكَّةَ ذَهَبَ فَارًّا مِنْهَا، فَلَمَّا رَكِبَ فِي الْبَحْرِ لِيَذْهَبَ إِلَى الْحَبَشَةِ، اضْطَرَبَتْ بِهِمُ السَّفِينَةُ، فَقَالَ أَهْلُهَا: يَا قَوْمِ، أَخْلِصُوا لِرَبِّكُمُ الدُّعَاءَ، فَإِنَّهُ لَا يُنْجِي هَاهُنَا إِلَّا هُوَ. فَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: وَاللَّهِ إِنْ كَانَ لَا يُنْجِي فِي الْبَحْرِ غَيْرُهُ، فَإِنَّهُ لَا يُنَجّي غَيْرُهُ فِي الْبَرِّ أَيْضًا، اللَّهُمَّ لَكَ عليَّ عَهْدٌ لَئِنْ خرجتُ لَأَذْهَبْنَ فلأضعَنّ يَدِي فِي يَدِ مُحَمَّدٍ فلأجدنه رؤوفًا رَحِيمًا، وَكَانَ كَذَلِكَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لِيَكْفُرُوا بِمَا آتَيْنَاهُمْ وَلِيَتَمَتَّعُوا﴾ : هَذِهِ اللَّامُ يُسَمِّيهَا كَثِيرٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْعَرَبِيَّةِ وَالتَّفْسِيرِ وَعُلَمَاءِ الْأُصُولِ لَامَ الْعَاقِبَةِ؛ لِأَنَّهُمْ لَا يَقْصِدُونَ ذَلِكَ، وَلَا شَكَّ أَنَّهَا كَذَلِكَ بِالنِّسْبَةِ إِلَيْهِمْ، وَأَمَّا بِالنِّسْبَةِ إِلَى تَقْدِيرِ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِمْ ذَلِكَ وَتَقْيِيضِهِ إِيَّاهُمْ لِذَلِكَ فَهِيَ لَامُ التَّعْلِيلِ. وَقَدْ قدَّمْنا تَقْرِيرَ ذَلِكَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿لِيَكُونَ لَهُمْ عَدُوًّا وَحَزَنًا﴾ [الْقَصَصِ: ٨] .

---

## 29:67-69 — verses 67-69 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, reminding the Quraysh of His favor upon them in what He made permissible for them of His sacred precinct, which He made equal for all people, both the resident there and the visitor, and whoever entered it was safe. So they were in great security, while the bedouin Arabs around them plundered one another and killed one another, as the Almighty said: {For the accustomed security of Quraysh, their accustomed security in the winter and summer journey. So let them worship the Lord of this House, who has fed them against hunger and made them safe from fear} [Quraysh: 1-4].

His saying: {Do they then believe in falsehood and disbelieve in the favor of Allah?} means: was their gratitude for this great favor to associate partners with Him, and to worship besides Him other idols and rivals, and {they exchanged the favor of Allah for disbelief and led their people to the abode of ruin} [Ibrahim: 28], and they disbelieved in the Prophet of Allah, His servant and Messenger? What would have befitted them was to devote worship sincerely to Allah, not to associate partners with Him, and to affirm the truth of the Messenger, honoring and revering him. Instead they denied him, fought him, and drove him out from among them. For this reason Allah stripped them of what He had bestowed upon them as favor, and those of them who were killed were killed at Badr, and dominion passed to Allah, His Messenger, and the believers. So Allah granted His Messenger the conquest of Mecca, humbled their noses, and abased their necks.

Then the Almighty says: {And who does greater wrong than one who invents a lie against Allah or denies the truth when it comes to him?} meaning: no one receives a more severe punishment than one who lies about Allah, saying that Allah revealed something to him when nothing was revealed to him, or one who says, "I will reveal something like what Allah has revealed." Likewise, no one receives a more severe punishment than one who denies the truth when it comes to him. The first is a fabricator, and the second is a denier. For this reason He said: {Is there not in Hell a dwelling place for the disbelievers?}

Then He says: {And those who strive for Us}, meaning the Messenger ﷺ, and his Companions and followers until the Day of Judgment, {We will surely guide them to Our ways}, meaning: We will surely enable them to perceive Our ways, that is, Our paths in this world and the Hereafter.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Abbas al-Hamdani, Abu Ahmad, from the people of Acre, regarding the saying of Allah: {And those who strive for Us, We will surely guide them to Our ways, and indeed Allah is with the doers of good} said: those who act upon what they know, He guides them to what they do not know. Ahmad ibn Abi al-Hawari said: I related this to Abu Sulayman al-Darani and it pleased him, and he said: it is not fitting for one who is inspired with something good to act upon it until he hears it confirmed in the transmitted reports (al-athar). When he hears it in the reports, he acts upon it and praises Allah when it agrees with what was in his own soul.

As for His saying: {And indeed Allah is with the doers of good}, Ibn Abi Hatim said:

[chain] al-Sha'bi said: Isa ibn Maryam (peace be upon him) said: doing good (al-ihsan) is only that you do good to one who has wronged you. It is not doing good that you do good to one who has done good to you. [And in the hadith of Jibril, when he asked the Messenger of Allah ﷺ about ihsan, he said: "Tell me about ihsan." He said: "That you worship Allah as though you see Him, and if you do not see Him, then indeed He sees you."]

[Here ends the tafsir of Surat al-Ankabut. To Allah belongs all praise and grace.]

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُمْتَنًّا عَلَى قُرَيْشٍ فِيمَا أَحَلَّهُمْ مِنْ حَرَمِهِ، الَّذِي جَعَلَهُ لِلنَّاسِ سَوَاءً الْعَاكِفُ فِيهِ وَالْبَادِي، وَمَنْ دَخَلَهُ كَانَ آمِنًا، فَهُمْ فِي أَمْنٍ عَظِيمٍ، وَالْأَعْرَابُ حَوْلَهُ يَنْهَبُ بَعْضُهُمْ بَعْضًا وَيَقْتُلُ بَعْضُهُمْ بَعْضًا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لإيلافِ قُرَيْشٍ إِيلافِهِمْ رِحْلَةَ الشِّتَاءِ وَالصَّيْفِ. فَلْيَعْبُدُوا رَبَّ هَذَا الْبَيْتِ. الَّذِي أَطْعَمَهُمْ مِنْ جُوعٍ وَآمَنَهُمْ مِنْ خَوْفٍ﴾ [قُرَيْشٍ: ١-٤] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَفَبِالْبَاطِلِ يُؤْمِنُونَ وَبِنِعْمَةِ اللَّهِ يَكْفُرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: أَفَكَانَ شُكْرُهُمْ عَلَى هَذِهِ النِّعْمَةِ الْعَظِيمَةِ أَنْ أَشْرَكُوا بِهِ، وَعَبَدُوا مَعَهُ [غَيْرَهُ مِنَ] الْأَصْنَامِ وَالْأَنْدَادِ، وَ ﴿بَدَّلُوا نِعْمَةَ اللَّهِ كُفْرًا وَأَحَلُّوا قَوْمَهُمْ دَارَ الْبَوَارِ﴾ [إِبْرَاهِيمَ: ٢٨] ، وَكَفَرُوا بِنَبِيِّ اللَّهِ وَعَبْدِهِ وَرَسُولِهِ، فَكَانَ اللَّائِقُ بِهِمْ إِخْلَاصَ الْعِبَادَةِ لِلَّهِ، وَأَلَّا يُشْرِكُوا بِهِ، وَتَصْدِيقَ الرَّسُولِ وَتَعْظِيمَهُ وَتَوْقِيرَهُ، فَكَذَّبُوهُ وَقَاتَلُوهُ وَأَخْرَجُوهُ مِنْ بَيْنِ ظَهْرِهِمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا سَلَبَهُمُ اللَّهُ مَا كَانَ أَنْعَمَ بِهِ عَلَيْهِمْ، وَقُتِلَ مَنْ قُتِلَ مِنْهُمْ بِبَدْرٍ، وَصَارَتِ الدَّوْلَةُ لِلَّهِ وَلِرَسُولِهِ وَلِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ، فَفَتَحَ اللَّهُ عَلَى رَسُولِهِ مَكَّةَ، وَأَرْغَمَ آنَافَهُمْ وَأَذَلَّ رِقَابَهُمْ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَنْ أَظْلَمُ مِمَّنِ افْتَرَى عَلَى اللَّهِ كَذِبًا أَوْ كَذَّبَ بِالْحَقِّ لَمَّا جَاءَهُ﴾ أي: لا أحد أشد عُقُوبَةً مِمَّنْ كَذَبَ عَلَى اللَّهِ فَقَالَ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ أَوْحَى إِلَيْهِ شَيْءٌ، وَلَمْ يُوحَ إِلَيْهِ شَيْءٌ. وَمَنْ قَالَ: سَأُنْزِلُ مِثْلَ مَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ. وَهَكَذَا لَا أَحَدَ أَشَدُّ عُقُوبَةً مِمَّنْ كَذَّبَ بِالْحَقِّ لَمَّا جَاءَهُ، فَالْأَوَّلُ مُفْتَرٍ، وَالثَّانِي مُكَذِّبٌ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿أَلَيْسَ فِي جَهَنَّمَ مَثْوًى لِلْكَافِرِينَ﴾ .

ثُمَّ قَالَ ﴿وَالَّذِينَ جَاهَدُوا فِينَا﴾ يَعْنِي: الرَّسُولَ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، وَأَصْحَابَهُ وَأَتْبَاعَهُ إِلَى يَوْمِ الدِّينِ ﴿لَنَهْدِيَنَّهُمْ سُبُلَنَا﴾ ، أَيْ: لنُبَصرنهم سُبُلَنَا، أَيْ: طُرُقَنَا فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ أَبِي الحَواري، حَدَّثَنَا عَبَّاسٌ الْهَمْدَانِيُّ أَبُو أَحْمَدَ -مِنْ أَهْلِ عَكَّا -فِي قَوْلِ اللَّهِ : ﴿وَالَّذِينَ جَاهَدُوا فِينَا لَنَهْدِيَنَّهُمْ سُبُلَنَا وَإِنَّ اللَّهَ لَمَعَ الْمُحْسِنِينَ﴾ قَالَ: الَّذِينَ يَعْمَلُونَ بِمَا يَعْلَمُونَ، يَهْدِيهِمْ لِمَا لَا يَعْلَمُونَ. قَالَ أَحْمَدُ بْنُ أَبِي الْحَوَارِيِّ: فَحَدَّثْتُ بِهِ أَبَا سُلَيْمَانَ الدَّارَانِيَّ فَأَعْجَبَهُ، وَقَالَ: لَيْسَ يَنْبَغِي لِمَنْ أُلْهِمَ شَيْئًا مِنَ الْخَيْرِ أَنْ يَعْمَلَ بِهِ حَتَّى يَسْمَعَهُ فِي الْأَثَرِ، فَإِذَا سَمِعَهُ فِي الْأَثَرِ عَمِلَ بِهِ، وَحَمِدَ اللَّهَ حِينَ وَافَقَ مَا فِي نَفْسِهِ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنَّ اللَّهَ لَمَعَ الْمُحْسِنِينَ﴾ ، قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ:

حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا عِيسَى بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ -قَاضِي الرَّيِّ -حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو جَعْفَرٍ الرَّازِيُّ، عَنِ الْمُغِيرَةِ، عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ قَالَ: قَالَ عيسى بن مَرْيَمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ: إِنَّمَا الْإِحْسَانُ أَنْ تُحْسِنَ إِلَى مَنْ أَسَاءَ إِلَيْكَ، لَيْسَ الْإِحْسَانُ أَنْ تُحْسِنَ إِلَى مَنْ أَحْسَنَ إِلَيْكَ. [وَفِي حَدِيثِ جِبْرِيلَ لَمَّا سَأَلَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَنِ الْإِحْسَانِ قَالَ: "أَخْبِرْنِي عَنِ الْإِحْسَانِ". قَالَ: "أَنْ تَعْبُدَ اللَّهَ كَأَنَّكَ تَرَاهُ، فَإِنْ لَمْ تَكُنْ تَرَاهُ فَإِنَّهُ يَرَاكَ".

[انْتَهَى تفسير سورة العنكبوت، ولله الحمد والمنة ]

---
